# Skyrim:Apocrypha (Filament and Filigree)

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Black Book: Filament and Filigree | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 25 |
| Occupants | |
| [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"), [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| [Black Soul Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem")  [Spell Tome: Healing Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Healing_Hands "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Healing Hands")  *[Three Thieves](/wiki/Skyrim:Three_Thieves "Skyrim:Three Thieves")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2POIBookLevel03 | |
| Location | |
| [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") | |

The Filament and Filigree Black Book in Kolbjorn Barrow

**Filament and Filigree** is an area of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora")'s [plane of Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Planes_of_Oblivion "Lore:Planes of Oblivion"), [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha"). There is only one zone in the area, *[Filament and Filigree](#Filament_and_Filigree)*.

The [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (book)") needed to access Filament and Filigree is found inside [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow"). You must complete the quest [Unearthed](/wiki/Skyrim:Unearthed "Skyrim:Unearthed") in order to retrieve the book.

The realm is inhabited by Daedra called [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") and [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"). Tentacles constantly breach the acidic dark waters and sometimes whip at you, causing a significant amount of damage if they manage to hit you. The acidic waters with the tentacles are also corrosive and cause damage if stepped in.

## Related Quests

- **[Black Book: Filament and Filigree](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (book)")'s hidden knowledge.

## Filament and Filigree

Filament and Filigree opens on a dim platform facing a dark corridor. The [darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Darkness "Skyrim:Traps") here is dangerous, literally; entering it will inflict continuous heavy damage which can not be resisted by any means, including the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout. Floating [Wisp-Lanterns](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp-Lantern "Skyrim:Wisp-Lantern") drift above the platforms, providing safe havens of light to walk in. Other forms of light will also work to prevent damage (e.g. torches, [Candlelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlelight "Skyrim:Candlelight"), [Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Magelight "Skyrim:Magelight")), so long as they keep away the darkness.

Ahead and to the right is a table and a font of magicka. On the table are two random soul gems and a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Three Thieves](/wiki/Skyrim:Three_Thieves "Skyrim:Three Thieves")*. Hidden behind the left statue at the bottom of the stairs to the left is a pod. At the top of the stairs is a closed gate. The scrye to open the gate is to the right, and to the left is a pod and a [scroll of invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Invisibility "Skyrim:Scroll of Invisibility"). An eye floats along to the right of the long platform ahead, but does not provide full protection from the darkness. Along the platform are two seekers and a lurker, and a lurker rises from the pool at the top of the stairs at the other end. At the top of stairs at the end of the platform is the black book *Filament and Filigree*, a vessel to the left, and a table to the right with copies of the [Spell Tome: Healing Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Healing_Hands "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Healing Hands") and the [Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Seeker "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker") (only if your [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill is at least level 40), a [scroll of mass paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis"), and three soul gems (one [black](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem") and two random). To exit this part of Apocrypha, use the non-circular part of the black book.

The three [Powers](/wiki/Skyrim:Powers "Skyrim:Powers") offered by this book are:

- [Secret of Arcana](/wiki/Skyrim:Secret_of_Arcana "Skyrim:Secret of Arcana") — Spells cost no magicka for 30 seconds.
- [Secret of Protection](/wiki/Skyrim:Secret_of_Protection "Skyrim:Secret of Protection") — You take half damage for 30 seconds.
- [Secret of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Secret_of_Strength "Skyrim:Secret of Strength") — Power attacks cost no stamina for 30 seconds.

# Skyrim:Apocrypha (The Hidden Twilight)

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Black Book: The Hidden Twilight | | |
| # of Zones | 8 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 25 |
| Occupants | |
| [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"), [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[2920, Hearth Fire, v9](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Hearth_Fire,_v9 "Skyrim:2920, Hearth Fire, v9")* *[A Hypothetical Treachery](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Hypothetical_Treachery "Skyrim:A Hypothetical Treachery")* *[Before the Ages of Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Ages_of_Man "Skyrim:Before the Ages of Man")* [Black Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem") *[Breathing Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Breathing_Water "Skyrim:Breathing Water")* *[Racial Phylogeny](/wiki/Skyrim:Racial_Phylogeny "Skyrim:Racial Phylogeny")* [Spell Tome: Conjure Ash Spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Ash Spawn") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2Book07Dungeon | |
| Location | |
| [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") | |

The Hidden Twilight Black Book in Tel Mithryn

**The Hidden Twilight** is an area of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora")'s [plane of Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Planes_of_Oblivion "Lore:Planes of Oblivion"), [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha"). There are eight zones (or chapters) in the area: *[Chapter I](#Chapter_I)*, *[Chapter II](#Chapter_II)*, *[Chapter III](#Chapter_III)*, *[Chapter IV](#Chapter_IV)*, *[Chapter V](#Chapter_V)*, *[Chapter VI](#Chapter_VI)*, *[Chapter VII](#Chapter_VII)*, and *[Chapter VIII](#Chapter_VIII)*.

The [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (book)") needed to access The Hidden Twilight is found inside [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)"). You must complete the quest [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") in order to retrieve the book.

The realm is inhabited by Daedra called [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") and [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"). Tentacles constantly breach the acidic dark waters and sometimes whip at you, causing a significant amount of damage if they manage to hit you. The acidic waters with the tentacles are also corrosive and cause damage if stepped in.

## Related Quests

- **[Black Book: The Hidden Twilight](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (book)")'s hidden knowledge.

### Chapter I

Chapter I opens in a dim room. On a raised central platform are two fonts of magicka. To the north ahead is a scrye that opens the gate next to another font of magicka behind the scrye. Beyond the gate is a room with a pod under an elevated central platform with two fonts of stamina and the book to Chapter II.

Outside and northeast of the gate is a gap in the walls allowing access to the main open area. Across the water to the east is the island comprising Chapter VII. It is possible to reach the island by using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") or by swimming using the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout and/or healing potions. From this island you can access Chapter VI and proceed to the end of the book. However, proceeding in this way glitches Chapters II through V, preventing access to the five [skill books](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") in Chapter V.

### Chapter II

Chapter II starts in a corridor, with a font of magicka behind the starting point. The corridor leads past four more fonts of magicka to a large room guarded by two seekers with two fonts of stamina, a font of magicka, and a table with a random soul gem. A ramp near the southeast corner ascends to the north to a font of magicka and a scrye that causes two bridges to rise and fall on either side of the platforms ahead to the east. If you fall from the bridges, you will land on the lower platform, where a scrye to the west opens a gate to the previous room.

At the far end of the second bridge is a junction. At the end of the corridor descending to the left is a room containing a font of magicka, a pod, and a table with two soul gems (one [grand](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Grand Soul Gem") and one random) and the [Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Seeker "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker") (only if your [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill is at least level 40). At the end of the corridor descending to the right is a font of magicka and the book to Chapter III.

### Chapter III

Chapter III starts in a small room with a pillar in the middle, with a font of magicka behind the starting point. On the far side of the pillar is a font of stamina and an alcove with a pod. To the southwest is a large room with two fonts of magicka and a currently inaccessible raised platform ahead. A pair of curved ramps ascend to a scrye that extends the stairs to the platform. On the platform is a seeker and two tables and a pedestal with three soul gems (two random and one leveled).

To the south, two fonts of magicka flank the gateway to a room guarded by a lurker. In the middle of the room is a font of stamina and a short set of stairs up to a closed gate. To the south is another short set of stairs up to a font of magicka and a ramp ascending to a scrye that opens the gate. To the southeast is a short corridor leading to a font of magicka and the book to Chapter IV.

Beyond the gate is a font of stamina and another short set of stairs ascending to the southeast. At the top of the stairs is another short set of stairs up to a font of magicka and another closed gate. To the southwest is a short set of stairs up to a font of stamina and a ramp ascending to a scrye that opens the gate. Beyond the gate is a font of stamina and a small network of corridors guarded by a seeker. The corridors lead east to a pod in what appears to be a dead end, but approaching the pod causes the corridor to extend to reveal the books to Chapters V and VI.

### Chapter IV

Chapter IV consists of a small room with a seeker, a font of magicka, and a scrye that opens a gate in Chapter V.

### Chapter V

Chapter V starts in a small room with a font of magicka and a scrye that opens the gate behind the scrye. Beyond the gate is another gate opened by the scrye in Chapter IV. Beyond the second gate is a small room guarded by a seeker with a pod and a table with copies of five skill books for five of the "[magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Overview "Skyrim:Magic Overview")" skills: *[2920, Hearth Fire, v9](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Hearth_Fire,_v9 "Skyrim:2920, Hearth Fire, v9")* ([Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration")), *[A Hypothetical Treachery](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Hypothetical_Treachery "Skyrim:A Hypothetical Treachery")* ([Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")), *[Before the Ages of Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Ages_of_Man "Skyrim:Before the Ages of Man")* ([Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion")), *[Breathing Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Breathing_Water "Skyrim:Breathing Water")* ([Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration")), and *[Racial Phylogeny](/wiki/Skyrim:Racial_Phylogeny "Skyrim:Racial Phylogeny")* ([Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration")).

### Chapter VI

Chapter VI starts in a corridor, with a font of magicka behind the starting point. The corridor leads to a font of stamina and the books to Chapters VII and VIII.

### Chapter VII

Chapter VII consists of an island with a seeker, a font of magicka, a pedestal with two random books, and a scrye that raises a bridge in Chapter VIII.

### Chapter VIII

Forbidden knowledge

Chapter VIII starts in a room with a seeker and two pillars, with a font of stamina behind the starting point. Behind the pillar to the left is a table with two soul gems (one [black](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem") and one [grand](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Grand Soul Gem")). To the west is a bridge raised by the scrye in Chapter VII. At the far end of the bridge is an area with two fonts of stamina, two pools from which two lurkers rise, and a scrye that opens the gate behind the scrye. Beyond the gate is another bridge ascending to the final platform. On the platform is a vessel, two tables with four soul gems (two black and two grand), a copy of the [Spell Tome: Conjure Ash Spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Ash Spawn"), a [scroll of ebonyflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Ebonyflesh "Skyrim:Scroll of Ebonyflesh"), a [scroll of grand healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Grand_Healing "Skyrim:Scroll of Grand Healing"), and a [scroll of paralyze](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Paralyze "Skyrim:Scroll of Paralyze"), and the black book *The Hidden Twilight*. To exit this part of Apocrypha, use the non-circular part of the black book.

The three [Powers](/wiki/Skyrim:Powers "Skyrim:Powers") offered by this book are:

- [Mora's Agony](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora%27s_Agony "Skyrim:Mora's Agony") — Summons a field of writhing tentacles that lasts 30 seconds and poisons foes who enter it.
- [Mora's Boon](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora%27s_Boon "Skyrim:Mora's Boon") — Fully restores your Health, Magicka, and Stamina.
- [Mora's Grasp](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora%27s_Grasp "Skyrim:Mora's Grasp") — Targets are frozen between Oblivion and Tamriel for 30 seconds, and immune to all damage.

# Skyrim:Apocrypha (The Sallow Regent)

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |

| Location | |
| [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") | |

The Sallow Regent Black Book in White Ridge Barrow

**The Sallow Regent** is an area of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora")'s [plane of Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Planes_of_Oblivion "Lore:Planes of Oblivion"), [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha"). There is only one zone in the area, *[The Sallow Regent](#The_Sallow_Regent)*.

The [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (book)") needed to access The Sallow Regent is found inside [White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow").

The realm is inhabited by Daedra called [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") and [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"). Tentacles constantly breach the acidic dark waters and sometimes whip at you, causing a significant amount of damage if they manage to hit you. The acidic waters with the tentacles are also corrosive and cause damage if stepped in.

## Related Quests

- **[Black Book: The Sallow Regent](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (book)")'s hidden knowledge.

## The Sallow Regent

The Sallow Regent opens in a dim chamber facing a dark corridor. The [darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Darkness "Skyrim:Traps") here is dangerous, literally; entering it will inflict continuous heavy damage which can not be resisted by any means, including the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout. Floating [Wisp-Lanterns](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp-Lantern "Skyrim:Wisp-Lantern") drift above the corridors and chambers, providing safe havens of light to walk in. Other forms of light work as well (e.g. torches, [Candlelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlelight "Skyrim:Candlelight"), [Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Magelight "Skyrim:Magelight")), so long as they keep away the darkness.

To the right of the starting point is a pod. A corridor to the south leads to a room with a pod to the left. The next corridor ascends to a larger room guarded by two seekers. A pod is to the left, and in the darkness straight ahead are two pedestals and a stack of unusable books with a [scroll of conjure flame atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Flame Atronach"), a random soul gem, and copies of the [Spell Tome: Detect Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Detect_Undead "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Detect Undead") and the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Second Seed, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Second_Seed,_v5 "Skyrim:2920, Second Seed, v5")*. Behind the pedestals is another pod. Through the darkness to the south is a table with three soul gems (one [black](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem"), one [grand](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Grand Soul Gem"), and one random) and a copy of the [Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Seeker "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker") (only if your [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill is at least level 40). The exit is to the southeast, with a pod to the left of the exit.

At the top of the corridor is a series of platforms twisting upwards, with a lurker on the platforms to the right. Beyond the lurker is a gap, but a bridge will automatically raise. Beyond the bridge is a table with a grand soul gem, a [scroll of dead thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Scroll of Dead Thrall"), and a copy of the [Spell Tome: Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Fast Healing"). The path continues to another bridge followed by another lurker, then splits around two pillars before again merging and leading to a set of stairs.

At the top of the stairs is the black book *The Sallow Regent*, a vessel to the left, and two tables with a [scroll of conjure storm atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), a [Spell Tome: Flame Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Flame_Thrall "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Flame Thrall"), and four soul gems (two [black](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem"), one [common](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem"), and one leveled). To exit this part of Apocrypha, use the non-circular part of the black book.

The three [Abilities](/wiki/Skyrim:Abilities "Skyrim:Abilities") offered by this book are:

- [Seeker of Might](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker_of_Might "Skyrim:Seeker of Might") — Combat skills are all 10% more effective.
- [Seeker of Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker_of_Shadows "Skyrim:Seeker of Shadows") — Stealth skills are all 10% more effective.
- [Seeker of Sorcery](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker_of_Sorcery "Skyrim:Seeker of Sorcery") — All spells cost 10% less magicka. Enchantments are 10% more powerful.

## Notes

- If you clear The Sallow Regent then return after it has respawned, the two bridges that extended at your approach during your first visit will have retracted, cutting off your path. If you stand at the edge, you can cross the gap with a single word of [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint"). Once you are on the other side, move away and approach the end of the bridge again to cause it to uncurl and extend.

# Skyrim:Apocrypha (The Winds of Change)

## Overview

The Winds of Change Black Book in Raven Rock Mine

**The Winds of Change** is an area of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora")'s [plane of Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Planes_of_Oblivion "Lore:Planes of Oblivion"), [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha"). There is only one zone in the area, *[The Winds of Change](#The_Winds_of_Change)*.

The [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (book)") needed to access The Winds of Change is found inside [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine"). You must progress in the quest [The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent") in order to retrieve the book.

The realm is inhabited by Daedra called [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") and [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"). Tentacles constantly breach the acidic dark waters and sometimes whip at you, causing a significant amount of damage if they manage to hit you. The acidic waters with the tentacles are also corrosive and cause damage if stepped in.

## Related Quests

- **[Black Book: The Winds of Change](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (book)")'s hidden knowledge.

## The Winds of Change

The Winds of Change opens on a dim platform, with a bridge over the murky water ahead. Beyond the bridge and up two sets of stairs is a room with five pedestals guarded by a seeker. Starting with the pedestal nearest the stairs and moving clockwise, the pedestals hold a random book and a random soul gem on the first, nothing of interest on the second, two random books on the third, a random book and a copy of the [Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Seeker "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker") (only if your [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill is at least level 40) on the fourth, and a random soul gem on the fifth.

To the east and northeast, two fonts of stamina flank a scrye that opens the nearby gate. Beyond the gate is a table to the left with two soul gems (one random and one leveled), followed by a font of magicka and a pod to the left. Southwest of the pod is a table with a leveled soul gem, a font of stamina, and a scrye that opens another nearby gate. Beyond the gate is a corridor guarded by a seeker. Along the corridor are two fonts of magicka, with another scrye that opens the gate at the end of the corridor.

Beyond the gate is a large room with a central pool from which a lurker rises to attack. East of the pool is a font of magicka next to a ramp that ascends to a small platform with a scrye and two pedestals flanking a table. The pedestal on the left holds two [scrolls of frenzy](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Frenzy "Skyrim:Scroll of Frenzy") and a [black soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem"), the pedestal on the right holds two [scrolls of fear](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fear "Skyrim:Scroll of Fear"), and the table holds two black soul gems and a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Words and Philosophy](/wiki/Skyrim:Words_and_Philosophy "Skyrim:Words and Philosophy")*. The scrye opens the gate on the other side of the room. West of the pool is a font of magicka and another scrye, which extends the stairs up to the gate. Beyond the gate is a vessel and the black book *The Winds of Change*. To exit this part of Apocrypha, use the non-circular part of the black book.

The three [Abilities](/wiki/Skyrim:Abilities "Skyrim:Abilities") offered by this book are:

- [Companion's Insight](/wiki/Skyrim:Companion%27s_Insight "Skyrim:Companion's Insight") — Your attacks, shouts, and destruction spells do no damage to your followers when in combat.
- [Lover's Insight](/wiki/Skyrim:Lover%27s_Insight "Skyrim:Lover's Insight") — Do 10% more damage and get 10% better prices from people of the opposite sex.
- [Scholar's Insight](/wiki/Skyrim:Scholar%27s_Insight "Skyrim:Scholar's Insight") — Reading Skill Books gives you an extra Skill Point.

# Skyrim:Apocrypha (Untold Legends)

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Black Book: Untold Legends | | |
| # of Zones | 5 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 25 |
| Occupants | |
| [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"), [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Advances in Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Advances_in_Lockpicking "Skyrim:Advances in Lockpicking")*  *[Beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_(book) "Skyrim:Beggar (book)")* [Black Soul Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem")  *[The Gold Ribbon of Merit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gold_Ribbon_of_Merit "Skyrim:The Gold Ribbon of Merit")*  *[The Rear Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rear_Guard "Skyrim:The Rear Guard")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2Book03Dungeon | |
| Location | |
| [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") | |

The Untold Legends Black Book in Benkongerike

**Untold Legends** is an area of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora")'s [plane of Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Planes_of_Oblivion "Lore:Planes of Oblivion"), [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha"). There are five zones (or chapters) in the area: *[Chapter I](#Chapter_I)*, *[Chapter II](#Chapter_II)*, *[Chapter III](#Chapter_III)*, *[Chapter IV](#Chapter_IV)*, and *[Chapter V](#Chapter_V)*.

The [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (book)") needed to access Untold Legends is found inside [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike").

The realm is inhabited by Daedra called [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") and [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"). Tentacles constantly breach the acidic dark waters and sometimes whip at you, causing a significant amount of damage if they manage to hit you. The acidic waters with the tentacles are also corrosive and cause damage if stepped in.

## Related Quests

- **[Black Book: Untold Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (book)")'s hidden knowledge.

### Chapter I

Chapter I opens at the top of a corridor. The corridor leads down past three fonts of magicka, three fonts of stamina, and a table with three soul gems (two random and one leveled) to the book to Chapter II.

### Chapter II

Chapter II starts on a platform. There are three fonts of stamina, two fonts of magicka, and a lurker along the way over the platforms to a junction. At the junction, to the right are two fonts of magicka and the book to Chapter III. To the left is a font of magicka and the book to Chapter IV.

### Chapter III

Chapter III consists of a small treasure room guarded by a seeker. On the table is a pod, a random soul gem, and a copy of the [Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Seeker "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker") (only if your [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill is at least level 40).

### Chapter IV

Chapter IV starts on a platform, with a font of stamina to either side of the starting point. The corridor ahead passes a font of magicka and two fonts of stamina on the way to a room with six alcoves, with three on either side. The room is guarded by three seekers, and requires you to activate four scryes to open the next corridor.

The first alcove on the left has an apprentice-locked pod, a font of stamina, and a table with two soul gems (one [black](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem") and one [greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Greater Soul Gem")) and copies of four [skill books](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") for four of the "[stealth](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth "Skyrim:Stealth")" skills: *[Advances in Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Advances_in_Lockpicking "Skyrim:Advances in Lockpicking")* ([Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking")), *[Beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_(book) "Skyrim:Beggar (book)")* ([Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket")), *[The Gold Ribbon of Merit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gold_Ribbon_of_Merit "Skyrim:The Gold Ribbon of Merit")* ([Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery")), and *[The Rear Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rear_Guard "Skyrim:The Rear Guard")* ([Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor")). The second alcove on the left is currently inaccessible, and the third alcove only has a font of stamina.

The three alcoves on the right each contain a font of magicka, and while the first and third alcoves have a pod (the pod in the third alcove has a novice lock), the middle alcove has a scrye outside to open its gate, and one inside to open the gate for the middle alcove on the left side of the room. Inside that alcove is an adept-locked pod and another scrye that opens the central platform, and on the platform are four fonts of magicka and a scrye to open the southern gate to the corridor ahead. Flanking the southern gate are two fonts of magicka, and beyond the gate is a vessel and the book to Chapter V.

### Chapter V

Chapter V starts at the top of a corridor, with a font of magicka behind the starting point. The hallway will move; watch for a lurker. Halfway along the corridor are two fonts of stamina, and at the end of the corridor are two more fonts of stamina and the black book *Untold Legends*. To exit this part of Apocrypha, use the non-circular part of the black book.

The three [Powers](/wiki/Skyrim:Powers "Skyrim:Powers") offered by this book are:

- [Bardic Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Bardic_Knowledge "Skyrim:Bardic Knowledge") — Summons a spectral drum that plays for 300 seconds, improving Stamina Regen for you and nearby allies.
- [Black Market](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Market "Skyrim:Black Market") — Summons a [Dremora merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Merchant "Skyrim:Dremora Merchant") for 15 seconds.
- [Secret Servant](/wiki/Skyrim:Secret_Servant "Skyrim:Secret Servant") — Summons a [Dremora butler](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Butler "Skyrim:Dremora Butler") for 15 seconds to carry your excess items.

# Skyrim:Apocrypha (Waking Dreams)

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Black Book: Waking Dreams | | |
| # of Zones | 6 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 25 |
| Occupants | |
| [Kruziikrel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kruziikrel "Skyrim:Kruziikrel"), [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)"), [Relonikiv](/wiki/Skyrim:Relonikiv "Skyrim:Relonikiv"), [Sahrotaar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahrotaar "Skyrim:Sahrotaar"), [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"), [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") | |

| Location | |
| [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") | |

The summit of Apocrypha

**Waking Dreams** is an area of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora")'s [plane of Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Planes_of_Oblivion "Lore:Planes of Oblivion"), [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha"). There are six zones (or chapters) in the area: *[Chapter I](#Chapter_I)*, *[Chapter II](#Chapter_II)*, *[Chapter III](#Chapter_III)*, *[Chapter IV](#Chapter_IV)*, *[Chapter V](#Chapter_V)*, and *[Chapter VI](#Chapter_VI)*.

The [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Waking_Dreams_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Waking Dreams (book)") needed to access Waking Dreams is found inside the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak"). You must complete the quest [The Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:The Temple of Miraak") in order to retrieve the book.

The realm is inhabited by Daedra called [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") and [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"). Tentacles constantly breach the acidic dark waters and sometimes whip at you, causing a significant amount of damage if they manage to hit you. The acidic waters with the tentacles are also corrosive and cause damage if stepped in.

## Related Quests

- **[The Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:The Temple of Miraak")**: Uncover the source of [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)")'s power in the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak").
- **[At the Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha")**: Confront [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)") at the summit of [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") and defeat him once and for all.

### Chapter I

Miraak at the base of the tower

When you first read the book during the quest [The Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:The Temple of Miraak"), you will be transported to an area at the base of a massive tower near [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)"). After a short monologue, he will instruct his seekers to "send you back where you came from". You will then be expelled from Apocrypha, but the next time you read the book when on Solstheim, you will be free to explore the area.

Chapter I opens in a large open area. A short distance behind the starting point is a table with copies of *[Bone, Part I](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone,_Part_I "Skyrim:Bone, Part I")*, *[Changed Ones](/wiki/Skyrim:Changed_Ones "Skyrim:Changed Ones")*, and *[Thirsk, A Revised History](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk,_A_Revised_History "Skyrim:Thirsk, A Revised History")*. Near the wall to the northwest behind the second pillar is a pod, with another pod by the grate in the wall to the southeast. To the north is a platform with two fonts of magicka and the book to Chapter II.

### Chapter II

Chapter II starts on a platform at the bottom of a huge tower, with two seekers patrolling the area. The path ascends three sets of stairs, with a table to the right on the second landing with a copy of *[The Guardian and the Traitor](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_and_the_Traitor "Skyrim:The Guardian and the Traitor")* and a [scroll of fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fireball "Skyrim:Scroll of Fireball"). At the top of the stairs, to the west on the ledge is a pod, and to the north is a table with a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Heavy Armor Forging](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor_Forging "Skyrim:Heavy Armor Forging")*.

Along the path and across the bridge is a raised platform with *[On Apocrypha: Boneless Limbs](/wiki/Skyrim:On_Apocrypha:_Boneless_Limbs "Skyrim:On Apocrypha: Boneless Limbs")*. Taking this book extends the stairs and opens the gate to the next area. To the north on the ledge on this side of the bridge is a pod. Beyond the gate is a balcony overlooking a sea of tentacles, with a font of magicka and the book to Chapter III.

### Chapter III

Chapter III starts in a corridor. To the right is a room behind a closed gate, and ahead is a room with two seekers and two fonts of magicka. The corridor to the southeast leads to a raised platform, with a pod at the bottom of a set of stairs on the far side. On the platform is another pod next to a table with a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") skill book *[Song of the Alchemists](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_of_the_Alchemists "Skyrim:Song of the Alchemists")*, a [scroll of fast healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Scroll of Fast Healing"), and a [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem"). Opposite the table is *[On Apocrypha: Delving Pincers](/wiki/Skyrim:On_Apocrypha:_Delving_Pincers "Skyrim:On Apocrypha: Delving Pincers")*. Taking this book opens the gate near the start of the chapter. Beyond the gate is a room with a font of magicka and a scrye, which reveals a corridor to the south.

The corridor passes a font of magicka and ascends to a font of stamina and a table with a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill book *[Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Weapon_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Weapon Enchantments")*, copies of *[History of Raven Rock, Vol. II](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock,_Vol._II "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock, Vol. II")* and *[The Poison Song, Book IV](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Poison_Song,_Book_IV "Skyrim:The Poison Song, Book IV")*, a scroll of fast healing, a [scroll of stoneflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Stoneflesh "Skyrim:Scroll of Stoneflesh"), and a [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem").

The path continues to the west to reenter the main section of the tower. To the south is a pod and a scrye, which opens a gate to the northwest to a small room with a vessel. The walkway south across the center of the chamber leads to a pod, a font of magicka, and *[On Apocrypha: Prying Orbs](/wiki/Skyrim:On_Apocrypha:_Prying_Orbs "Skyrim:On Apocrypha: Prying Orbs")*. Taking this book opens a gate to the west. Beyond the gate is a corridor that passes a font of magicka to end at a font of stamina and the book to Chapter IV.

### Chapter IV

| The books in the trove |
| --- |
| *[Antecedants of Dwemer Law](/wiki/Skyrim:Antecedants_of_Dwemer_Law "Skyrim:Antecedants of Dwemer Law") [Biography of Barenziah, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v1 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v1") [Biography of Barenziah, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v3 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v3") [Charwich-Koniinge, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge,_v2 "Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge, v2") [Fragment: On Artaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment:_On_Artaeum "Skyrim:Fragment: On Artaeum") [Life of Uriel Septim VII](/wiki/Skyrim:Life_of_Uriel_Septim_VII "Skyrim:Life of Uriel Septim VII") [Magic from the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_from_the_Sky "Skyrim:Magic from the Sky") [Opusculus Lamae Bal](/wiki/Skyrim:Opusculus_Lamae_Bal "Skyrim:Opusculus Lamae Bal") Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirit_of_the_Daedra "Skyrim:Spirit of the Daedra") [The Hope of the Redoran](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hope_of_the_Redoran "Skyrim:The Hope of the Redoran") [The House of v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v2 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v2") [The Wolf Queen, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v3 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v3") [The Wolf Queen, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v4 [Thirsk, A Revised History](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk,_A_Revised_History "Skyrim:Thirsk, A Revised History") [Walking the World, Vol XI](/wiki/Skyrim:Walking_the_World,_Vol_XI "Skyrim:Walking the World, Vol XI")* |
| \*There are two copies of the following  three books, making a total of 26 books: *The Wolf Queen, v2* *The Wolf Queen, v5* *Walking the World, Vol XI* |

Chapter IV starts on a high platform, with several walkways and platforms below. Two seekers are down the stairs to the right. To the southwest is a font of stamina followed by a pod. Along the east wall near the lowest level is a table with copies of *[Killing - Before You're Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Killing_-_Before_You%27re_Killed "Skyrim:Killing - Before You're Killed")*, *[2920, Sun's Dusk, v11](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Sun%27s_Dusk,_v11 "Skyrim:2920, Sun's Dusk, v11")*, *[The Anticipations](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Anticipations "Skyrim:The Anticipations")*, and *[Horker Attacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Attacks "Skyrim:Horker Attacks")*. The corridor to the next area is to the south.

The corridor continues to a junction and a table with a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). The path branches to the east and south, with fonts of magicka and stamina at the start of the corridor to the east. Both corridors retract when entered, and two seekers appear. After both corridors have retracted, the corridor to the west shifts position to lead to a large room. To the southwest is a raised platform with a pod and a table with a [scroll of muffle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Muffle "Skyrim:Scroll of Muffle"), a [scroll of fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fury "Skyrim:Scroll of Fury"), a [scroll of oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Oakflesh "Skyrim:Scroll of Oakflesh"), and a [scroll of firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Firebolt "Skyrim:Scroll of Firebolt").

On another platform up the stairs from the first is a font of magicka and *[On Apocrypha: Gnashing Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:On_Apocrypha:_Gnashing_Blades "Skyrim:On Apocrypha: Gnashing Blades")*. Taking this book reveals a corridor to the south on the bottom level. The corridor leads to a crossroads. To the left is an empty alcove, to the right is an alcove with two tables, and ahead is what appears to be another alcove with two more tables. However, once you step into this alcove, the corridor extends ahead. A trove of twenty-six books is on three of the tables (see the list to the right), while on the fourth table is a [scroll of detect life](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Detect_Life "Skyrim:Scroll of Detect Life"), a scroll of fast healing, a scroll of fury, and a [greater soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Greater Soul Gem").

The corridor continues to the east past two fonts of stamina and a pod. In the next room is another font of stamina, while the path continues to the right. At the top of the first set of stairs is a seeker guarding a table with a common soul gem and copies of *Horker Attacks*, *The Poison Song, Book IV*, *Shadowmarks*, *[Five Songs of King Wulfharth](/wiki/Skyrim:Five_Songs_of_King_Wulfharth "Skyrim:Five Songs of King Wulfharth")*, and *[Myths of Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Myths_of_Sheogorath "Skyrim:Myths of Sheogorath")*. At the top of the next set of stairs is a font of stamina, with nothing else of interest on the rest of the ascending walkways except a scrye at the end. The scrye again repositions the entrance corridor to allow access to a new area.

The corridor continues to the next room, with copies of *Thirsk, A Revised History*, *[The Poison Song, Book III](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Poison_Song,_Book_III "Skyrim:The Poison Song, Book III")*, and *[The Five Far Stars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Five_Far_Stars "Skyrim:The Five Far Stars")* on the ground next to another scrye to the west, and a closed gate nearby to the north. The scrye opens a gate to a small treasure room visible just behind the scrye accessed by a short corridor starting to the southwest. Passing the pool in the middle of the room on the way to the corridor causes a lurker to rise from the water. In the treasure room is a vessel and a table with two soul gems (one [petty](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") and one [lesser](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem")), a [scroll of frost thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Frost_Thrall "Skyrim:Scroll of Frost Thrall"), a [scroll of magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Magelight "Skyrim:Scroll of Magelight"), and a copy of the [Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Seeker "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker") (only if your [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill is at least level 40). The scrye to open the gate to the north is just outside the treasure room. Beyond the gate is a stairway ascending past two fonts of stamina to end at a font of magicka and the book to Chapter V.

### Chapter V

Chapter V starts in a corridor, with a font of magicka at the starting point. The corridor passes a font of stamina before entering the top level of the tower. Three seekers guard the area, three pods are along the outer walkway to the west and north, and four pedestals are also on the outer walkway. In order to access the book to Chapter VI, the four "On Apocrypha" books collected earlier must be placed on the four pedestals, and will become irretrievable after the fourth book is placed. The solution, starting from the pedestal near the entrance and moving clockwise, is **Gnashing Blades—Prying Orbs—Boneless Limbs—Delving Pincers**. Once the four books are placed in the correct order, the book to Chapter VI appears on the pedestal in the center of the tower.

### Chapter VI

Chapter VI starts in a room with a wall in the middle. Around to the right is a table with a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill book *[The Art of War Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Art_of_War_Magic "Skyrim:The Art of War Magic")*, a scroll of stoneflesh, a [scroll of grand healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Grand_Healing "Skyrim:Scroll of Grand Healing"), and a greater soul gem. Around to the left is a pod that may be difficult to activate; you will need to aim the cursor at its lower section. The corridor ascends to the west past an open gate to a large open area. Two seekers guard the area, and if you have not started the quest, a lurker rises from the pool in the middle of the area when you pass the gate, which closes behind you. Flanking the gate are two fonts of stamina, with two more fonts of stamina on either side of the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") ahead. The wall teaches part of the [Dragon Aspect](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Aspect "Skyrim:Dragon Aspect") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"), applying the term "word wall" literally, as it appears as a scrolling book.

If the quest [At the Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha") has not started, you will be unable to progress further. After the quest has started, [Sahrotaar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahrotaar "Skyrim:Sahrotaar") will appear once the word has been learned. You must use all three words of [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") to force him to obey you. Once you are riding Sahrotaar, he will fly northwest over a platform with two seekers and a lurker, and will then head to the top of the tower. There, you will confront Miraak and two other dragons, [Kruziikrel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kruziikrel "Skyrim:Kruziikrel") and [Relonikiv](/wiki/Skyrim:Relonikiv "Skyrim:Relonikiv"). Once Miraak is defeated, Hermaeus will appear, kill Miraak, and raise the *Waking Dreams* book from the pool in the middle. Your reward is the ability to reassign perk points. At the cost of one dragon soul per skill, you will be able to choose a skill from which to remove your activated perks, and can then use the reclaimed perk points to unlock any perks you wish, including perks in the initially chosen skill. More details can be found [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills#Perks "Skyrim:Skills"). To exit this part of Apocrypha, use the non-circular part of the black book.

## Notes

- Unlike the other sections of Apocrypha accessed through Black Books, you can never return to the first five chapters of this area after you defeat Miraak, so be sure to pick up any items you don't wish to leave behind before mounting Sahrotaar.
  - If you previously read Waking Dreams and advanced to Chapter 6 before starting the quest, you will proceed directly from there.

# Skyrim:Apocrypha

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Worldspace: Apocrypha  ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Apocrypha "Lore:Apocrypha")) | | |
| # of Zones | 7 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | 25 |
| Occupants | |
| [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"), [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2ApocryphaEnd01, DLC2ApocryphaEnd02, DLC2ApocryphaEnd03, DLC2ApocryphaEnd04, DLC2ApocryphaEnd05, DLC2ApocryphaEnd06, DLC2ApocryphaEnd07, DLC2ApocryphaEnd08, DLC2ApocryphaEnd09, DLC2ApocryphaEnd10, DLC2ApocryphaEnd11, DLC2ApocryphaEnd12, DLC2ApocryphaEnd13, DLC2ApocryphaEnd14, DLC2ApocryphaEnd15, DLC2ApocryphaEnd16, DLC2ApocryphaOrigin, DLC2ApoIslandA01, DLC2ApoIslandA02, DLC2ApoIslandA03, DLC2ApoIslandA04, DLC2ApoStart02, DLC2ApoStart03, DLC2ApoStart04, DLC2ApoStart05, DLC2Book01DungeonEnd01, DLC2Book01DungeonEnd02, DLC2Book01DungeonEnd03, DLC2Book01DungeonEnd04, DLC2Book01DungeonEnd05, DLC2Book01DungeonEnd06, DLC2Book01DungeonEnd07, DLC2Book02DungeonExterior | |
| Location | |
| [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion") | |

Apocrypha

**Apocrypha** is [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora")'s [plane of Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Planes_of_Oblivion "Lore:Planes of Oblivion").

It is an endless library where all forbidden knowledge can be found, with stacks of books reaching towards the glowing green sky. You can enter the plane via Black Books found in dungeons and other locations throughout [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim"). According to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth"), the Black Books are of unknown origin; he claims that some may have been written long ago, and others could be from the future.

The realm is inhabited by Daedra called [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") and [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"). Tentacles constantly breach the acidic dark waters and sometimes whip at you, causing a significant amount of damage if they manage to hit you. The acidic waters with the tentacles are also corrosive and cause damage if stepped in. Some areas of Apocrypha, specifically [Filament and Filigree](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(Filament_and_Filigree) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (Filament and Filigree)") and [The Sallow Regent](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(The_Sallow_Regent) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (The Sallow Regent)"), are covered in a consuming [darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Darkness "Skyrim:Traps") that will inflict continuous health damage if you enter it; to avoid damage, you must either create or seek sources of light, such as the plane's floating [Wisp-Lanterns](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp-Lantern "Skyrim:Wisp-Lantern").

Some areas are divided into "chapters"; to progress, you must find the book to access the next chapter. Every chapter does not necessarily need to be accessed in turn in order to reach the end of a book, as certain chapters in some areas may be skipped entirely or accessed out of numerical order. One great example of this is The Hidden Twilight, of which the only uses for chapters 4 and 5 are to solve a puzzle fight 2 seekers and get a skill book for every school of magic.

There are seven accessible areas of Apocrypha, each associated with a [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book (book)"):

- [Epistolary Acumen](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(Epistolary_Acumen) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (Epistolary Acumen)")
- [Filament and Filigree](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(Filament_and_Filigree) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (Filament and Filigree)")
- [The Hidden Twilight](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(The_Hidden_Twilight) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (The Hidden Twilight)")
- [The Sallow Regent](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(The_Sallow_Regent) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (The Sallow Regent)")
- [The Winds of Change](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(The_Winds_of_Change) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (The Winds of Change)")
- [Untold Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(Untold_Legends) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (Untold Legends)")
- [Waking Dreams](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha_(Waking_Dreams) "Skyrim:Apocrypha (Waking Dreams)")

The location and reward of each Black Book is detailed on the respective location pages.

For historical information on Apocrypha, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Apocrypha "Lore:Apocrypha").

#### Dragonborn Main Quest

- **[The Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:The Temple of Miraak")**: Uncover the source of [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)")'s power in the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak").
- **[The Gardener of Men](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gardener_of_Men "Skyrim:The Gardener of Men")**: Travel to the realm of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora") to learn the rest of [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will").
- **[At the Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha")**: Confront [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)") at the summit of Apocrypha and defeat him once and for all.

#### Side Quests

- **[Black Book: Filament and Filigree](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (book)")'s hidden knowledge.
- **[Black Book: The Hidden Twilight](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (book)")'s hidden knowledge.
- **[Black Book: The Sallow Regent](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (book)")'s hidden knowledge.
- **[Black Book: The Winds of Change](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (book)")'s hidden knowledge.
- **[Black Book: Untold Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (quest)")**: Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (book)")'s hidden knowledge.

## Notes

[Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") in Apocrypha

- The Black Books will only transport you to Apocrypha if you are currently in [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you use a Black Book while you are in Skyrim, the ground will briefly shake, and the message "A vision of Solstheim swims before your eyes and then is gone." will appear on the screen, and you will not be teleported to Apocrypha.
- The Black Books will only transport you to Apocrypha if you read them while standing. If you read a Black Book while sitting down, the message "You are unable to concentrate on what you're reading." will appear on the screen, and you will not be teleported to Apocrypha.
- You cannot normally die in Apocrypha. If you lose sufficient health, you will fall to your knees in a fashion similar to essential characters and the message "You can't continue fighting." will appear, after which you are removed from the realm and returned to the location in Solstheim where you used the book. The exception to this is the [final battle](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha") with [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)").
- You can also return to Solstheim from within the realm by reading any Black Book inside Apocrypha; the book does not have to be the same one you used to enter the realm.
- Even after the Dragonborn questline is finished, all Black Books will permanently remain as quest items with no way to remove them from your inventory.
- Apocrypha features unique activators and containers. "Scryes" open gates and extend staircases, while "fonts of magicka" and "fonts of stamina" may be used to restore your [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") and [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina"), respectively. [Pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Pod "Skyrim:Pod") and [vessels](/wiki/Skyrim:Vessel "Skyrim:Vessel") contain a variety of loot.
- There is an abundance of valuable books, scrolls, and [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") in Apocrypha, found on shelves and tables, in pods and vessels, and dropped by seekers and lurkers upon death. This includes [skill books](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books"), as well as [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells "Skyrim:Spells") you might not be able to acquire otherwise based on your current level or skills.
- Followers cannot accompany you into Apocrypha. However, you can still summon reinforcements using abilities such as [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spells and the [Summon Spectral Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Spectral_Assassin "Skyrim:Summon Spectral Assassin") power. The [Call Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Call_Dragon "Skyrim:Call Dragon") and [Summon Durnehviir](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Durnehviir "Skyrim:Summon Durnehviir")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") shouts will not work here, however.
- Only one reward per Black Book can be active at a time. You can change your reward at any time by reading the Black Book where it originated from. The only exception is Waking Dreams, which grants a permanent reward.
- When first reading a book, the "Return to Solstheim" option only appears after choosing one of the rewards. The following times, the option is directly available and, since the return to Solstheim takes several seconds, you can activate it first and then choose a reward.
- The [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout will protect you from the corrosive black water, but not the dark areas.
- If you wear [Ahzidal's boots of Waterwalking](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Boots_of_Waterwalking "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Boots of Waterwalking") to walk over the black water, you will still take damage as if you were swimming in it. In addition, upon touching the water, you'll be applied with a unique effect for a few seconds: you'll be surrounded by neon green smoke and you'll take on a ghostly appearance, albeit in the same neon green glow. The same can happen if you hover above the water in [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") form.
- It is impossible to see when in the black water of Apocrypha: while the water isn't that deep and does have a bottom, it is opaque black, and no light source (such as [Candlelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlelight "Skyrim:Candlelight")) or game setting (such as turning the brightness all the way up) will allow you to see anything, even your character if you dive (or fall) into the water in third-person. Because of this, it is extremely easy to get lost in the water and die unless you swim in first person.

## Bugs

- Several animated pieces in Apocrypha do not make sounds when walked on.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- You may be unable to go back to Solstheim using either the Black Book or the activator at the end, instead receiving the message "You are unable to concentrate on what you're reading."
  - Disable [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode") if you have it enabled.
  - Step into the black water in Apocrypha or, if available, a dark area that causes damage. When you lose all your health, you'll be transported out of the book.
  -  Use the `coc` command to move to another location, (e.g., `coc DLC2RavenRock01`).
- You may continue taking damage after dying in a dark area, even though you're no longer in Apocrypha or in darkness.
- Upon returning to Solstheim the sky may still be set to the swirling green sky effect for Apocrypha.
  - Fast-traveling to any Solstheim location will remove the effect.
- Masser and Secunda may appear in the sky, even though you aren't supposed to be in Tamriel. This is especially noticeable at night. **?**
- DLC2ApocryphaWeather and DLC2ApocryphaWeatherNEW both have an invalid sound type set to a deleted form ID.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.8, addresses this issue. The bad sound entries have been removed as no correct ones could be located.

## Overview

Aquillius Aeresius

**Aquillius Aeresius** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") living in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") with [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici").

At 8am, he heads down to the [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") docks and wanders around there. He goes to sleep at midnight inside of Vittoria's house.

Aquillius wears a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes#00086991 "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes#00086993 "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"). He carries a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Vittoria Vici's House") to [Vittoria Vici's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici%27s_House "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici's House").

## Dialogue

He shares these two dialogue lines with Vittoria Vici. If talked to, he will say either:

:   *"Good business for the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") means all the more gold for the [Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion")."*
:   *"I don't have time for anyone too lazy or cowardly to make their own way in this world."*

## Notes

- It's unclear what exactly Aquillius' purpose is. It's possible he was intended to take over as merchant for the East Empire Company in case Vittoria died, but this role is actually given to the [East Empire Dockmaster](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Dockmaster "Skyrim:East Empire Dockmaster") internally. His factions imply that he might have also functioned as a backup for Vittoria's presence at the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") party during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), but besides being in all the same factions as Vittoria (which were in all likelihood just copied), there is no evidence he was to be involved in the quest. He has no alias for it, no coding mentions him, and he doesn't have equivalent lines for Vittoria's specific dialogue during the quest. Generic rumors for the guests are recorded in his voice type, which no other guest uses, but these might have also been accidentally recorded for [Malborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Malborn "Skyrim:Malborn"), as he does have the same voice type.
-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, raises Aquillius' level from 1 to 4, and removes his -49 health modifier.
- Aquillius has almost the exact same schedule as Vittoria, the only difference being his sandbox package `SolitudeDocksWander8x12`, which Vittoria doesn't possess. This results in him spending almost the entire day following her around.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, removes Aquillius' counter AI package from his base actor so he doesn't crowd Vittoria while she works. It's been added to the EastEmpire alias in the `DialogueSolitude` quest so that he'll resume when Vittoria is killed.
-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, adds merchant factions to Aquillius' faction list, in line with changes made to Vittoria.

## Bugs

- Due to having no cleanup script attached, Aquillius' body will remain in the world forever, in case he dies.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, addresses this issue. He has been given a cleanup script, and his body will now be present inside of a coffin inside the Hall of the Dead. This coffin was previously unused.

source_url: "https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Aranea_Ienith"
title: "Skyrim:Aranea Ienith"

Aranea Ienith at Azura's shrine

Aranea chanting to Azura

**Aranea Ienith** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [elemental mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageElemental "Skyrim:CombatMageElemental") and a worshipper of [Azura](/wiki/Lore:Azura "Lore:Azura"). She can be found praying at the [Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura") and will task you with finding [Nelacar](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelacar "Skyrim:Nelacar"), whom she says holds the power of the stars. According to Aranea, Azura led her people out of [Vvardenfell](/wiki/Lore:Vvardenfell "Lore:Vvardenfell") to safety. If you choose to return [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star") to the shrine rather than give it to Nelacar, she will become a potential [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") after completion of the quest. In addition, she can be [recruited](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades") to join the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades") at [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple"). If you cleanse it with the help of Nelacar, turning it into [The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star_(item) "Skyrim:The Black Star (item)"), she will threaten to kill you for defiling a Daedric artifact.

She is a very powerful mage wearing [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0006b46c "Skyrim:Boots") when you meet her. She carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a [staff of frostbite](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Frostbite "Skyrim:Staff of Frostbite"). She knows a variety of [spells](#Spells) as well.

## Related Quests

- **[The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star")**: Help find and repair [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star").
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

## Dialogue

At the shrine, she can be heard chanting to Azura:

:   *"No harm shall come to me, for I live under Azura's wisdom. Her foresight protects me. Her insight sustains me."*
:   *"We are children of the Twilight. Beings who are to be guided from the darkness into the light. And from the light into darkness."*
:   *"Azura. Who led her children away from the disaster of Vvardenfell. You are the prophet that reveals our true future."*

You may continue to hear this chanting during [The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star"), but not after you complete the quest.

### The Black Star

Upon greeting her, she will tell you:

:   *"Azura has seen your coming, traveler. It was not curiosity, but fate, that has led you here."*

You can reply in three ways:

:   :   '**Seen my coming'? What do you mean?**
    :   *"Azura has given me the gift of foresight. I had a vision of you walking up the steps to this altar long before you were born. You have been chosen to be her champion. I know it is unexpected, but do not worry. It will all unfold as she has predicted.*

:   :   **What is this place? Who's Azura?**
    :   *"This shrine was built by the Dunmer. As our land was scorched by fire and brimstone, Azura's prophecies led us to safety. She is a Daedra, a powerful being who watches from beyond our mortal plane. She has chosen you to be her champion."*

:   :   **I don't believe in fate.**
    :   *"Perhaps that is what you are meant to believe. To better serve your role as Azura's champion. Do not fight it. Azura's prophecies always come to pass. To deny them is to go headlong into the darkness with no light to guide you."*

Whichever option you chose, you can still refuse to be anyone's champion. She will concede:

:   :   :   **I'm not anyone's champion. Find someone else.**
        :   *"There is no one else, but very well. I cannot force you to accept your destiny."*

If you agree to do Azura's bidding, Aranea will elaborate on a vision she received:

:   :   :   **Very well. What does Azura need?**
        :   *"You must go to a fortress, endangered by water, yet untouched by it. Inside, you will find an elven mage who can turn the brightest star as black as night. It is cryptic, I know, but Azura's signs are never wrong. I believe the fortress may refer to [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). Ask if they know this elven enchanter."*

You can then follow up with more questions.

:   **I'd like to know more about Azura.**
:   *"She is the Goddess of Dawn and Dusk. Azura sees into the Twilight of the future, and guides her followers through it."*

As for where the shrine came from, she will explain:

:   **Where did this shrine come from?**
:   *"My people, the Dunmer, built it. We fled from [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") after Vvardenfell erupted almost [200 years ago](/wiki/Lore:Red_Year "Lore:Red Year"). Those of us who were faithful to Azura were given a vision that led us away from the island before the worst came. This shrine is our thanks to her. That none will forget that she watches over us all."*

Should you ask her, she will also confirm that she is all alone at the shrine:

:   **Are you all alone here?**
:   *"Yes. There were others at first, but Azura's visions tested everyone's faith. One by one, they left. Afraid to know their own future. But I refuse to abandon the shrine. The visions are a gift. Azura warns me of tragedy, war, death before it happens. I won't leave her guidance."*

When you part ways with her, she will tell you:

:   *"Twilight guide your path."*
:   *"May Azura's magic protect you."*
:   *"This has all been foreseen, and we must play our parts."*

Greeting her again will have her say:

:   *"Azura is watching over you. She has seen this before it ever happened."*
:   *"All will happen as it has been foretold."*
:   *"The Twilight has foreseen all of this. Everything will be revealed in time."*

With further investigation in Winterhold, you will discover that the mage is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") named Nelacar, who lives at [the Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth"). After some persuasion, he will confess that he studied [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star") under a fellow mage, [Malyn Varen](/wiki/Skyrim:Malyn_Varen "Skyrim:Malyn Varen"). Malyn was later banished from the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") for killing a student, and moved to [Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep") to further his research on the Star. He will plead you to keep the Star from Azura, but whether you choose to do so or not, you have to retrieve the Star from Ilinalta's Deep. If you have not retrieved Azura's Star yet, you can still report your findings to Aranea, who will be encouraging:

:   **I think I found the mage from your vision.**
:   *"Good. All will be revealed in time. Keep playing your part, and Azura will reward you."*

Once you have the broken Star, you can choose to bring it to Nelacar or to Aranea. When you talk to her, she will say:

:   *"Azura's Star! I knew the Lady of Twilight had sent you for a reason. Hand it over to me. I will ask Azura to restore the Star to its original purity."*

Should you request for more time to think about it, she will respond:

:   :   **I need a moment. I'll be back later.**
    :   *"I understand. Speaking to a goddess is overwhelming for many. Return when you're prepared."*

When you approach her again, she will ask:

:   *"Are you ready for me to show Azura her Star and receive her wisdom?"*

Letting her take it will have her say:

:   :   **Here. Take it.**
    :   *"I will commune with Azura."*

As she takes the Star, placing it on the altar.

She will pray:

:   *"Azura. Mother of Roses. Goddess of Dusk and Dawn. Your chosen champion has returned your Star to you."*

She'll then address you:

:   *"She wishes to speak to you herself. Please. Place your hands on the altar, and you will hear her voice."*

She will walk away from the altar, and if talked to, she will repeat:

:   *"Please place your hands on the altar. Azura wishes to speak with you."*

From the planes of [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion"), Azura will tell you that her Star is useless for now, as it is occupied by Malyn Varen's soul. She will offer to send you to the Star's realm, so you can dispatch Malyn and claim the Star as yours. Once you have done so, you will be returned to Skyrim, and Aranea will return to pray at the altar. If you approach her, you will see that she is filled with loss:

:   *"While you were in the Star, Azura gave me a vision. Her last, she said. I have never been without Azura's foresight since escaping Morrowind. I don't know what to do."*

She will come up with an idea:

:   *"If you need me, I'd be honored to accompany you, Guardian of the Star. It would give me a purpose."*

If you express your thanks, she will warmly wish you:

:   :   **Thank you, Aranea.**
    :   *"Twilight watch over you, guardian."*

If you instead ask of her usefulness, she will respond:

:   :   **What use would you be?**
    :   *"I was a sorceress of no small skill before I came into Azura's faith. Afterwards, her magic sustained me. I could easily provide my spells to your cause. Protect you from harm. Defeat your enemies."* Either way, she is now available as your follower.

If asked, she will tell you that Azura isn't giving her more visions:

:   **So Azura isn't giving you more visions?**
:   '"No. She said my part was over. That my fate had moved beyond the Twilight, and I was on my own. I will tend Azura's shrine when you do not need me. I still have my duties, but for the first time I feel... alone."

She will bid you farewell with the words:

:   *"Until next time, guardian."*
:   *"It's been an honor, guardian."*

Her greetings are similar:

:   *"The Twilight watches us all, guardian."*
:   *"Yes, champion of Azura?"*
:   *"What do you need, guardian?"*

Alternatively, you can return Azura's Star to Nelacar, turning it into the Black Star. Should you choose this option, attempting to speak to Aranea will only have her warn:

:   *"Leave this shrine, blasphemer, before I kill you for defiling Azura's artifact."*

She cannot be engaged with, but despite what she claims, she will not turn hostile if you linger around the place.

## Spells

She is able to cast the following spells:

[Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration")
:   [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh"), [Stoneflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoneflesh "Skyrim:Stoneflesh")

[Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration")
:   [Conjure Flame Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Flame Atronach"), [Conjure Frost Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Frost Atronach")

[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")
:   [Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Chain Lightning"), [Ice Spike](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Spike "Skyrim:Ice Spike"), [Ice Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Storm "Skyrim:Ice Storm"), [Icy Spear](/wiki/Skyrim:Icy_Spear "Skyrim:Icy Spear"), [Lightning Bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt"), [Thunderbolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Thunderbolt "Skyrim:Thunderbolt")

[Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration")
:   [Close Wounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Close_Wounds "Skyrim:Close Wounds"), [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing"), [Steadfast Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Ward "Skyrim:Steadfast Ward")

## Bugs

- After inducted into the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades"), Aranea will use the lines she says as greetings after you receive [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star"), instead of the generic Blades greetings. **?**

Arcadia's Cauldron

**Arcadia's Cauldron** is an [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") shop in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s market area.

It is run by apothecary and [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") trainer [Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia "Skyrim:Arcadia") who also lives in the store. If Arcadia is killed, [Ahlam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahlam "Skyrim:Ahlam") will take over. It consists of one area only, *[Arcadia's Cauldron](#Arcadia.27s_Cauldron)*.

Like all other stores, Arcadia's Cauldron has a number of fixed wares on display scattered around the main trading room. These can be bought from the proprietor Arcadia and will disappear from the room when purchased. For a list of these special items, see [this section](#Displayed_Merchandise).

## Related Quests

- **[Alchemy Tutorial](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Tutorial "Skyrim:Alchemy Tutorial")**: Learn the basics of potion making. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
