- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Arcadia's Cauldron

Inside Arcadia's Cauldron

The main trading room consists of a huge fireplace, an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and a huge desk to the east, where Arcadia stands every day between 8am and 8pm. Without the displayed merchandise, only a few items are left on the desk; namely copies of the books *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")*, which adds four map markers for [standing stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones"), and *[Of Fjori and Holgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Of_Fjori_and_Holgeir "Skyrim:Of Fjori and Holgeir")*, which details the events of [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)"). In the southeastern corner are two food sacks, a few common books, and a cupboard with clutter. Between the cupboard and the alchemy lab is a door leading to Arcadia's private study. On the table sits a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") with two [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), and a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") skill book  *[Herbalist's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbalist%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:Herbalist's Guide to Skyrim")*. The shelves in the southwestern corner hold some common books, along with some [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), a slice of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), some common books, and a food sack. The room also has a back door leading to Whiterun. The main trading room also has two doors along the western wall. One of them is apprentice-locked and leads to a non-respawning chest with some random loot, a [food barrel](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Barrel "Skyrim:Containers"), and two fish barrels. The other door leads to a set of stairs to the upstairs area.

The second floor overlooks the main trading room and is pretty bare-bones, save for two non-respawning wardrobes with clothes and, in the northwestern corner, a table with some [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a [grilled chicken breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Chicken_Breast "Skyrim:Grilled Chicken Breast"), right next to a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"). Underneath the table is a food sack. Along the southern wall is a door to Arcadia's private quarters which consists of a bed, a non-respawning wardrobe with clothes, the *[Business Ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger")*, and the [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") which contains random items.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are initially situated around the store. You can purchase them from Arcadia or steal them. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

|  |
| --- |
| - **Apparel**: 1 [College Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:College_Boots "Skyrim:College Boots") - **Potions**: 3 [Frostbite Venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), 1 [Potion of Haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling"), 3 [Potion of Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), 1 [Potion of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), 4 [Potion of Minor Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), 1 [Potion of Minor Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), 1 [Potion of Resist Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), 1 [Potion of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), 1 [Weak Aversion to Shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Shock "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Shock"), 1 [Weak Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison"), 1 [Weak Stamina Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Stamina_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Stamina Poison") - **Ingredients**: 3 [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), 1 [Blue Dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Dartwing "Skyrim:Blue Dartwing"), 1 [Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), 2 [Canis Root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), 1 [Creep Cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"), 7 [Deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), 1 [Ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), 1 [Fire Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), 1 [Glow Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), 1 [Hagraven Feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), 1 [Ice Wraith Teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth"), 1 [Imp Stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), 1 [Juniper Berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), 2 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), 1 [Orange Dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"), 1 [Rock Warbler Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), 1 [Skeever Tail](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail"), 2 [Slaughterfish Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), 1 [Spider Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg"), 1 [Spriggan Sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Sap "Skyrim:Spriggan Sap"), 1 [Taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), 1 [Troll Fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), 2 [Void Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), 3 [White Cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") - **Books**: 1 *[Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths](/wiki/Lore:Herbane%27s_Bestiary:_Ice_Wraiths "Lore:Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths")* - **Misc**: 1 [Basket](/wiki/Skyrim:Basket "Skyrim:Basket"), 1 [Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Flagon "Skyrim:Flagon"), 1 [Tongs](/wiki/Skyrim:Tongs "Skyrim:Tongs") |

Other items may also be present in the store, but are not available for purchase.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the store's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |

| ~11 | Common [Ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") | Max 15 (15@75%) |
| 1 | Common [Recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes") |  |
| ~8 | Leveled Fortify Skill [Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~13 | Leveled Healing [Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") | Max 15 (10@75% + 5@100%) |
| ~8 | Leveled Other [Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~8 | Leveled Resist [Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~8 | Leveled [Poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~1 | Poison [Recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes") | Max 1 (1@50%) |

## Notes

- The [Key to Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Key to Arcadia's Cauldron") is carried by Arcadia.
  - This key will only open the front door to the shop, it will not open the back door.
- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the right of the front door outside. This mark indicates the valuable loot inside, such as the various potions and ingredients, the chest, and the Alchemy skill book.
- If you complete the quest [Salt for Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_for_Arcadia "Skyrim:Salt for Arcadia"), you can then take all low-level items from this location, due to the quest increasing your disposition with Arcadia.
- With the Merchant perk of the Speech skill you can place stolen objects into the cupboard in Arcadia's Cauldron and then buy them back from her which clears the stolen flag.

## Bugs

- If you break into the shop at night, [Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia "Skyrim:Arcadia") might be talking in her sleep. She will say all of her normal phrases but while in her bed and not moving her mouth.
- The store may be locked during normal business hours and open in the middle of the night, when Arcadia won't do business with you.
  - A successful workaround may be to fast-travel out of the city and return. You may need to fast-travel from many different locations.
  - You may also need to try waiting for long periods of time (potentially many days) in order for the store's hours to reset.
  - Breaking into the shop during normal business hours may serve as a workaround as well, since Arcadia should be inside at work during those hours.

Arcadia

**Arcadia** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerAlchemyExpert "Skyrim:TrainerAlchemyExpert") and the proprietor of [Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron"), an alchemy shop in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). She sells potions and poisons and allows you to use her [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"). She even gives you a [hint](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Tutorial "Skyrim:Alchemy Tutorial") about how to create a healing potion, should you happen to ask. She uses her skills to provide expert [training](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") and also works on creating a love elixir to test on an unsuspecting [castle wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire").

She sleeps in her bed above the main trading room every night between midnight and 8am. She then unlocks the doors and spends twelve solid hours offering her various services to paying customers. From 8pm until her bedtime, she wanders around the shop, at times relaxing, eating, or working at her alchemy lab. She is never seen outside her store.

She wears a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223c "Skyrim:Clothing") with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223d "Skyrim:Clothing"). She carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), the [shop key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Key to Arcadia's Cauldron") and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Alchemy Tutorial](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Tutorial "Skyrim:Alchemy Tutorial")**: Learn the basics of potion making. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Salt for Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_for_Arcadia "Skyrim:Salt for Arcadia")**: [Farengar](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") asks you to deliver some [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") to Arcadia.
- **[Further Study](/wiki/Skyrim:Further_Study "Skyrim:Further Study")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Collect a fish to help an alchemist experiment with potions. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Salt for Arcadia

If you accept to do Farengar Secret-Fire a [favor](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_for_Arcadia "Skyrim:Salt for Arcadia") and bring his special salts to Arcadia, she will reveal what it is used for:

:   *"Ah, splendid, splendid. It's for a special brew I'm working on. A love elixir like none other. Maybe I'll test it on Farengar first... Oh, but I suppose you expect some compensation. Um... here, these potions should suffice."*

## Dialogue

When brewing potions in her store, she says one of the following:

:   *"You brewed a truly vile poison there. I pity the beast that tastes that."*
:   *"An "interesting" mixture... Keep experimenting. You will improve with practice."*
:   *"That's a fine potion you've put together."*

When you enter her store, she will readily give you the full sales speech, randomly picking between:

:   *"You'll find tonics, salves, poultices and potions on my shelves. Browse to your heart's content."*
:   *"If there's anything I can help you with, you have but to ask."*
:   *"I offer remedies for ailments both common and rare. Do let me know if I can be of service."*
:   *"I sell cures for all ills, and I'll be happy to serve you."*
:   *"Maybe a hardy Nord like you doesn't need a cure-all. Hmm? What about an invisibility potion?"*
:   *"I have several elixirs for sale."*

She will also claim you are sick, just to sell her products:

:   *"You look rather pale. Could be Ataxia. It's quite a problem back home in Cyrodiil."*
:   *"Pardon me, but do I detect a case of the Rattles? I've got something for that."*

If you ask her about training, she will comment:

:   *"I think I can teach you a thing or two."*

She will finish conversations with:

:   *"Come back anytime if you need a remedy."*

Should you invest in her store, she will say:

:   *"By helping me, you're helping the good folk of Whiterun. How could I say no to that?"*
:   *"May prosperity bless us both!"*

When spoken to directly, she can be asked questions:

:   **So you're a healer?**
:   *"Of a sort. I don't have formal training in the Restoration school, but... something just as good. Within these walls, I have all that I need to brew a potion for nearly any ailment. If I had a Septim for every case of Rockjoint or Witbane I've cured since I opened this shop, I'd be a rich woman indeed."*

:   **You ever think of returning to Cyrodiil?**
:   *"Why, because I'm a proud citizen of the Empire? Because the Stormcloaks only want Nords in Skyrim? The Stormcloaks can rot in Oblivion for all I care. I've lived in this city for twenty years. Twenty!"*

Her strong political stance will be turned into frustration if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") conquer Whiterun. She will then greet you with:

:   *"These Stormcloaks are ridiculous. They won't shop here because they think I'll sell them poisoned tonics. I should just go back to Cyrodiil."*

## Notes

- Arcadia is depicted on the [Cauldron Keeper](/wiki/Legends:Cauldron Keeper) card in [Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends").

## Bugs

- Arcadia will sometimes say *"Maybe a hardy [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") like you doesn't need a cure-all."* regardless of your race.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- Arcadia will sometimes use her normal generic dialogue like *"If there's anything I can help you with, you have but to ask."* while she is sleeping, no matter where you are in her store.
- Her body will never disappear and, as a result, nobody will take over her store.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters

## Overview

Arcane Enchanter

**Arcane Enchanters** are workbenches where [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") can be done. New enchanted items can be created, or existing items can be broken down, allowing you to learn any new magical effects used in the item's enchantment. How an Arcane Enchanter is used is described on the [Enchanting page](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting#Skill_Usage "Skyrim:Enchanting"). A category listing places where enchanters can be found is available at [Skyrim-Places-Arcane Enchanters](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Arcane_Enchanters "Category:Skyrim-Places-Arcane Enchanters").

### Eastmarch

-  **[Ansilvund Excavation](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_Excavation "Skyrim:Ansilvund Excavation")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") led by [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ansilvund)
-  **[Cragwallow Slope](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragwallow_Slope "Skyrim:Cragwallow Slope")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") home to [conjurers](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") and [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cragwallow+Slope)
-  **[Cronvangr Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Cave "Skyrim:Cronvangr Cave")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cronvangr+Cave)
-  **[Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") initially occupied by [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Amol)
-  **[Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar")** — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") and their leader [Naris the Wicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Naris_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Naris the Wicked"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Morvunskar)
-  **[Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings")** — A large [castle](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles") at the far end of the Valunstrad district in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Palace+of+the+Kings)
-  **[Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah")** — The [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sacellum+of+Boethiah)
-  **[Snapleg Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Snapleg_Cave "Skyrim:Snapleg Cave")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Rift Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Watchtower "Skyrim:Rift Watchtower") occupied by [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") and [monsters](/wiki/Skyrim:Monsters "Skyrim:Monsters"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Snapleg+Cave)
-  **[Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")** — A major city in the northeast of Skyrim near the [Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass") to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), and the capital of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windhelm)

### Falkreath Hold

-  **[Anise's Cabin](/wiki/Skyrim:Anise%27s_Cabin "Skyrim:Anise's Cabin")** — A small [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") west-southwest of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Anise%27s+Cabin)
-  **[Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne")** — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"), [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"), [gargoyles](/wiki/Skyrim:Gargoyle "Skyrim:Gargoyle"), and [death hounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bloodlet+Throne)
-  **[Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass")** — A small [passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") through the mountains between [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") and [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") containing a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brittleshin+Pass)
-  **[Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary")** — An active [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") sanctuary west of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dark+Brotherhood+Sanctuary)
-  **[Glenmoril Coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Coven "Skyrim:Glenmoril Coven")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") or [Glenmoril Witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Glenmoril+Coven)
-  **[Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Haemar%27s+Shame)
-  **[Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") north of the [Lady Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lady_Stone "Skyrim:The Lady Stone") containing [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ilinalta%27s+Deep)
- **[Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Falkreath)")** — The seat of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath")'s government and home to its [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Jarl%27s+Longhouse+%28Falkreath%29)
-  **[Orphan Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan_Rock "Skyrim:Orphan Rock")** — A wooded valley with a central rock plateau northeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch") or [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") led by a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Orphan+Rock)
-  **[Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing the conjurer [Bashnag](/wiki/Skyrim:Bashnag "Skyrim:Bashnag") and his [coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellsword_(NPC) "Skyrim:Spellsword (NPC)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Southfringe+Sanctum)
-  **[Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north-northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sunderstone+Gorge)

### Haafingar

-  **[Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace")** — The current seat of power for [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"), and [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"); and home to the [High King of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blue+Palace)
- **[Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour")** — A large [fortress](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") which acts as the headquarters of the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and residence of the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Dour)
- **[Erikur's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur%27s_House "Skyrim:Erikur's House")** — A large mansion lying just northwest of the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Erikur%27s+House)
-  **[Kilkreath Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins")** — A large [ruined temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [corrupted shades](/wiki/Skyrim:Corrupted_Shade "Skyrim:Corrupted Shade") created by the necromancer [Malkoran](/wiki/Skyrim:Malkoran "Skyrim:Malkoran"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kilkreath+Ruins)
-  **[Rimerock Burrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Rimerock_Burrow "Skyrim:Rimerock Burrow")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing an [atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach") and the powerful conjurer [Sebastian Lort](/wiki/Skyrim:Sebastian_Lort "Skyrim:Sebastian Lort"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rimerock+Burrow)
-  **[Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large [fortress](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles") on an island far northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") connected to [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar") which serves as the [Volkihar vampire clan](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan")'s home. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Volkihar+%28DG%29)

### Hjaalmarch

-  **[Dead Men's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Men%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Dead Men's Respite")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dead+Men%27s+Respite)
- **[Falion's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion%27s_House "Skyrim:Falion's House")** — The home of the town wizard in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falion%27s+House)
-  **[Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") initially occupied by [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Snowhawk)
-  **[Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian")** — A large [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"), [wisps](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Morokei](/wiki/Skyrim:Morokei_(creature) "Skyrim:Morokei (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Labyrinthian)
-  **[Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") northeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ustengrav)

### The Pale

-  **[Dimhollow Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Dimhollow_Crypt "Skyrim:Dimhollow Crypt")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills") and southwest of [Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt") where [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") is trapped. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dimhollow+Crypt+%28DG%29)
-  **[High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Vokun](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun_(creature) "Skyrim:Vokun (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=High+Gate+Ruins)
-  **[Nightcaller Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightcaller_Temple "Skyrim:Nightcaller Temple")** — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") on the clifftop overlooking [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nightcaller+Temple)
- **[The White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall")** — A large two-story structure that sits on a hillside overlooking most of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+White+Hall)

### The Reach

-  **[Dead Crone Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Crone_Rock "Skyrim:Dead Crone Rock")** — A small ruined [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") inhabited by [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), located south-southwest of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), just above [Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dead+Crone+Rock)
-  **[Deepwood Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt")** — A large [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Deepwood+Redoubt)
-  **[Dragontooth Crater](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragontooth_Crater "Skyrim:Dragontooth Crater")** — A [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") north-northwest of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragontooth+Crater)
-  **[Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"), [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"), and [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hag%27s+End)
-  **[Ragnvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald "Skyrim:Ragnvald")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Otar the Mad](/wiki/Skyrim:Otar_the_Mad "Skyrim:Otar the Mad"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ragnvald)
-  **[Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep")** — An ancient Dwarven keep built into the mountainside, used as a palace by the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Understone+Keep)

### The Rift

-  **[Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"), [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"), and [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darklight+Tower)
-  **[Darkwater Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pass "Skyrim:Darkwater Pass")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south-southwest of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkwater+Pass)
-  **[Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [Dragon Cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Cultist "Skyrim:Dragon Cultist"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Forelhost)
-  **[Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") which serves as the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)")'s base of operations. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Dawnguard+%28DG%29)
-  **[Geirmund's Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Geirmund%27s_Hall "Skyrim:Geirmund's Hall")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") east of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the draugr [Sigdis Gauldurson](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigdis_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Sigdis Gauldurson"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Geirmund%27s+Hall)
-  **[Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep")** — A castle located at the southern end of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mistveil+Keep)
-  **[Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") northwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Redwater+Den+%28DG%29)
-  **[Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southeast of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Treva%27s+Watch)

### Solstheim DB

-  **[Altar of Thrond](/wiki/Skyrim:Altar_of_Thrond "Skyrim:Altar of Thrond")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A [landmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Landmarks "Skyrim:Landmarks") west of the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") next to a small cave containing [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Altar+of+Thrond)
-  **[Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") containing a hidden [Tribunal Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple") shrine to the goddess [Almalexia](/wiki/Lore:Almalexia "Lore:Almalexia"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Ashfall%27s+Tear+%28CC%29)
-  **[Ashfallow Citadel](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfallow_Citadel "Skyrim:Ashfallow Citadel")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Imperial [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Highpoint Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Highpoint_Tower "Skyrim:Highpoint Tower") and northwest of the [Sun Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Stone "Skyrim:Sun Stone") being used as a base of operations by the [Morag Tong](/wiki/Skyrim:Morag_Tong "Skyrim:Morag Tong"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Ashfallow+Citadel)
-  **[Highpoint Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Highpoint_Tower "Skyrim:Highpoint Tower")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") containing [albino spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider "Skyrim:Albino Spider"), [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn"), and [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth")'s former apprentice [Ildari Sarothril](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari_Sarothril "Skyrim:Ildari Sarothril"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Highpoint+Tower)
- **[Morvayn Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvayn_Manor "Skyrim:Morvayn Manor")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — The home of [Lleril Morvayn](/wiki/Skyrim:Lleril_Morvayn "Skyrim:Lleril Morvayn"), [Adril Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Adril_Arano "Skyrim:Adril Arano"), and [Cindiri Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Cindiri_Arano "Skyrim:Cindiri Arano") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Morvayn+Manor)
-  **[Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in northern [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") initially containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Zahkriisos](/wiki/Skyrim:Zahkriisos_(creature) "Skyrim:Zahkriisos (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Raven+Rock+Mine)
- **[Severin Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Severin_Manor "Skyrim:Severin Manor")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — Initially the home of [Mirri Severin](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirri_Severin "Skyrim:Mirri Severin"), [Tilisu Severin](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilisu_Severin "Skyrim:Tilisu Severin"), and [Vendil Severin](/wiki/Skyrim:Vendil_Severin "Skyrim:Vendil Severin") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"), which can be obtained as player housing by completing the quest [Served Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Served_Cold "Skyrim:Served Cold"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Severin+Manor)
- **[Shaman's Hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Shaman%27s_Hut "Skyrim:Shaman's Hut")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — The home of shaman [Storn Crag-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider") and his daughter [Frea](/wiki/Skyrim:Frea "Skyrim:Frea") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Shaman%27s+Hut)
- **[Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — The main tower and home of [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") and his apprentice [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon") in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Tel+Mithryn)

### Whiterun Hold

-  **[Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass")** — A small [passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") through the mountains between [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") and [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") containing a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brittleshin+Pass)
-  **[Broken Fang Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Fang_Cave "Skyrim:Broken Fang Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") containing [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") and [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Broken+Fang+Cave)
-  **[Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach")** — The residence of the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), the hold's seat of political power, and the location of the hold's jail. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragonsreach)
-  **[Drelas' Cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas%27_Cottage "Skyrim:Drelas' Cottage")** — An isolated [cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") at the foot of a mountain in northern [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), and south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Drelas%27+Cottage)
-  **[Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [Silver Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dustman%27s+Cairn)
-  **[Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east-northeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock"), [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach"), and [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"), and the mages' leader, [the Caller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Caller "Skyrim:The Caller"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fellglow+Keep)
-  **[Serpent's Bluff Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Serpent%27s_Bluff_Redoubt "Skyrim:Serpent's Bluff Redoubt")** — A small [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and ruin southwest of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Serpent%27s+Bluff+Redoubt)
- **[Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn")** — A small [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") and tavern in the town of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sleeping+Giant+Inn)
  - It is in the secret room revealed to you during the quest [A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark").

### Winterhold

- **[Arch-Mage's Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch-Mage%27s_Quarters "Skyrim:Arch-Mage's Quarters")** — The area within the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") in which its current Arch-Mage resides. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Arch-Mage%27s+Quarters)
- **[Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach")** — An immense, naturally lit [cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") inhabited by hordes of [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and containing the ruins of a [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blackreach)
- **[Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance")** — The main living and sleeping quarters for most of the higher ranked mages of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hall+of+Countenance)
-  **[Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hob%27s+Fall+Cave)
- **[Reeking Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Reeking_Tower "Skyrim:Reeking Tower")** — A small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") occupied by [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider").
- **[Sea Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_Cave "Skyrim:Sea Cave")** — A cave located in the [Japhet's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly") area. The cave leads to the lower section of Japhet's Folly Towers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sea+Cave)

Arch-Curate Vyrthur

*"Your pathetic powers are no match for mine!"*

**Arch-Curate Vyrthur** is a [Snow Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Elf "Skyrim:Snow Elf") [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") located in the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"). He is the brother of [Knight-Paladin Gelebor](/wiki/Skyrim:Knight-Paladin_Gelebor "Skyrim:Knight-Paladin Gelebor") and the only other uncorrupted [Snow Elf](/wiki/Lore:Falmer "Lore:Falmer"). He created the [prophecy](/wiki/Lore:Tyranny_of_the_Sun "Lore:Tyranny of the Sun") which [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon") is chasing in the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") questline, after having been forsaken to [vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism") by [Auri-El](/wiki/Lore:Auri-El "Lore:Auri-El"). He sought revenge through the corruption of Auri-El's influence on [Nirn](/wiki/Lore:Nirn "Lore:Nirn")—his [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow")—which would have been achieved by dousing the artifact in the blood of a Daughter of Coldharbour, a being of the purest evil in [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel").

He wears a set of ancient Falmer armor, including [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Falmer_Boots "Skyrim:Ancient Falmer Boots"), [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Falmer_Cuirass "Skyrim:Ancient Falmer Cuirass"), and [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Falmer_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Ancient Falmer Gauntlets"). He carries an [Elven Dagger of Blizzards](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger_of_Blizzards "Skyrim:Elven Dagger of Blizzards"), as well as some random [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") and [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). He knows a number of spells, namely [Drain Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampiric_Drain "Skyrim:Vampiric Drain"), [Conjure Frost Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Frost Atronach"), [Vampiric Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Embrace_of_Shadows "Skyrim:Embrace of Shadows"), [Lightning Bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt"), [Ice Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Storm "Skyrim:Ice Storm"), [Icy Spear](/wiki/Skyrim:Icy_Spear "Skyrim:Icy Spear"), [Frost Cloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Cloak "Skyrim:Frost Cloak"), [Banish Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Banish_Daedra "Skyrim:Banish Daedra"), and [Command Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Command_Daedra "Skyrim:Command Daedra").

## Related Quests

- **[Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky")**: Find and retrieve [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow").

## Dialogue

During the quest [Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky"), Gelebor asks you to kill Vyrthur in exchange for [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow"). He is found sitting on a throne in [Auriel's Chapel](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Chapel "Skyrim:Auriel's Chapel"). As you approach he will begin to speak to you about [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana").

:   *"Did you really come here expecting to claim Auriel's Bow? You've done exactly as I predicted and brought your fetching companion to me. Which, I'm sorry to say, means your usefulness is at an end!"*

He will then release the [Frozen Chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Frozen_Chaurus "Skyrim:Frozen Chaurus") to attack you. After defeating them, he will say:

:   *"An impressive display, but a wasted effort. You delay nothing but your own deaths!"*

He will then use his power to pull down the ceiling and release half the [Frozen Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Frozen_Falmer "Skyrim:Frozen Falmer") to attack you:

:   *"Finish them!"*

After defeating the Frozen Falmer, the now angry Vyrthur will say *"This has gone on long enough."* as he summons an [Ancient Frost Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Ancient Frost Atronach") and releases the rest of the Frozen Falmer. During the fight, Serana remarks that his life will end here; however, he merely replies:

:   *"Child, my life ended long before you were born!"*

After defeating the Falmer and atronach, a now fearful Vyrthur will say:

:   *"No... I won't let you ruin centuries of preparations..."*

When Serana tells him to surrender and hand over the bow he will say:

:   *"Death first!"*

He will then use all his power to destroy Auriel's Chapel with you inside and run outside to the Temple Balcony. Exhausted from using all of his power he will begin to talk to Serana, allowing him time to recover.

:   **Serana**: *"Enough, Vyrthur. Give us the bow!"*
:   **Vyrthur**: *"How dare you. I was the Arch-Curate of Auri-El, girl. I had the ears of a god!"*
:   **Serana**: *"Until the "Betrayed" corrupted you. Yes, yes. We've heard this sad story."*
:   **Vyrthur**: *"Gelebor and his kind are easily manipulated fools. Look into my eyes, Serana. You tell me what I am."*
:   **Serana**: *"You're... you're a vampire? But Auriel should have protected you..."*
:   **Vyrthur**: *"The moment I was infected by one of my own Initiates, Auri-El turned his back on me. I swore I'd have my revenge, no matter what the cost."*
:   **Serana**: *"You want to take revenge... on a god?"*
:   **Vyrthur**: *"Auri-El himself may have been beyond my reach, but his influence on our world wasn't. All I needed was the blood of a vampire and his own weapon, Auriel's Bow."*
:   **Serana**: *"The blood of a vampire... Auriel's Bow... It... it was you? You created that prophecy?"*
:   **Vyrthur**: *"A prophecy that lacked a single, final ingredient... the blood of a pure vampire. The blood of a Daughter of Coldharbour."*
:   **Serana**: *"You were waiting... all this time for someone with my blood to come along. Well, too bad for you... I intend on keeping it. Let's see if your blood has any power to it!"*

Recovering enough to resume the fight, he will once again attack. As you kill him, his final words will be *"Farewell."* or *"Auri-El, forgive me..."*

## Combat Dialogue

| Condition | Dialogue | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Attacking an enemy | *"Her blood will be mine!"* | *"You're no match for me!"* |
| *"You can't stop the inevitable!"* | *"I'll scatter your ashes myself"* |
| *"Die, damn it... die!"* | *"I'll stain the ground with your blood!"* |
| *"The prophecy's end approaches!"* | *"You have no dominion here!"* |
| *"I'll darken the skies with her blood!"* | *"Your suffering will be legendary!"* |
| *"Your pathetic powers are no match for mine!"* | |
| Defeating an enemy | *"I'll feed your corpse to the Betrayed."* | |
| Detecting an enemy | *"Show yourself."* | *"This is pointless."* |
| *"Enough of these games."* | |
| Engaging an enemy | *"Come and face your destruction!"* | |
| Giving up the search | *"Craven fool. This isn't over."* | *"Hide if you wish, it matters little to me."* |
| Looking for an enemy | *"This is a waste of time."* | *"I'll find you yet, coward."* |
| Losing sight of an enemy | *"Run, coward! Run and never return!"* | *"You only delay the inevitable."* |
| *"Pitiful sorcery. You'll not stay hidden long."* | |
| Spotting an enemy | *"There you are!"* | *"This time, to the death!"* |
| Taunting an enemy | *"Centuries of preparation will not fall to ruin because of you!"* | *"I will herald the fall of eternal night!"* |
| *"Let twilight fall and blood spill!"* | *"Your existence is meaningless!"* |

## Notes

- His editor ID reveals his full name to be "Althadan Vyrthur".
- In the game files, he is part of a newly-created race known as `SnowElfRace`. It is largely based off of the [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") race, and even bears the name "High Elf", but for all purposes Vyrthur can be considered to be a [Snow Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Elf "Skyrim:Snow Elf").
  - The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* classifies him as the only member of the "Unique Falmer" section under the larger Falmer bestiary entry.
- Despite being a vampire, Vyrthur is still susceptible to poisons. This is because he is not actually a vampire as recognized by the game code: vampires of each race are treated as separate variants of the normal NPC races, and there is no proper vampire variant of the Snow Elves.
- Despite being a Snow Elf, Vyrthur's blood cannot be harvested for use in the [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane") quest.
- Since [Knight-Paladin Gelebor](/wiki/Skyrim:Knight-Paladin_Gelebor "Skyrim:Knight-Paladin Gelebor") cannot be killed or pickpocketed, Vyrthur has the only set of [Ancient Falmer Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Equipment#Falmer_Armor "Skyrim:Falmer Equipment") that you can retrieve in the game.
  - With version 2.0.2 of the [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch") and up, he additionally wears the Ancient Falmer Crown, which is also otherwise unobtainable.

# Skyrim:Arch-Mage's Quarters

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | House: Arch-Mage's Quarters ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Arch-Mage%27s+Quarters)) | | |

| # of [Arcane Enchanters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") | 1 |

Inside the Arch-Mage's Quarters

The **Arch-Mage's Quarters** is the area within the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") in which its current Arch-Mage resides.

All of the items found in the room are marked as owned and taking any of them is considered stealing until you become the Arch-Mage, although taking them in plain sight does not incur a bounty.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren") |

## Related Quests

- **[Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal")**: Uncover the mysteries beneath this ancient ruin.
- **[Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions")**: Find and consult the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain").
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.

## Arch-Mage's Quarters

The Arch-Mage's quarters are located at the top of the tallest tower in the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). The quarters are locked until the quest [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") has been completed. Prior to that point, the Arch-Mage, [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren") is either in the central courtyard of the College of Winterhold (night) or just inside the door to the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements") (day). It is an dodecagonal room (twelve-sided) with an antechamber and central garden containing various plants and fungi as listed below. There is a curved partition stone wall separating the sleeping area from the garden and the rest of the room. There are many different rugs on the floor around the outside of the room. The antechamber is an open empty space with a long wooden bench against both of the side walls with two College of Winterhold banners hanging above and a large rug on the floor. There are two entrances with stairs leading up from the antechamber in front of the Hall of Elements and [the Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"). Both of the flights of stairs continue past the antechamber to an exit to the roof of the tower. However this cannot be used as an additional entrance as there is no way to access this from the outside.

On your left as you enter the main part of the room is a square wooden table and two chairs. There are many mounted animal heads and skulls on the outer wall around the room including [bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear"), [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") and [sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat"). Beyond this is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") with a set of shelves on either side and two further sets to the right holding various [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"). Several barrels and baskets containing further ingredients are also in this area of the room. Continuing around the room to the left are several more sets of shelves holding a selection of random items, all listed below. Coming out from a wall to the northeast is a good quality double bed with small tables flanking it. To the right of the bed are two small wardrobes with one tall wardrobe between them; these all contain a selection of random [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots"), loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and items of clutter. On the right-hand small wardrobe is a dagger display case containing a [Dwarven Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"). There is a large round table and chair against the next wall section to the right with a wash basin beside it. To the right of this is a large display cabinet containing several [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), listed below. Next to this is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") with two wall shelves above holding several more soul gems. The final outer wall section before completing the circuit back to the antechamber has another square wooden table and two chairs. The curved partition wall starts opposite the second section with sets of shelves against the outer wall and continues around to opposite the large display cabinet. There are several [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks and a barrel by the start of it, a small table and two chairs against the first section, followed by a [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Safe "Skyrim:Safe"), a long unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") opposite the double bed containing random items, another square wooden table with two more chairs, and finally an open crate on the floor with a wall shelf above. There are three College of Winterhold banners hanging from the inside (facing the garden) of the partition wall. There are small semicircular windows high up on each of the twelve sections of wall, except the section by the antechamber, which has a large circular window also high on the wall, and is lead-lined with the College symbol.

## Notes

- Although the quarters themselves respawn every ten days (necessary for the alchemy garden to regrow), all the [containers](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers "Skyrim:Containers") inside are [safe for storage](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Containers "Skyrim:Containers").
- The quarters are also locked until you speak to [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") during the quest [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions").

## Bugs

- Sleeping in the bed as Arch-Mage will not result in being [well rested](/wiki/Skyrim:Well_Rested "Skyrim:Well Rested").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Taking some items in chests while Arch-Mage may still count as stealing. **?**

Arcturus

**Arcturus**, an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial"), is part of the group of [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Agent "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Agent") agents sent to the [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary") during the quest [Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate").

When you search the destroyed sanctuary for survivors, you will encounter [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") battling Arcturus near the dinner table in the northern chamber. Obviously losing the fight, the weakened Nazir will call upon you for help and you will have no choice but to battle and kill Arcturus.

Arcturus wields an [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword") and a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"). He wears a complete set of [Penitus Oculatus armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Armor "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Armor") and carries a few spare coins and possibly some random items like a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"), an [amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Amulets_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"), some inn [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and/or a drink.

## Related Quests

- **[Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate")**: Assist [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") members in the fight against the [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus") assault.

# Skyrim:Arcwind Point

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Ruin.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Ruin.png) | Nordic Ruin: Arcwind Point ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Arcwind+Point)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Arcwind_Point "Lore:Arcwind Point")) | | |

Arcwind Point

**Arcwind Point** is a small outdoor [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") and, after [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon").

## Related Quests

- **[Bones for a Crow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bones_for_a_Crow "Skyrim:Bones for a Crow")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragon_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragon Plate"): Hunt down the Forsworn Crowstooth.
- **[The Cause](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause_(quest) "Skyrim:The Cause (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause"): Investigate the activities of the [Mythic Dawn](/wiki/Lore:Mythic_Dawn "Lore:Mythic Dawn") cult.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

This location consists of several separate ruins. The area can be reached by a path south of the [Rift Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Imperial Camp"), or another path between [Froki's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Froki's Shack") and [Autumnwatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnwatch_Tower "Skyrim:Autumnwatch Tower"). It can be awkward to find the beginning of the path for the former route. The easiest way to find it is to leave the Imperial camp via the southeastern exit. Ahead on your right is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") beside a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"). If you turn and head due west, you'll join up with the early part of the path. The latter route also has a canis root near the beginning and a couple [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") bushes along it as it zigzags up the mountainside. You may also alert the dragon roosting on Autumnwatch Tower unless you choose to deal with it beforehand. Just after the path turns west and widens, there is an altar with three random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") on it and two [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") on or in front of it. You can also reach this path by climbing the mountain immediately to the right of Froki's shack. At the top of the mountain climb is a [shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrine of Talos"). From here, dropping down the mountain to the west brings you to where the second of the paths turns west and widens.

Circular barrow with a chest and dead Nord

Sunken barrow

Continuing along the path heading west, you are likely to face two leveled creatures near a circular barrow, the type with a covered passage around a central circular chamber. On the right, just before the barrow is a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein"). The barrow is nearly filled with snow and ice, and to reach the center you need to enter via the right-hand path. In the middle chamber is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") with a dead [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead) "Skyrim:Nord (dead)") beside it. Farther along the path heading west, it begins to descend. Ahead is a square stone arch with a sunken barrow beyond it. As you near the barrow, use of [Detect Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Undead "Skyrim:Detect Undead") will reveal a draugr slumbering in an upright sarcophagus. Any noise fighting the draugr may alert several skeletons to your presence and cause them to converge on you. There are two paths continuing to head west from here; most of the ten skeletons are found along the southern of the two paths, as is a second quicksilver ore vein. If Dragon Rising has been completed, you may also encounter a dragon at any point from here onward, as it is regularly disturbed by up to two leveled draugr found near the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") who it may be fighting against. To the north is the other path that leads to the ruins.

The word wall added by *Dawnguard*

The two paths merge again just before a huge structure made from interconnecting arches, with a raised platform in the center and stairs on each side leading up to it. On the platform is a sarcophagus containing a highly leveled draugr. If you have *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* installed, a series of flights of stairs to the west lead up to a word wall, which teaches a part of the [Drain Vitality](/wiki/Skyrim:Drain_Vitality "Skyrim:Drain Vitality") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

To the north are more flights of stairs rising up to another building. In front of the entrance, which is an open doorway, is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") from the entrance. The building is narrow, with two large openings on the other side and a stone table between them holding two random [potions of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka"), a random [potion of resist cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Cold "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Cold"), and a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons").

Upon exiting out the other side, another highly leveled draugr will burst from an upright sarcophagus which is against the side of the building and between the openings. To the west is a grave with a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plant beside it, and farther west is a third quicksilver ore vein on the ground. There are two more rows of graves opposite the building with several more nightshade plants.

To the east, you can see a tower with stairs leading up to it. Take care, as two more draugr are patrolling in front of this tower, and at higher levels both may use the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") dragon shout, which may knock you off the mountainside and can kill you. Inside, the tower is empty except for the top two floors. There is an unlocked boss-level chest on the floor just below the top floor. The top floor features a skeleton that you can loot in front of a pedestal holding a copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Withershins](/wiki/Skyrim:Withershins "Skyrim:Withershins")*.

## Notes

- The draugr in the sarcophagus past the small building containing traps can be unusually powerful relative to your level. For example, at level 15 you could find a Draugr Death Overlord here. In this case, the defeated enemy could drop an [ebony weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Weapons "Skyrim:Ebony Weapons"), making this spot useful for finding ebony weapons earlier in the game than they are generally accessible.
- There is little to no space for the dragon to land or crash at Arcwind Point itself. The dragon may fly over the mountain to the north to land.
- The tower containing *Withershins* can harbor additional enemies if the [Alternative Armors - Dragon Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragon_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragon Plate") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") is installed.
- Arcwind Point also [appears](/wiki/Online:Arcwind_Point "Online:Arcwind Point") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The dragon and the draugr here may be hostile to each other.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- Killing the dragon here does not mark the location as cleared, because it is not tagged as a boss.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- If sent here for the quest [The Words of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Words_of_Power "Skyrim:The Words of Power"), finding the word wall may not mark the quest as completed in your journal.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  -  Using the command `SetStage FreeFormHighHrothgarA 20` will end the quest and allow you to acquire another quest normally.
  - Going to [Northwind Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Summit "Skyrim:Northwind Summit") and collecting the shout there should complete the quest, but only if you haven't already learned that word, and you may be sent to Arcwind Point again in the future for The Words of Power since it won't be marked as cleared.
-  When visiting Arcwind Point the second time for the quest The Words of Power, the word wall chanting will be heard, but the wall will appear blank and no visual effect of learning a word will occur. Nevertheless, approaching the wall will teach you another word of the Drain Vitality shout.[*verification needed*]

Ardwen on her pilgrimage

**Ardwen** is a [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") pilgrim to the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") that can be [randomly encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Pilgrim_visiting_the_tree_in_Whiterun "Skyrim:World Interactions") with her [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog") after [The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature") is complete, if you restored the Gildergreen with sap. She does not appear if you completed the quest by bringing a sapling back. She will continue traveling from where you encounter her until she reaches [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

She is a respectable [elemental mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageElemental "Skyrim:CombatMageElemental"), able to cast a leveled selection of spells from the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction"), [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), and [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") schools. Her outfit consists of [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0006b46c "Skyrim:Boots").

## Related Quests

- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").

## Dialogue

If spoken to, she will tell you the reason for her journey:

:   *"We are traveling to [the Shrine of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth") in Whiterun. I hear the Gildergreen is more beautiful than ever since it's been restored. They say that eating the fruit it bears will add years to your life."*

## Notes

- If you follow her, she will eventually end up standing in front of the Gildergreen in Whiterun and will begin praying there.
- After completing her related quest, she will often just end up standing near the [Whiterun stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables") 24 hours a day. She can be engaged in conversation there, but will only say *"Hello"*, with no further dialogue available.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. Her random encounter quest will now terminate if she has arrived and you change locations to anywhere other than Whiterun.

## Overview

The corpse of the Arena Fan

The Arena Fan is a deceased [Bosmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") found at a camp southeast of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), southwest of [Geirmund's Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Geirmund%27s_Hall "Skyrim:Geirmund's Hall"), and northeast of [Honeystrand Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeystrand_Cave "Skyrim:Honeystrand Cave"). A [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Arena_Fan%27s_Note "Skyrim:Arena Fan's Note") is found on his body that details how he journeyed to Skyrim in search of a former Bloodletter of the [Imperial City](/wiki/Lore:Imperial_City "Lore:Imperial City") Arena, [Urgnok](/wiki/Skyrim:Urgnok "Skyrim:Urgnok").

He is garbed in simple [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006C1D8 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"). In addition to his aforementioned note, he also carries a copy of *[The Crimson Dirks, v8](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Crimson_Dirks,_v8 "Skyrim:The Crimson Dirks, v8")*.

## Related Quests

- **[Fan Favorite](/wiki/Skyrim:Fan_Favorite "Skyrim:Fan Favorite")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dwarven_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dwarven Mail"): Track down a fugitive Arena combatant.

## Notes

- He is a reference to the [Adoring Fan](/wiki/Oblivion:Adoring_Fan "Oblivion:Adoring Fan").

## Bugs

- The Arena Fan's corpse may despawn if you take too long to head to his camp. If the corpse despawns, it must be the case that the player unknowingly draws near enough to spawn the Arena Fan's corpse, then leaves away unknowingly too. In fact, several corpses in Skyrim may despawn accidently, it's a design flaw, these corpses should only be designed to despawn if the player interacts with them once. **?**

# Skyrim:Aretino Residence

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Aretino Residence ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Aretino+Residence)) | | |
