| Special Features | |
| [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") | [Danger](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Danger") Danger |

The Aretino Residence in Windhelm

The **Aretino Residence** is a house in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") owned by the Aretino family. After the death of Naalia Aretino, her son [Aventus](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") was sent to [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage") until his sixteenth birthday. However, Aventus ran away from the orphanage and returned home to perform the [Black Sacrament](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Kiss,_Sweet_Mother "Skyrim:A Kiss, Sweet Mother").

The house is found on the eastern side of Windhelm, above the Gray Quarter. The house is easy to spot, since its building has a curious shape, spanning over the road. It consists of one area, *[Aretino Residence](#Aretino_Residence)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") |

## Related Quests

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").

## Aretino Residence

Inside Aretino Residence

The front door opens to a set of stairs leading up, and you will hear [Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") chanting somewhere in the house. The first room is dimly lit and contains a non-respawning end table with some random books and a knocked-over bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on the floor. Along the southern wall sits a non-respawning dresser, with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a non-respawning food sack on top.

The neighboring room is lit up by numerous candles used by Aventus to perform the ritual. Next to the door is a respawning knapsack and a set of shelves with some [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), and a small bowl with [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"). Behind the shelves is a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Hypothetical Treachery](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Hypothetical_Treachery "Skyrim:A Hypothetical Treachery")*. Along the eastern wall is Aventus' owned bed and another non-respawning dresser with a bottle of alto wine on top. In the adjacent corner is a small dinner table with some food, a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), and a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). The unlit fireplace holds two pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") and a non-respawning pot. On the floor is a devastating [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_the_Steward "Skyrim:Letter from the Steward") written by [Jorleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorleif "Skyrim:Jorleif"), the personal steward of [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak").

The alcove

In the southern alcove sits Aventus, chanting the Black Sacrement over and over, frustrated that the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") doesn't hear his plea. For the ritual he has set up a number of candles, along with a chunk of [human flesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Flesh "Skyrim:Human Flesh") and a [human heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Heart "Skyrim:Human Heart"). The obligatory tome *[A Kiss, Sweet Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Kiss,_Sweet_Mother "Skyrim:A Kiss, Sweet Mother")* lies next to him, with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a sample of [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") on top. Talking to Aretino will trigger the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost").

## Notes

- When you first approach the house, you will overhear a conversation between [Idesa Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Idesa_Sadri "Skyrim:Idesa Sadri") and [Grimvar Cruel-Sea](/wiki/Skyrim:Grimvar_Cruel-Sea "Skyrim:Grimvar Cruel-Sea") about Aventus Aretino.
- There is a "Danger" shadowmark on the bottom of the arch in front of the house.
- As the house is scripted to reset, it provides a supply of both human hearts and flesh.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, addresses this issue. It removes the ritual items but the house still respawns.

## Bugs

- After completing the quest [Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost"), [Angrenor Once-Honored](/wiki/Skyrim:Angrenor_Once-Honored "Skyrim:Angrenor Once-Honored") carries around a key to the Aretino Residence. He should have moved into the house after the quest, but the scripting is incomplete.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.3, fixes this bug.

Argis the Bulwark

**Argis the Bulwark** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") living and working at [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). Once you have purchased the home and [attained](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:Thane of the Reach") the rank of [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") by completing quests issued by the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"), Argis is appointed to be your personal [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"). As such, he is not accessible until Vlindrel Hall has been purchased.

Argis wears a set of [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor"), a pair of [steel Nordic gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Nordic_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Nordic Gauntlets"), and a pair of [steel cuffed boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Cuffed_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Cuffed Boots"). He is equipped with a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") and a [steel shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield").

Argis can be asked to accompany you as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), a capacity in which he is rather useful. At level 50, Argis has 100 in Block, Heavy Armor, and One-handed, as well as 98 Archery and 72 Two-handed. He is also a potential candidate for [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").

## Related Quests

- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

## Notes

- Argis is the only housecarl who cannot become a [personal steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward").

A dead female Argonian

They also have a 50% chance of wearing a random hat (3 variants). They have a 25% chance of carrying a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and/or a small amount of gold.

# Skyrim:Argonian Ale Extraction

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **[Brenuin](/wiki/Skyrim:Brenuin "Skyrim:Brenuin") longs for the taste of [Argonian Ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale "Skyrim:Argonian Ale"). Can you steal some for him?** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Brenuin](/wiki/Skyrim:Brenuin "Skyrim:Brenuin") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun's](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") streets, [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") |
| Reward: | [Potion of Vigorous Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigorous_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Vigorous Healing") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 (Brenuin) |
| ID: | FreeformWhiterunQuest02 |

The bottle of Argonian Ale

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Meet [Brenuin](/wiki/Skyrim:Brenuin "Skyrim:Brenuin") on the streets of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
2. Go to [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") and acquire the [Argonian Ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale "Skyrim:Argonian Ale").
3. Return to Brenuin to be rewarded.

## Detailed Walkthrough

After you give [Brenuin](/wiki/Skyrim:Brenuin "Skyrim:Brenuin") a gold coin on the streets of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), the option to ask him if he is always drunk will become available. Ask him, and he will reply *"Only if I can help it."* He then asks you to bring him a special bottle of ale: *"In [the Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare"), there's this bottle of [Argonian Ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ale "Skyrim:Argonian Ale"). The good stuff. Get it for me."*

The inn is in the market area of Whiterun's Plains District, where Brenuin usually pesters the stall owners outside the inn or customers inside. The ale is in the inn's kitchen (to the left from the main entrance), on the cupboard opposite the [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot").

After acquiring the ale, return to Brenuin. He will thank you and reward you with a [Potion of Vigorous Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigorous_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Vigorous Healing") that he had recently "obtained" from the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth"), or as he puts it: *"I, er, "found" it in the temple."*

## Notes

- You can refuse to feed his habit when he asks you to steal the ale, though this does not lock you out of the quest as the option still remains to discuss his sobriety later.
- Alternatively, the ale can be obtained by raising the disposition of the innkeeper [Hulda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hulda "Skyrim:Hulda"). This can be done by chopping wood outside the inn and selling it to her. Her disposition will then be high enough that she allows you to take low-value items from the inn without it being theft. This includes the bottle of Argonian Ale. The amount of wood given to Hulda does not matter; her disposition will be raised even if you sold just one piece.

## Quest Stages

| Argonian Ale Extraction (FreeformWhiterunQuest02) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Steal the Argonian Ale |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Give the Argonian Ale to Brenuin |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255, 500.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformWhiterunQuest02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformWhiterunQuest02`.

# Skyrim:Argonian Assemblage

## Overview

:   *"They must remain outside, for their own safety."* —[Jarl Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter")

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Argonian Assemblage ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Argonian+Assemblage)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | |

| Special Features | |

| # of [Workbenches](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") | 1 |
| [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") | [Empty](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Empty") Empty |

Argonian Assemblage

The **Argonian Assemblage** is the building on the docks of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") in which all the [Argonian](/wiki/Lore:Argonian "Lore:Argonian") dockworkers are forced to live.

It is located west of the stairs leading from the docks up to the city of Windhelm and to the east is the [office](/wiki/Skyrim:Clan_Shatter-Shield_Office "Skyrim:Clan Shatter-Shield Office") of clan Shatter-Shield.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Neetrenaza](/wiki/Skyrim:Neetrenaza "Skyrim:Neetrenaza")  [Scouts-Many-Marshes](/wiki/Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes "Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes") [Trainer (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Common)")[Light Armor (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Light Armor (Common)")  [Shahvee](/wiki/Skyrim:Shahvee "Skyrim:Shahvee")  [Stands-In-Shallows](/wiki/Skyrim:Stands-In-Shallows "Skyrim:Stands-In-Shallows") |

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout.
- **[A Few Words with You](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Few_Words_with_You "Skyrim:A Few Words with You")**: Do a favor by talking to someone about a problem.
- **[Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft")**: Do a favor by stealing an item.

## Exterior

Outside of the assemblage is Windhelm's docks where, during the day, the occupants of the assemblage work; no matter the weather conditions. To the northeast of the door is a wooden rack holding seven [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Salmon_.28dead.29 "Skyrim:Passive Creatures") that can be freely harvested. On the docks there is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") available for you to use.

## Argonian Assemblage

Inside the Argonian Assemblage

Both inside and out, the Argonian Assemblage is dark and in disrepair; a perfect place for the prejudiced and proud [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") to keep their unwanted Argonian workers. The dockworkers retire at the end of the work day to their shared living quarters. Inside, there is not much to look at. Cobwebs hang from the ceiling, and a dull fire burns under empty cooking pots. There are four beds, one for each resident of the assemblage.

There are several round wooden pillars supporting the high ceiling around the room. On your left as soon as you enter is a round wooden table. Against the west wall is a cupboard holding a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") and bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). A dresser to the right holds a copy of the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(book) "Skyrim:Thief (book)")*, and a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") on top. There is a second dresser further to the right with two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") on top and a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") and chair beside it. Against the north wall is a tall wardrobe. Both this and the dressers all contain various items of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"). There are several crates further along the wall. Next to these is an alcove containing a square table and two chairs with a bottle of wine, a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and a couple of wedges of cheese on top and an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie") on the floor underneath. More crates are to the right of the table with a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") on top of one of them, containing leveled items.

Along the east wall is a long fire pit with several unusable pots hanging over it, a bottle of wine on the floor to the left, a cast iron pot containing three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") on the right-hand edge of the surround, and two pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") to the right of the pit. In front of it is a long wooden table and bench with a bottle of wine, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a loaf of bread, a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), and a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") all on top. There are also several unusable barrels in the southeastern corner.

There are four beds in a row to the left of the middle of the room; each bed has an end table either at the head or foot of it. The third has a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top and the fourth has a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat") on top.

## Notes

- Because the master-level lock on the entrance door resets often, it seems [Scouts-Many-Marshes](/wiki/Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes "Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes") and [Stands-In-Shallows](/wiki/Skyrim:Stands-In-Shallows "Skyrim:Stands-In-Shallows") become trapped inside after turning in for the night, and cannot come out the next day unless the door is unlocked by you.
- Even if you are an Argonian, you will still receive a bounty for trespassing unless you are married to one of the residents.
- There is an  "Empty") Empty [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the bottom left of the entrance door.
- Three of the four reptilian residents offer quests.
- The cupboard and the sack on its upper shelf, the four end tables, the two dressers, and the wardrobe are non-respawning. Consequently, they are safe storage. The small sack, and the knapsack are not safe.

# Skyrim:Ari

## Overview

| Ari (RefID: 000411CD) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000411CD | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000411CF |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 25 |
| Voice Type | [FemaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [BanditFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:BanditFaction "Skyrim:BanditFaction") | | |

Ari's corpse

**Ari** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") that was killed by [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") when her party chased a [bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") sow into [Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern"). After [Niels](/wiki/Skyrim:Niels "Skyrim:Niels") was ambushed and almost instantly killed, she took off running before being overcome. The only survivor of their party was [Valdr](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdr "Skyrim:Valdr") who requests that you help avenge his fallen comrades. If you help Valdr, he will bury Ari's corpse.

Ari wears [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor_(item) "Skyrim:Light Armor (item)") (either [fur](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), [hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), or [studded](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Armor")), with either [fur shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Shoes "Skyrim:Fur Shoes") or [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"), and a 50% chance of a pair of bracers (either [fur](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Bracers "Skyrim:Fur Bracers") or [hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers")). She carries a [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons") (either [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") or [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel")) with a 20% chance of a shield (either [hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield") or [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield")), along with a small amount of gold. She may also carry other minor items and loot.

## Related Quests

- **[Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern_(quest) "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern (quest)")**: Help an [injured hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdr "Skyrim:Valdr") avenge his fallen companions.

# Skyrim:Aringoth

## Overview

| Aringoth (RefID: 00019E13) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Goldenglow Estate Second Floor](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate") | | |
| Race | [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") | Gender | Male |
| Level | PC×1 (range=8-20) | Class | [Ranger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranger_(class) "Skyrim:Ranger (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00019E13 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001334A |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50+(PC-1)×10 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50+(PC-1)×5 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery")**, **[Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor")**, [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleElfHaughty](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleElfHaughty "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleElfHaughty") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [FavorExcludedFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction "Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction"); [Goldenglow Estate Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate_Faction "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate Faction"); [TG02 Aringoth Player Neutral Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:TG02_Aringoth_Player_Neutral_Faction "Skyrim:TG02 Aringoth Player Neutral Faction") | | |

Aringoth in the Goldenglow Estate

**Aringoth** is the [Altmer](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") owner of [Goldenglow Estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate"), a bee farm outside of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") which used to supply [honey](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey "Skyrim:Honey") to the [Black-Briar Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery"). The [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") made sure the operations ran smoothly and would extort considerable payment from Aringoth. Lately, he has stopped shipments, fortified the island and hired an army of mercenaries, infuriating [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") and causing the Guild to single him out for punishment.

Befitting his status, Aringoth wears [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#00086991 "Skyrim:Clothing") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#00086993 "Skyrim:Clothing"). He is armed with a leveled dagger, leveled bow, and up to 144 arrows of various qualities up to daedric, all limited by your level. He also carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Cellar_Key "Skyrim:Goldenglow Cellar Key") to his cellar, a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Safe_Key "Skyrim:Goldenglow Safe Key") to his safe and up to 45 gold coins.

## Related Quests

- **[Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear")**: Send a message to a former [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") client.

### Loud and Clear

Once you've broken into the estate, Aringoth will be found crouching in his room on the second floor. As soon as you come close he'll spit:

:   *"Worthless mercenaries. I didn't think Maven or [Mercer](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey") would allow me to get away with this, but I had little choice."*
:   **I just want the key to your safe.**
:   *"I can't. If I do, I may as well cut my own throat."*

:   :   **What makes you think I won't? (Persuade)**

        :   *"Fine. Take it! Once the new owner finds out I gave in, I'm as good as dead anyway."* (Success)
        :   *"I don't believe you. That's not your way."* (Fail)

:   :   :   :   **New owner? What are you talking about?**
            :   *"I've already said too much. I gave you what you came here for, now go. Leave me in peace."*

:   :   **Then I'll take it off your corpse!**

        :   *"Give it your best shot!"*

:   :   **Forget it. I'll just open it myself.**

        :   *"No! I'm not about to let you ruin everything I've worked so hard for!"*

If spoken to again if you got the key from him peacefully:

:   *"Go, leave me in peace."*

## Notes

- If left alive, he will remain crouched in the corner for the rest of the game.

## Bugs

- Aringoth was intended to be a [Bosmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf"), as [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf"), [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex"), and Mercer Frey all refer to him as a Wood Elf.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Arivanya

## Overview

| Arivanya (RefID: 0001B144) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | | |
| House | [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables") | | |
| Race | [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 4 | Class | [Bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard_(class) "Skyrim:Bard (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001B144 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00014127 |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionEastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch "Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch"); [TownWindhelmFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownWindhelmFaction "Skyrim:TownWindhelmFaction"); [WindhelmCandlehearthPatrons](/wiki/Skyrim:WindhelmCandlehearthPatrons "Skyrim:WindhelmCandlehearthPatrons"); [WindhelmStablesFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:WindhelmStablesFaction "Skyrim:WindhelmStablesFaction") | | |

Arivanya

*"No! Someone help me! Please!"*

**Arivanya** is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard_(class) "Skyrim:Bard (class)") who is married to [Ulundil](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulundil "Skyrim:Ulundil") and lives with him at the [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables"). She takes over selling the stables' horses if anything happens to her husband, even though she constantly tells everyone how much she dislikes horses.

To get away from the stables and their stench she frequently heads to town, where she can be found in [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") or the [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub").

She can be killed during the quest by [Calixto Corrium](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto_Corrium "Skyrim:Calixto Corrium"), however it can be prevented by choosing to talk to [Wuunferth the Unliving](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving") before [Jorleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorleif "Skyrim:Jorleif"). If killed by Calixto, her body can be found outside [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall").

Arivanya wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0003452e "Skyrim:Clothing") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0003452f "Skyrim:Clothing"). She wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables_Key "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables Key") to the stables along with a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") is plagued by a shadowy killer.

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

When spoken to she can say:

:   *"Horses. All day long. Do you have any idea how dull horses are?"*
:   *"Ugh. I'll need to bathe thoroughly to get this stench off of me."*
:   *"I love my husband, but he can be a bit... dull at times."*

If you have not completed [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice"), she will comment about the Butcher:

:   *"If the guards would listen to [Viola](/wiki/Skyrim:Viola_Giordano "Skyrim:Viola Giordano"), they'd have caught the Butcher by now."*

## Notes

- It's possible that Arivanya was at one point meant to be the bard at Candlehearth Hall. She's in the bard class and has the same voice type as the bard who's there in the final game, [Luaffyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Luaffyn "Skyrim:Luaffyn"). Luaffyn was also created much later than most of the city's residents and appears to be a very rudimentary NPC, while Arivanya was created alongside them and is more fleshed out. She also has a couple of notable quirks unbefitting her role as stablehand. She doesn't have any scenes set up with her husband, spends the majority of her time away from the stables (she is the only stablehand in the game besides [Shadr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadr "Skyrim:Shadr") to exhibit such behavior), is marked as friends with Viola Giordano and [Tova Shatter-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Tova_Shatter-Shield "Skyrim:Tova Shatter-Shield"), two women who are tied to the butcher investigation, she also mentions the former in dialogue, and can even fall victim to the killer herself. This all seems to imply that at the very least, Arivanya originally had some kind of bigger role in the quest.
- When [Susanna](/wiki/Skyrim:Susanna_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Susanna the Wicked") is killed by the Butcher, she gets distinctive wounds all over her body. Arivanya does not get any such markings when she is killed, however, she was very likely intended to. An unused "outfit" bearing Arivanya's name has similar wounds, and also follows the naming scheme of Susanna's.
  -  Version 1.2.4 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") makes it so the unused outfit gets used when Arivanya is killed, making her appear with the distinctive markings as well.

## Bugs

- Arivanya has AI packages to spend time at both Candlehearth Hall and the New Gnisis Cornerclub, but she was never added to the cornerclub faction.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.

## Overview

Arkngthamz

**Arkngthamz** is a small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") southeast of [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal") containing [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). It contains only one zone, *[Arkngthamz](#Arkngthamz)*.

A map marker for the location will be added by reading the book *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*, giving you a miscellaneous objective to investigate the ruins. Copies of this book can be found in several places, but the copy on the [adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Adventurer "Skyrim:Adventurer")'s body near the entrance to [Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft") is a quest item which will make additional copies of the book be treated as quest items until you read the journal found in Arkngthamz. The copy on the body of the conjurer adventurer near [Deep Folk Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Deep_Folk_Crossing "Skyrim:Deep Folk Crossing") may also be a quest item.

## Related Quests

- **[Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages")**: Search for the Dwemer's [Aetherium Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Forge "Skyrim:The Aetherium Forge").

### Exterior

There is a path heading east from the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") of [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal") that passes Arkngthamz. Several wild [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") can be found in the region, including one that is usually very near to the entrance. Many [juniper trees](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") grow throughout the surrounding area. You may notice the ground shaking when nearing the ruins. These tremors continue inside the ruins as well. As noted by [Katria](/wiki/Skyrim:Katria "Skyrim:Katria"), some of the dangers present in Arkngthamz include major earthquakes, massive chasms, and unstable ground. The ruins have suffered greatly from these.

### Arkngthamz

Arkngthamz interior

The entrance leads directly into a passage heading north. As you proceed, you will hear Katria telling you to turn back. At the end, a fallen pillar provides a ramp down into a narrow chamber with a stream fed by a waterfall on your right flowing through it. Beneath the pillar, you'll find the remains of a [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider"), and the first of many [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") found throughout these ruins. At the bottom of the pillar, a large doorway leads into a passage that turns east after a few more paces. There are several pillars along this passage that have been damaged by earthquakes, making the floor uneven with rubble, among which are the remains of a [Dwarven sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere"). As you follow this passage, you will again hear Katria warning you to turn back.

The passage opens into a huge open-roofed chamber with large ledges split by a fast-moving river below. The opposite ledge is above the level of the near ledge, and has some Falmer fencing along part of the edge. This side is fairly empty and open, with stairs to your right leading up to a platform with the remains of another Dwarven spider at the far end. From the edge of the open area, you can see some masonry where possibly a bridge has fallen. The only way forward is a stone pillar that has fallen and is leaning against this edge, leading down to the top of an earthen column with a dead body on top. There is a large waterfall to the left, and the water runs under the wall to the right. The dead body turns out to be Katria, who died in a fall from a ledge far above, and whose ghost appears next to you shortly after you first enter these ruins. As you approach her body, Katria will tell you to retrieve her [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Katria%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Katria's Journal") from her corpse. The journal provides more info regarding the site, the forge, and other important sites, and at the back, a few hints regarding a tonal lock. Once you read the journal, copies of *The Aetherium Wars* are no longer classed as quest items, and thus can be dropped and weigh the same as normal books. From here, you can follow a broken pipe down to the water. The current flows northwest to a ledge which contains the remains of a Dwarven spider and sphere. On the west side of the water, a ramp heads south past the body of a dead Falmer up to a dead end with an unlocked Dwarven [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Returning to Katria's body, cross another pipe to a small tunnel. Lying at the end of the small tunnel is another dead Falmer, while beneath the grating used as flooring is a small space you can drop down into to find two [Dwarven metal ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Metal_Ingot "Skyrim:Dwarven Metal Ingot") and a [centurion dynamo core](/wiki/Skyrim:Centurion_Dynamo_Core "Skyrim:Centurion Dynamo Core"). Walk back up the pipe and follow the small tunnel past the dead Falmer, where two leveled Dwarven spiders will drop from a [Dwarven scuttle](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Scuttle "Skyrim:Dwarven Scuttle") and attack. At the far end is a completely flooded room with pipes above. The remains of another Dwarven sphere are directly ahead. Under the water in the northeastern corner is an unlocked Dwarven chest. A pipe can be climbed and followed up and around to a passage in the northwestern corner. Any [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), including Katria, may be reluctant to make the short drop to the area beyond the fence at the end of the pipe. However, the "wait" command can resolve this for most followers, while the next time Katria speaks, she will reappear beside you regardless.

At the end of the passage is a metal gate that keeps opening and closing as a tonal lock keeps rising and falling. Around the corner is a second tonal lock by a closed gate. You can activate a tonal lock by casting a ranged spell or hitting it with a melee or ranged weapon. Strike the second tonal lock to open the second gate. Striking the first tonal lock will cause it to stop falling, which will stop the gate from closing and end the clanging noise. Beyond the gate is a flight of stairs leading up to a passage that is off-kilter. Around a corner is another flight of stairs, with a Falmer patrolling the area. As you continue, if Katria is with you, she may warn you about Falmer before they can see you. The stairs lead up to the far side of the huge chamber split by the fast-flowing river. You come out at the top of stairs leading down. There is a second Falmer patrolling across the top of the stairs, and a Falmer tent to the right containing an unlocked Falmer chest. Another leveled Falmer can be seen wandering to the left of the tent, overlooking the drop below. There are the bodies of two further dead Falmer in this area that can be looted. Following the front edge back to the north, at the far end of a narrow ledge is an unlocked Dwarven chest.

There is a path heading up past the tent to the south before crossing over the river to the east then following the wall farther to the south. There are several glowing mushrooms found growing on the walls, and the occasional [Falmer hive](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Hive "Skyrim:Falmer Hive") with Falmer that drop from them as you approach. After the first set of hives, a bridge formed by another stone pillar crosses to the north. South of the bridge is a closed Dwarven metal gate; as you approach, Katria will exclaim *"Look, there's a chest in there. Door's sealed tight, though..."*. The gate cannot be opened from this side. Instead of crossing the bridge, if you walk to the end of the ledge on this side and look below, you will see a couple of ledges that step down to a ramp leading up from the water. Either jump into the water or use the ledges to drop to a tunnel with water streaming out of it below. Entering this tunnel leads to an area with a lot of vegetation, including several [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing off the edge of an earthen ramp that leads up and around to where the water exits under the rock. At the end of the stream are the remains of a [Dwarven centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion"), and to the right up the ramp by a broken pipe are those of a Dwarven spider. At the top of the ramp is a Dwarven scuttle, from which emerges a leveled Dwarven sphere. Once the sphere is dispatched, keep climbing the ramp to the unlocked Dwarven chest Katria originally saw behind the closed gate. A lever that opens the gate is to the right of the gate. Note it's best to instruct followers to wait before dropping down. Also, when opening the gate, Katria can get stuck; closing and reopening the gate resolves this.

Now cross the bridge to the north; the path on the far side continues left and right. To the right is another Falmer hive containing a Falmer, unless you've already faced it, and shortly after a dead end. To the left the path continues to climb before again crossing the chamber and the water below. On the far side is another leveled Falmer and possibly a chaurus. The path then turns a corner and splits, with the left-hand side continuing up, and the right-hand side descending; under the path that descends is an unlocked Falmer chest. The chamber is tall, circular, and flooded with deep water. Under the water to the west is a small submerged tunnel that leads to a hidden chamber containing an unlocked wooden chest, a random one-handed weapon and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), two [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") (one large and one small), a total of twelve loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and a lootable skeleton.

Following the left-hand path and continuing to climb, the path soon crosses the chamber one final time before entering a tunnel heading northeast, with many glowing mushrooms by the mouth of the tunnel. After a short distance, the passage turns to the northwest, then enters another chamber containing a Falmer tent and two Falmer hives. There is a chaurus or [chaurus hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter") in front of you, and a leveled Falmer at the top of a ramp, off to the right. Inside the tent is an unlocked Falmer chest. In the rear corner of the room is a pen containing another chaurus or chaurus hunter, and in front of the pen a Falmer gated tunnel heading southwest. There are a few chaurus egg sacs along this tunnel, which leads to another chamber containing two more chaurus or chaurus hunters and several more egg sacs. A ramp at the rear of this chamber leads to another tunnel, with water rushing along it before pouring out as a waterfall at the end into the chamber with the deep water previously passed. There is a small ledge to the left of the waterfall with an unlocked Falmer chest on it, and a Falmer hive above containing a Falmer that drops down and attacks. There is another ledge below to the right which you can jump down to (you may suffer minor damage), and from there another tunnel with a waterfall coming out of it to the right. At the far end of this tunnel is a veil of water, behind which is another unlocked Falmer chest. From this tunnel, your only option is to drop to the deep water below and retrace your steps back up to the chamber containing the Falmer tent and chaurus, then follow the ascending ramp at the back.

Climbing the ramp leads to a tunnel heading northeast to the huge open-roofed chamber, far above where you originally entered it. There are trees and vegetation all around, but no further Falmer, chaurus, or automations (except those released for incorrect puzzle attempts). As you enter, Katria will comment *"Here's where I fell. Feels like ages ago."* and then exclaim *"Hey, there's my bow! There, out on the log. Wondered what happened to it."* Hanging off the end of a large tree trunk hanging over the edge of the ledge opposite is her unique [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") [Zephyr](/wiki/Skyrim:Zephyr "Skyrim:Zephyr"), which fires 30% faster than standard bows. Once you retrieve it, Katria asks you to *"Take good care of it for me."* There is an earthen ramp at the rear of the chamber, which leads to another ramp that continues to climb before reaching a stone square arch. Beyond the arch is a ledge that descends into the final chamber.

As you approach the first stone arch in this room, if you look to your left, you will see another stone arch on a lower level with a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), a large coin purse, and an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") on top of it; you can jump to this arch and collect the loot. Under the skeleton is also an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"). Before this, on a ledge that you can drop to below the entrance to this chamber is an [ebony ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Ebony Ore Vein"); the ledge can more easily be seen from the roof of the building in the wall to your left as you enter. Continuing down the ramp to the other end of the chamber, there is another ledge with a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") that you can drop to. A careful jump along the wall just past this ore vein will allow you to reach another small ledge with a Dwarven chest, but you cannot interact with it. There is another ebony ore vein near the quicksilver vein, which you can reach from the floor of the chamber. This room has many Falmer hives on the walls, but they seem to contain no Falmer. There are a total of five skeletons in the room in the area near the tonal lock puzzle, four of which can be looted for a few coins, the remains of a Dwarven sphere, and the body of a dead adventurer, with many [Dwarven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow") piercing the corpse and on the ground nearby. The dead adventurer is carrying a [scrap of paper](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrap_of_Paper "Skyrim:Scrap of Paper") that provides more clues to the correct order for the tonal locks; these supplement the clues contained in Katria's journal. There is a stone square arch leaning over nearby, with the fifth skeleton pierced by a huge ballista bolt (the bones may have fallen in a heap, and in any case can not be interacted with). Using the nearby earthen ramp and column, it is possible to jump atop the leaning arch, and from there reach a ledge behind a vertical brass pipe against the wall; another unlocked Dwarven chest is behind this pipe.

The five kinetic resonators

To get to the treasures, including the [Aetherium Shard](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherium_Shard "Skyrim:Aetherium Shard"), you must strike the five [kinetic resonators](/wiki/Skyrim:Kinetic_Resonator "Skyrim:Kinetic Resonator") in the correct order with ranged attacks to trigger the tonal locks. If you hit the resonators in the wrong order, the ports on the front of the structure will release four Dwarven spiders the first time, two Dwarven spheres the second time, and a Dwarven centurion (which emerges from its dock hidden behind the middle gate) the third or fourth time. After the Dwarven centurion, there will be no more enemies released for incorrect attempts, but the [Dwemer ballista](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwemer Ballista") at the top of the structure will briefly rain down bolts after each wrong answer that does not release an enemy. You can avoid the bolts by hugging the structure. The correct answer is: **lower left, lower right, upper left, upper right, lower middle**. This will open both outer gates. Once the outer gates have been opened, you cannot get the Dwarven automatons released.

Follow the tunnel through either door, and you will see the Aetherium Shard. There is a Dwarven boss chest behind the shard and two further Dwarven chests, one each on the walls to either side. All three chests are unlocked. To either side of the shard are sets of shelves containing various Dwemer metal items, Dwarven metal ingots, and two centurion dynamo cores. After you collect the loot, head for the water in the west side of the chamber, and take the tunnel there for a shortcut back to a ledge in the main chamber. Save before taking the long drop to the water, though, as you or any followers could easily die if you or they hit the rocks at the end of the pool or another hard surface. Finally, backtrack to the entrance, and exit the ruins.

## Notes

- Enemies' corpses in Arkngthamz never disappear.

## Bugs

- Although Arkngthamz is geographically located within the borders of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), in the game data it is identified as being within [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
- Although the zone flag suggests the location is clearable, there is no boss defined and no call to `SetCleared()`.
  - Killing all enemies in the ruin and setting off all traps in the tonal lock room will mark the dungeon as "cleared".
  -  Killing all enemies in the ruin without activating the traps and entering the console command `killall` will mark the dungeon as "cleared".

## Maps

- 

  Arkngthamz

# Skyrim:Armor

## Overview

This article is about the type of apparel. For the magic effect, see [Armor (effect)](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_(effect) "Skyrim:Armor (effect)"). For the spells, see [Armor (spells)](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_(spells) "Skyrim:Armor (spells)").

**Armor** is a type of apparel that is worn on the body to reduce damage from attacks. Armor comes in two varieties, corresponding to the two different skills governing armor usage: [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") and [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor"). In addition, there are shields which provide an additional passive increase to armor rating (active blocking is governed by the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") skill).

Armor comes in several pieces which can be equipped independently of each other. These pieces are:

- **Armor**: covers your legs, chest and shoulders
- **Boots**: covers your feet and ankles
- **Gauntlets**: covers your hands up to your elbow
- **Helmet**: covers your head
- **Shield**: protect and block attacks

The [Divine Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Divine_Crusader "Skyrim:Divine Crusader") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") adds an additional type of armor: the [Fastened Shield of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Fastened_Shield_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Fastened Shield of the Crusader"), which is a **Shoulder** piece.

In addition to standard pieces of armor, two necklaces in the game provide an armor bonus: the [Locket of Saint Jiub](/wiki/Skyrim:Locket_of_Saint_Jiub "Skyrim:Locket of Saint Jiub")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), and the [Amulet of Articulation](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Articulation "Skyrim:Amulet of Articulation").

## Armor Materials

Armor appears in several different materials and styles, which determine the quality of the armor. Higher quality armor provides better protection (but is generally heavier). Which quality armor you will find is generally determined based on your character's level.

The following tables describe the *base* level at which an armor type begins to show up randomly for the player. Lower level armor will also randomly appear, but so will higher level armors in certain situations: potentially up to at least 12 levels "early". Enchanted versions of each armor type will begin to appear one level later; see [Generic Magic Apparel](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel") for more information. See [Leveled Lists](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") for details on how these lists are used to determine the probabilities of individual items appearing. Although [Dragonscale](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonscale_Armor "Skyrim:Dragonscale Armor"), [Dragonplate](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonplate_Armor "Skyrim:Dragonplate Armor"), and [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Armor") armors can all be found in random loot, once your level is high enough, the chances of finding any of these armor types is 20 times less than finding other armor types.

Most armor from the list below can be created at [Forges](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), by using the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") skill. The ability to make armor is not dependent upon your character's level, but is instead dependent upon which Smithing perks you have unlocked. All standard armor can also be tempered at [Workbenches](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), if you have the necessary auxiliary item. Tempering is twice as effective if you have unlocked the perk necessary to forge that armor. Tempering an enchanted version of the armor (whether custom-[enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting"), or [generic](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel")) is similar to tempering the base version - it requires the same auxiliary item, and is twice as effective if you have unlocked the forging perk - but also requires the [Arcane Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Blacksmith "Skyrim:Arcane Blacksmith") perk to be unlocked.

Jewelry (specifically, [amulets/necklaces](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet "Skyrim:Amulet") and [rings](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring "Skyrim:Ring")), can be created at any blacksmith's forge from ingots and jewels, but these are not counted as protective armor (the two exceptions to this are noted in the section above); similarly, [circlets/crowns](/wiki/Skyrim:Circlet "Skyrim:Circlet") - like common [clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing") - have no armor/protection value and cannot be crafted. The [Aetherial Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Aetherial_Crown "Skyrim:Aetherial Crown"), which is a unique, [quest-related](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages"), crafted item (added by the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") add-on), unlike other jewelry items, is eligible for improvement by ordinary [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing"), but still only ever bears an armor rating of 0.

The [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge") allows you to create [Ancient Nord armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Armor "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Armor"), a type of heavy armor, if you finish the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") questline. Also, it may be found from level 1 onward in a few locations. Additionally, there are several other wearable armor sets/pieces that are made available as [loot/specialty gear](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") or as [unique/quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Unique_Items "Skyrim:Unique Items") items; generally, these can all be improved by [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") and possibly fortified with [enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchantments "Skyrim:Enchantments") (if not enchanted already), though they cannot be forged as player-created items. (*See also:* [Magic Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Items "Skyrim:Magic Items") and [Artifacts](/wiki/Skyrim:Artifacts "Skyrim:Artifacts"))

The [Dragonborn add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") adds craftable [Bonemold](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold "Skyrim:Bonemold") (heavy), [Chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Chitin "Skyrim:Chitin") (light/heavy), [Nordic Carved](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic "Skyrim:Nordic") (heavy), and [Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") (light/heavy) armors.

The [Dawnguard add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") adds  [2 generic Falmer armors](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Equipment "Skyrim:Falmer Equipment") (heavy) and [Vampire armors](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Armor "Skyrim:Vampire Armor") (light), which may be worn/improved but cannot be forged by the player.

[Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") by Material (Numerical Values are for a full, matched suit)

[^](#note_No_Shield)Those armors sets have no matching shield so they are given one of the same material, if any available

[^^](#note_studded)Studded armor only comes in a cuirass, so there is no studded suit - the values listed here pair it with a hide suit.

[^^^](#note_vampire)Vampire armor has no helmet.

[^^^^](#note_bonemold)Improved Bonemold equipment must be made - it will not be randomly found.

[†](#note_Dragonplate)Dragonplate Cuirasses and Shields are tempered using Dragon Bone; all other Dragonplate armor is improved using Dragon Scales.

[††](#note_Stahlrim)Forging Stalhrim armor also requires completion of the quest [A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim").

[‡](#note_Daedric)All Daedric armor can also be made at the [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge") (except the boots, see [Atronach Forge bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge#Bugs "Skyrim:Atronach Forge")), in which case the Daedric Smithing perk is not needed, but instead the [Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Sigil Stone") must be obtained. Tempering armor created at the Atronach Forge is still augmented by the Daedric Smithing perk.

[‡‡](#note_AncientNord) Version 1.2.7 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") moves the Ancient Nord armor to the "Steel" category, and makes it require [Steel Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Smithing "Skyrim:Steel Smithing") to forge.

## Armor Rating

Armor Ratios

For all of the armor listed on this site, the provided armor ratings are the **base armor ratings**. The actual protection your character will receive from the armor is dependent upon your skill in that armor type and any relevant perks that you have unlocked. The rating can also be improved by using [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") to change the armor's quality to "Fine", "Superior", "Exquisite", "Flawless", "Epic", or "Legendary".

The armor rating only reduces physical damage, not magical damage. Each point of armor rating reduces damage by 0.12%.

**Approximate formulas**:

- *Item Armor rating* = CEILING[ (*base armor rating* + *item quality*) × (1 + 0.4 × (*skill* + *skill effect*)/100) ] × (1 + *unison perk*† ) × (1 + *[Matching Set](/wiki/Skyrim:Matching_Set "Skyrim:Matching Set")*) × (1 + *armor perk*‡)
- *Shield rating* = CEILING[ (*base shield rating* + *item quality*) × (1 + 0.4 × (*skill* + *skill effect*)/100) ] × (1 + *unison perk*† ) × (1 + *[Matching Set](/wiki/Skyrim:Matching_Set "Skyrim:Matching Set")*)
- *Displayed armor rating* = SUM(*item armor rating*) + *shield rating* + *armor effects*
- *Base damage reduction of 3% per piece worn* = Hidden armor rating of 25 per piece worn, including shields
- *Damage reduction percentage* = *displayed armor rating* × 0.12 + (3.00 × *number of pieces worn).*

† [Custom Fit](/wiki/Skyrim:Custom_Fit "Skyrim:Custom Fit") for light armor or [Well Fitted](/wiki/Skyrim:Well_Fitted "Skyrim:Well Fitted") for heavy armor
‡ [Agile Defender](/wiki/Skyrim:Agile_Defender "Skyrim:Agile Defender") for light armor or [Juggernaut](/wiki/Skyrim:Juggernaut "Skyrim:Juggernaut") for heavy armor

Clothing and robes do not benefit from the hidden armor rating bonus.

For NPCs the skill coefficient is 1.5 instead of 0.4, and 1.25 ^ 2 (1.5625) instead of 1.25 for Custom Fit.

Note the difference between *skill* effects (e.g. Fortify Light/Heavy Armor equipment, [Ancient Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Knowledge "Skyrim:Ancient Knowledge")) and *armor* effects (e.g. [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh"), [The Lord Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lord_Stone "Skyrim:The Lord Stone")).

Your durability against physical attacks (i.e. the amount of raw damage you can sustain) is proportional to 100/(100 − damage reduction percentage). This results in hyperbolic growth in your physical durability, up to the cap of 80% damage reduction giving a ×5 multiplier to your physical durability. Thus, the more armor rating you have, the more each additional point of armor rating is worth. The graph displayed shows the multiplier to your physical durability relative to no armor based on the displayed armor rating, assuming you are wearing all four pieces of armor (+12% hidden damage reduction) and have no other effects.

### Armor Rating Example

- Dragonscale Armor
- Dragonscale Boots
- Dragonscale Gauntlets
- Dragonscale Helmet
- Dragonscale Shield
- 100 Light Armor Skill
- 100 Smithing Skill (*item quality bonus* of +20 or +10)
- 5/5 [Agile Defender](/wiki/Skyrim:Agile_Defender "Skyrim:Agile Defender")
- [Custom Fit](/wiki/Skyrim:Custom_Fit "Skyrim:Custom Fit")
- [Matching Set](/wiki/Skyrim:Matching_Set "Skyrim:Matching Set")

*Dragonscale Armor rating*

- CEILING [(41 + 20) \* (1 + 0.4 \* (100/100))] \* 1.25 \* 1.25 \* 2
- = 86 \* 1.25 \* 1.25 \* 2
- = 268.75

*Dragonscale Helmet rating*

- CEILING [ (17 + 10) \* (1 + 0.4 \* (100/100)) ] \* 1.25 \* 1.25 \* 2
- = 118.75

*Dragonscale Boots rating* & *Dragonscale Gauntlets rating*

- CEILING [ (12 + 10) \* (1 + 0.4 \* (100/100)) ] \* 1.25 \* 1.25 \* 2
- = 96.875

*Dragonscale Shield rating*

- CEILING [ (29 + 10) \* (1 + 0.4 \* (100/100)) ] \* 1.25 \* 1.25
- = 85.9375

*Displayed armor rating*

- 268.75 + 118.75 + 96.875 + 96.875 + 85.9375
- = 667.1875

## Armor Cap

Regardless of your displayed armor rating you can never exceed an 80% physical damage reduction, the **armor cap**. You'll reach the armor cap at 542 displayed armor rating when wearing all four pieces of armor and a shield, 567 without a shield, or 667 when not wearing any armor or shield at all. There are a few different ways you can reach this cap:

**Light / Heavy armor skills only**

Let's say you have 100 armor skill and *all* relevant armor perks acquired and active (i.e. you're wearing a matched set of all light or all heavy armor):

- Without a shield your armor must provide a base armor rating of about 130 (567 / (1.4 \* 1.25 \* 1.25 \* 2)) to reach the armor cap.
  - *Heavy Armor*: The best heavy armor, [Daedric armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric#Daedric_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric") has 108 base armor rating → 481 displayed armor rating → 69.8% damage reduction.
  - *Light Armor*: The best light armor, [Dragonscale armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Items#Dragonscale_Armor "Skyrim:Dragon Items") has 82 base armor rating → 362 displayed armor rating → 55.5% damage reduction
- With a shield, you must reach a displayed armor rating of 542 to reach the armor cap.
  - *Heavy Armor*: Daedric armor with a matching shield yields 560 displayed armor rating, enough to reach the armor cap. The next best Heavy Armor, [Dragonplate](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Items#Dragonplate_Armor "Skyrim:Dragon Items") with a matching shield provides 525 displayed armor rating → 78.0% damage reduction
  - *Light Armor*: Dragonscale armor with a matching shield yields 426 displayed armor rating → 66.2% damage reduction

**Light / Heavy armor skills + magic effects**

While it's impossible for a light armor user to reach the cap relying only on Light Armor skill and perks, you can still reach the cap without using Smithing, Enchanting, or Alchemy effects. A player with maxed out Light Armor skills, a full set of Dragonscale armor, and a Dragonscale shield will have a displayed armor rating of 423 and a 65.66% damage reduction, 119 less than the 542 displayed armor rating needed to reach the armor cap. Activating the Lord Stone will boost displayed armor rating to 473 and a 71.66% damage reduction. Casting the [armor spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_(spells) "Skyrim:Armor (spells)") Ironflesh or Ebonyflesh will boost displayed armor rating over 542, reaching the 80% armor cap.

**Light / Heavy armor skills + smithing**

Reaching the armor cap becomes significantly easier with smithing. Let's say you have 100 smithing and all relevant smithing perks in addition to 100 armor skill and all relevant armor perks.

- Improving a piece of armor to Legendary quality adds +10 to the armor rating, or +20 if the piece is chest armor. This means that improving a fully matched armor set to legendary boosts the total base armor rating by 20 + 10 + 10 + 10 = 50.
- Without a shield your armor must provide a base armor rating of about 80 to reach the armor cap, since 80 + 50 = 130 (567 / (1.4 \* 1.25 \* 1.25 \* 2)).
  - *Heavy armor*: A full set of [Chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Chitin#Chitin_Armor "Skyrim:Chitin") or [Steel Plate armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Advanced_Armors#Steel_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Advanced Armors") provides 87 base armor rating, so any tempered set of heavy armor with equal or greater base armor rating will allow you to reach the armor cap
  - *Light armor*: Only Dragonscale armor provides a high enough armor rating (82) to reach the armor cap with tempering
- With a shield, you must reach a displayed armor rating of 542 to reach the armor cap.
  - *Heavy Armor*: A full set of tempered [Iron Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron#Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron") with a matching shield yields a displayed armor rating of 547, enough to reach the armor cap. This means that any matching set of heavy armor equal or higher in quality to iron armor can be used to reach the armor cap. Since iron armor is the lowest quality heavy armor, this means that any tempered heavy armor set will reach the armor cap
  - *Light armor*: A full set of tempered [Elven Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven#Elven_Armor "Skyrim:Elven") with a matching shield yields a displayed armor rating of 550, enough to reach the armor cap. This means that any matching set of light armor equal or higher in quality to elven armor can be used to reach the armor cap.

**Light / Heavy armor skills + smithing + alchemy + enchanting**

With Fortify Smithing enchanted apparel and Fortify Smithing potions you can boost Smithing even further, which can potentially allow *any* material to reach the cap, without needing any further benefits (such as the [Notched Pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Notched_Pickaxe "Skyrim:Notched Pickaxe")); with maxed out enchanting and alchemy and the appropriate perks, using fortify enchanting potions to make better fortify alchemy apparel to make better fortify enchanting potions, to provide the best available Smithing bonuses, you will add 134 total tempering to any suit *even without a perk*, which is above the 130 rating mentioned above. This means you could temper a theoretical 0-rating suit (which doesn't exist) high enough to hit the cap, and you don't need a shield to get there. *With* a tempering perk, you will nearly double this, adding 259 to any suit you make; this is practically sufficient to drop any non-chest piece from any suit, and even with the loss of *two* armor perks (for wearing a full suit and wearing a matched set), you will still hit the cap, allowing you to walk around without a helmet, if you like - just remember, you will also lose any *other* armor perks you have that trigger from having a piece in all 4 wearable slots.

## Notes

- Clothes such as robes and other apparel do not count as armor, and as such do not benefit from the hidden armor rating bonus.
- [Custom Fit](/wiki/Skyrim:Custom_Fit "Skyrim:Custom Fit"), [Well Fitted](/wiki/Skyrim:Well_Fitted "Skyrim:Well Fitted"), and [Matching Set](/wiki/Skyrim:Matching_Set "Skyrim:Matching Set") perks are applied to shields if the four pieces of worn armor (armor, helmet, gloves, boots) match appropriately. The shield does not have to be of the same set, or even the same type (light or heavy).
- Shields do not benefit from either [Agile Defender](/wiki/Skyrim:Agile_Defender "Skyrim:Agile Defender") or [Juggernaut](/wiki/Skyrim:Juggernaut "Skyrim:Juggernaut"), and do not advance the light or heavy armor skills when struck.
- Armor rating/damage reduction does not affect the speed at which the skill is trained.
- If you drop a piece of armor or clothing in front of an NPC, generally in a city or town, they may run up to you and [ask you](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#.22Can_I_have_that_armor.3F.22 "Skyrim:World Interactions") if you are throwing it away.
- [Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Dialogue#Reactions_to_Player.27s_Equipment "Skyrim:Guard Dialogue") may comment on what kind of armor you're wearing, depending on what faction they belong to and what you're wearing at the time.
- With version 1.2.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), the Matching Set perks for Light Armor and Heavy Armor have had their conditions changed so that they're now looking for >= 4 instead of just == 4 to qualify for the perk.

[^](#note_No_Shield)Those armors sets have no matching shield so they are given one of the same material, if any available

[††](#note_Stahlrim)Forging Stalhrim armor also requires completion of the quest [A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim").

[†††](#note_Creation_Club)Those sets will be found during their respective quests and then can be forged by the player but will not appear at random in chests or NPCs.

[‡](#note_Daedric)All Daedric armor can also be made at the [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge") (except the boots, see [Atronach Forge bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge#Bugs "Skyrim:Atronach Forge")), in which case the Daedric Smithing perk is not needed, but instead the [Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Sigil Stone") must be obtained. Tempering armor created at the Atronach Forge is still augmented by the Daedric Smithing perk.

[‡‡‡](#note_Daedric_Mail)Daedric Mail set has no helmet.

# Skyrim:Arnbjorn

## Overview

Arnbjorn sharpening a blade

Werewolf Arnbjorn

**Arnbjorn** is a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf") [assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatAssassin "Skyrim:CombatAssassin"), former [Companion](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions"), and a member of the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"). He is also [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid")'s husband.

He wears a special set of [Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Shrouded Armor") with elbow-length sleeves instead of the usual wrist length, and fights with an [Iron Battleaxe of Chills](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe_of_Chills "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe of Chills").

Arnbjorn lives a very relaxed life at the Sanctuary. He gets up at 8AM then spends the rest of the day usually sharpening weapons or [talking to the other family members](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood#Radiant_Conversations "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"). Then, at midnight, he'll head to his bed to finally get some sleep.

When you greet him, he'll reveal his marital status first, saying, *"Let me guess - Astrid failed to mention I'm her husband? She has a tendency to do that. Doesn't want the others thinking she plays favorites."* He also uses a lot of food-related nicknames, *"What do you want, beef roast?"*, *"You're part of a family now, hamshank. I trust you... you trust me. Got it?"*, and *"Hello, tidbit."* He'll also explain these by saying how he thinks of you as food *"Don't take offense to the nicknames, morsel. I'm a werewolf. Hard not to think of you as a snack."* If he catches you [sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") by him, he'll say, *"You're putting your hand... in my pocket? Have you gone complete cracked?"* If you ask him to tell something about himself, he will give you a small summary of information. *"Look. If you're trying to get to know me - don't. I don't like you, and I never will. It's nothing personal. But... My wife trusts you, and I trust her judgment. So you can't be all bad. Here's all you need to know: I'm a werewolf. I like killing things. I love Astrid. I hate annoying people. And the color blue gives me a headache."* This response, however, changes drastically if you are a member of [The Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Companions "Skyrim:The Companions"); *"I might ask the same of you. For you are more than mortal. You are moon-born. You are wolf. So you're a Companion, then? I can't imagine you got your gift anywhere else. I hope you have better luck with them than I did. Oh yes, I was once brother to the Companions. Let's just say they found my methods "unsettling." The Dark Brotherhood, obviously, feels differently."* If you ask him what he thinks about [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") and the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother"), he will boldly state, *"The witless fool and his pet corpse? Take a guess."* When exiting conversation, Arnbjorn will use more nicknames, saying either *"Take care of yourself, beef roast."*, *"Later, ham hock."*, or a more out-of-character *"Yeah, good luck."*

## Related Quests

- **[The Cure for Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cure_for_Madness "Skyrim:The Cure for Madness")**: Confront the traitor among the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood").
- **[Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate")**: Assist [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") members in the fight against the [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus") assault.
- **[Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!")**: Finish the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") and rid Skyrim of their kind.

### Sanctuary

When you first enter the Sanctuary, Arnbjorn will be taking part in the following conversation:

Quality "family" time

**Arnbjorn**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**[Veezara](/wiki/Skyrim:Veezara "Skyrim:Veezara")**: *"Ha ha ha ha! Again! Again! Do the part where he tries to buy you some candy."*
**[Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette")**: *"Okay, okay. Wait. Here we go. "Ooh, you are such a pretty little girl. Would the sweetie like a sweetie? Oh yes, how about some chocolate?" Oh yes, please, kind sir. My mama and papa left me all alone, and I'm so very hungry. I know a shortcut to the candy shop. Through this alley. Oh ya, very good. Very good. My it is dark down here. Oh, but you are so beautiful. Such a lovely smile. Your teeth... your teeth! No! Aggghh!!"*
**[Gabriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Gabriella "Skyrim:Gabriella")**: *"Oh Babette, but you are so wicked."*
**[Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir")**: *"What about you, Festus? How did that last contract turn out?"*
**Arnbjorn**: *"Oh, yes, please, old man. Regale us with your tales of wizardry..."*
**[Festus Krex](/wiki/Skyrim:Festus_Krex "Skyrim:Festus Krex")**: *"Ah, the young and stupid. Always mocking the experienced and brilliant. My contract went very well, I'll have you know. Tried a new spell. Little something I've been working on in my spare time. Came "this" close to turning that priest inside out. Damned messy."*
**Gabriella**: *"And what of your latest, Arnbjorn. Something about a [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit")? Merchant was it?"*
**Babette**: *"Oh, a big doggy chasing a little kitty! How adorable!"*
**Nazir**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Festus**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Veezara**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Arnbjorn**: *"I am not adorable, it was not funny, and he wasn't a merchant. He was a Khajiit monk, a master of the [Whispering Fang](/wiki/Lore:Whispering_Fang "Lore:Whispering Fang") style. But now he's dead... and I have a new loincloth."*
**Arnbjorn**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Babette**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Festus**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*
**Nazir**: *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha ha!"*

From the very first moment you speak to him it's clear that he is not impressed by you. *"Well, well. It's raw meat. Oh, my beautiful wife has told me all about you."* Regardless of how you react, he will follow up with *"I'll give you a week before you end up dead in a ditch."*

### The Cure for Madness

*"I gave as good as I got."*

When you return to the Sanctuary, you'll find Veezara wounded on the ground. Neither Cicero or Arnbjorn are anywhere to be found. Speaking to Astrid will fill you in on the details, *"I want you to find that miserable little fool and end his life! But first... find my husband. Make sure he's all right. After the attack, Arnbjorn flew into a rage. When Cicero left... Arnbjorn went after him. They disappeared into the wild."* Once you find evidence pointing to the location that they were headed, Astrid once again urges you to make sure Arnbjorn is in good health, *"Every moment counts, so I want you to take my horse. His name is [Shadowmere](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmere "Skyrim:Shadowmere"). You'll find him outside, by the pool. Let's just say he's... one of us. Find Arnbjorn. Make sure my husband's all right."*

While Astrid is clearly worried, Nazir seems to have more confidence in Arnbjorn, stating *"Going after Cicero now would be a fool's errand. That little jester is currently being digested in Arnbjorn's stomach, mark my words."*

Once you arrive at the [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary"), you will immediately spot Arnbjorn sitting on the ground, clearly in pain. When he notices you, he will start dialogue:

:   *"Should have figured Astrid would send you."*

    :   **You're hurt.**
    :   *"What gave it away? Ha ha ha ha ha. Yeah, got to admit that little jester is good with that butter knife. But don't worry, I gave as good as I got."*

        :   **Where's Cicero now?**
        :   *"In there! Through the door. Some old Sanctuary, by the looks of it. I would have followed him, but I don't know the phrase."*

            :   **I know the phrase. I'll get Cicero - you go home.**
            :   *"All right, you convinced me. Doubt I'd be much good to you, anyway. The little fop cut me pretty deep. But I slashed him good. Pretty sure I severed an artery. Don't know what you're going to find in there... but you can probably just follow the blood."*

He will end the conversation with a request:

:   *"Do me a favor and kill that little jester twice. Just to make sure."*

After this he leaves with the words: *"Good hunting. I'll see you back at the Sanctuary."*

If you exited the conversation at any point, he will say, *"Gee, thanks for the help."*

When you return to the Sanctuary after finishing business with Cicero, Arnbjorn will be happy to see you and say, *"There you are. Look, I... I just wanted to say thanks for coming to find me. Back in Dawnstar. Crazy jester finally met his match, am I right?"*

### Death Incarnate

When you finish [To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire"), and return to Sanctuary, you will find Arnbjorn in Werewolf form fending off members of the [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus"). While doing so, he will meet his demise.

### Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!

During Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!, you will be sent to kill every Dark Brotherhood member in the [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary"), Arnbjorn will be one of the required people to kill. During this quest, he gains a leveled battleaxe as well as leveled gold and two leveled healing potions.
