Arniel Gane

**Arniel Gane**, a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer"), is one of the scholars at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"). He specializes in the art of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") although most of his time is spent on research entirely unrelated to the arcane arts, something he keeps a secret from everyone until you have completed [Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books"). At that point he reveals his secret and asks for your help to uncover one of the greatest mysteries in Skyrim history.

He lives in the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"), in the first room on the right on the second floor, and sleeps there every night between 4am and noon. He then dedicates the entire day to his secret studies and stays in his room. At 8pm he seeks out his friend and colleague [Phinis Gestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Phinis_Gestor "Skyrim:Phinis Gestor") who will be in the [Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"). At 11pm Arniel returns to his quarters and strolls around until bedtime. There are several exceptions to this routine, as he will participate in several quests related to the discovery of the [Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Lore:Eye_of_Magnus "Lore:Eye of Magnus"). See [this section](#Quest-Related_Events) for details.

He wears [adept robes of Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Adept_Robes_of_Alteration "Skyrim:Adept Robes of Alteration") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#0006b46c "Skyrim:Shoes"). He is a very skilled mage and knows numerous spells, including [Ironflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironflesh "Skyrim:Ironflesh"), [Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Dread Zombie"), [Revenant](/wiki/Skyrim:Revenant "Skyrim:Revenant"), [Frost Cloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Cloak "Skyrim:Frost Cloak"), [Ice Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Storm "Skyrim:Ice Storm"), [Icy Spear](/wiki/Skyrim:Icy_Spear "Skyrim:Icy Spear"), [Lightning Bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt"), [Close Wounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Close_Wounds "Skyrim:Close Wounds"), [Grand Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Healing "Skyrim:Grand Healing"), [Greater Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Ward "Skyrim:Greater Ward"), and [Steadfast Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Ward "Skyrim:Steadfast Ward").

When you first join the College as a mere apprentice, Arniel Gane will be secretive about his research although he hints at something very big: *"I'm working on some very important research, I assure you."* and *"The exact nature of my research is a secret, I'm afraid, but it really is quite valuable."* Unfortunately, nobody cares about his important research: *"I don't think anyone here truly understands how useful my work will be."* and *"When I've finished what I'm working on, everyone will understand its significance."* Even if he sounds like he could use a hand, he will not share his secret with you: *"You mean the official sort of business? Hmm, well... no. No, not really."* He will then close the conversation without revealing anything else.

As you progress through the College quest line, Arniel will share several opinions on the strange and sometimes tragic events that unfold. Like everyone else, he is not too fond of [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") advisor [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano"): *"He's asked far, far too many questions about my research. I think the Thalmor are trying to steal my work! I haven't told him anything, of course. What I'm doing is far too important. Can't breathe a word of it."* During the quest [Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions") you can also ask him how to find the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain"): *"What? The Augur? Oh no, I'm quite sure that's... He's nothing I'm involved in. No, no. Mirabelle Ervine... Or Tolfdir. They're qualified to discuss him. Not me, definitely not."* Also, as the College quest line progresses, he will become more and more nervous, greeting you with: *"I can't lose all my research. There has to be a way to save the College."*, *"I hope you know what you're doing."*, and *"I'll be amazed if any of us survive this."*

## Related Quests

- **[Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal")**: Uncover the mysteries beneath this ancient ruin.
- **[Containment](/wiki/Skyrim:Containment "Skyrim:Containment")**: Deal with the aftermath of the Eye's power surge.
- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Under Saarthal

Arniel in [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal")

The first time Arniel Gane ventures outside the College is when [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") suggests that you and the other apprentices help out with the excavation of [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal"), one of the oldest ruins in Skyrim. At that point Arniel will be teleported to a spot inside the excavation site. Once you have entered, ask Tolfdir what you can do to help and he will say: *"Ah, yes. Hmm. Well, why don't you see if you can assist Arniel Gane? He's one of our scholars, here working on cataloging our finds. I expect he'd appreciate some help in locating any additional magical artifacts here in the ruins."* When asked again he will repeat: *"Find Arniel Gane. He's somewhere in the northern section of the ruins. He'll show you what to do."*

Arniel will wander around in the northwestern tunnels of the site, seemingly unengaged, still researching his secret project by reading a book. When approached he will say: *"Well, certainly none of this will benefit my research..."*, and will be skeptical about the whole affair: *"I'll be amazed if we find anything useful here."* and *"It's going to take forever to sift through all this."* If you have talked with him before at the College he will greet you with: *"What? Ah, yes. You. I remember you. You're going to help? That's fine. Just... Just don't make a mess of my work."* Alternatively, he will greet you with: *"You must be one of the new apprentices, then? Fine, fine. Just... just don't make a mess of my work, all right?"* He will then continue: *"I've only looked through a portion of this section. You, uh, you can look around in the chambers just north of here. Try and be careful, all right? We don't want to damage anything."* You will now be tasked with a mini-quest of finding four magical artifacts. When asked again, Arniel will repeat: *"Just round up the rest of the magical artifacts so that I can catalog them."* When you pick up the [Saarthal Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal_Amulet "Skyrim:Saarthal Amulet"), you will be trapped and Tolfdir will panic while Arniel will remain unaffected. Once you have broken the barrier, you can head back to Arniel and hand him your findings. Once again, he will be uninterested but will take them back with the words: *"I see. It probably doesn't even matter now, what with the mess that's been made in here. I'll add this to the rest of the items. I don't think there's anything further I need from you."* Arniel will then stay behind while you and Tolfdir investigate the rest of the ruin leading to the discovery of a very mysterious orb. When the quest is completed, Arniel will travel all the way back to the College on foot, a trip that takes him over four in-game hours.

|  |
| --- |
| [MW-item-Dwemer Parchment.png](/wiki/File:MW-item-Dwemer_Parchment.png) Arniel's Endeavor Part 1 Once you have completed [Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books"), thus gaining respect from the members of the College, Arniel Gane will be ready to share a very little bit of his secret and admit he could use some help: *"You mean the official sort of business? Hmm, well... no. No, not really. But... I can't help but notice that you're doing quite well for yourself, rising through the ranks and all. It may not be 'official', but there is a, uhh, project I've been working on. I wonder if perhaps you could assist with it."* He will, however, not really share any secrets; he just wants your help. Two options are available. When asked if he wants to tell about his project he will say: *"Ah, yes. Umm, no. No, I don't think so. Not at this point. It's just that, well I'm not even really sure it's going to amount to anything just yet. All theoretical right now, you understand. But the implications are quite intriguing, I think. I simply need some experimental results to confirm my suspicions."* If you instead ask him if he is involved with something dangerous he will decline: *"What? No, no. Goodness, no! At least, I don't think so. No, it's just... It's just something I'd prefer to keep to myself."* Both options will lead to his first request: *"Just... Just bring me some Dwemer cogs. I need to examine them for the methods used in forging them. Ten of them should be enough for me to get a better understanding of how they were crafted. That's all I need, all right?"* When asked about the task again he will reveal that he is secretly studying the ancient [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer"): *"I simply need more pieces of Dwemer equipment to study. It's nothing dangerous... At least, not necessarily. And please, let's just... Let's keep this between us."* This starts [Part 1](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor#Part_1 "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor") of the quest [Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor").  When you return to Arniel with the ten [Dwemer cogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cog "Skyrim:Dwemer Cog") he will be happy to see his project getting underway and say: *"Ah, that's excellent news. This will be most helpful in furthering my research. I'm afraid I can't offer you much right now, but please take this. And perhaps, if this is all successful... Well, let's not get ahead of ourselves. It's too early to be getting excited. Still, this is most encouraging. Thank you again. If I require anything else, I shall be sure and let you know."* This concludes part 1 of the quest and you can start [Part 2](#Arniel.27s_Endeavor_Part_2) right away. |

Despite his huge knowledge and many skills, Arniel Gane is obviously shy, clumsy, and not really skilled in the art of communication. Nobody cares about his important research and some will not even talk to him. [Nirya](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirya "Skyrim:Nirya") in particular will be hateful, while [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir") will be a bit more friendly. During the course of the day, Arniel was supposed to make several attempts to converse with the other College members, but doesn't, due to a [bug](#Bugs):

*"What is it?"*

**Arniel**: *"Err, excuse me Enthir. Might I have a moment?"*
**Enthir**: *"What is it?"*
**Arniel**: *"Yes, err, apologies for the intrusion. I was wondering, err, if you could possibly, ah, procure a few select items for me."*
**Enthir**: *"Really, Arniel? Because I seem to recall doing just that for you recently, at which point you assured me that you'd cover my expenses. And that, my nervous little friend, has not happened. Would you care to comment on that, perhaps?"*
**Arniel**: *"Ahh, hmm. Yes. I, err, I was unaware that I had forgotten that. I will, err, I mean I'll take care of that as soon as possible."*
**Enthir**: *"See that you do."*

**Nirya**: *"What are you up to, Gane? Hmm?"*
**Arniel**: *"What? Err, nothing!"*
**Nirya**: *"Some days I marvel that you haven't managed to blow yourself up."*

**Arniel**: *"Hello, Nirya."*
**Nirya**: *"Don't even talk to me, Gane."*
**Arniel**: *"Ah, err, yes. Sorry."*

|  |
| --- |
| [MW-item-Dwemer Parchment 03.png](/wiki/File:MW-item-Dwemer_Parchment_03.png) Arniel's Endeavor Part 2 While things turn bad elsewhere in the College, Arniel Gane will offer you the next task right away, starting [Part 2](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor#Part_2 "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor") of [Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor"). When asked if you can offer further assistance he will say: *"As a matter of fact, there is something you can do for me. I had retained Enthir's services in, uhh, acquiring something specific. But now he's refusing to deliver. Could you perhaps speak with him, and see if we can come to some sort of arrangement?"*  [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"), a [Bosmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") with very strong ties to the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), lives on the same floor as Arniel. Confront him with Arniel's claim and he will say: *"Oh dear. He's so afraid to talk to me he's sending you to do it? I should've expected as much. I'm afraid you've been a little mis-informed. I have something of mine, that I was going to sell to Arniel. I told Arniel what I wanted in exchange for it, and he was unwilling to come up with it. Now, if you're here on his behalf, I'm afraid I'm going to have to insist on my original payment."* He then reveals that you need to acquire the [Staff of Tandil](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Tandil "Skyrim:Staff of Tandil") to exchange whatever it is Arniel is after. When you return with the staff, Enthir will be pleased and say: *"Well, well. All right, you delivered on your end, so I'll deliver on mine. Here's the gem Arniel was after. Can't imagine what he expects to do with that... it's warped beyond any ability to capture a soul."* He then hands you the [Warped Soul Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Warped_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Warped Soul Gem") and finishes the conversation.  When you tell Arniel you have the soul gem, he will be excited to see his research continued, although he will still not reveal a thing: *"Do you? Wonderful. I was afraid I'd have to give up, and when I'm so close... Thank you for this. I have a great deal of work ahead of me."* This finishes Part 2 of the quest and, if you have yet to complete the College quest line, an entirely new story for Arniel. |

### Containment

*"Come on, Arniel. Let's go."*

Arniel fights the [magic anomalies](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Anomaly "Skyrim:Magic Anomaly")

The quest [Revealing the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Revealing_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Revealing the Unseen") ends with a big bang. [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano")'s obsession with the [Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Lore:Eye_of_Magnus "Lore:Eye of Magnus") causes a tragedy as Arch-Mage [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren") dies from the explosion. As you enter the courtyard, most of the members of the College will stand and look at the dead body in disbelief. Before long, [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") will take control and order you to protect the city of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") from the aftermath of Ancano's action. When you reach the bridge you will find a confused Arniel along with [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda"). After a brief conversation with Faralda, Arniel will only say: *"What have we gotten ourselves into now?"* before he runs towards Winterhold. Along the way, Faralda will notice the hesitating Arniel and will yell: *"Come on, Arniel. Let's go."* and Arniel will respond: *"Do we have to? They'd never lift a finger to help us."* On the main street of Winterhold, Arniel will finally show what he is capable of and will use all his magical skills to defeat the [magic anomalies](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Anomaly "Skyrim:Magic Anomaly") that float around. When all is said and done, Arniel will stretch and comment: *"Well, this certainly won't help our image."* He will then stay behind and make sure the town is safe while you go talk to [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") back at the College. When the quest [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus") is initiated, Arniel will be back in the College, scared: *"I can't lose all my research. There has to be a way to save the College."* and *"I hope you know what you're doing."* He will not say anything else, so you will have to complete [The Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus") before you can help him any further with the research.

|  |
| --- |
| [MW-item-Dwemer Parchment 05.png](/wiki/File:MW-item-Dwemer_Parchment_05.png) Arniel's Endeavor Part 3 After the events with the Eye of Magnus and Ancano, you will be Arch-Mage and Arniel will have gained so much respect for you that he is ready for [Part 3](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor#Part_3 "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor") of [Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor") and will finally reveal the truth. When approached he will ironically reflect on the recent events at the College: *"Perhaps we can go another few decades without a disaster. That would be nice."* When asked how the project is going he will be quite upset: *"Terrible, just terrible. I vastly underestimated the heat transfer necessary, and have destroyed my only working model. I'm at a loss."* Two options are now available. If you attempt to make fun at him he will angrily say: *"Don't patronize me!"* If you tell him you have no idea what he is talking about he will say: *"Look, it's all very simple. The [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer"), they were uhh, masters of magic in a way we can't even begin to conceive of. Their greatest achievement, however, has also been their greatest, shall we say... Mystery."* Although you once again have two options he will get to the same point if you comment on how the Dwemer have been gone for a long time: *"Precisely! What could be worth studying about a long-lost civilization? Their disappearance, of course! Instant, unexplainable. The stories have fascinated me... Ever since I was young, I wanted to know what really happened. After years and years of work, I'm closing in on a way to investigate what happened through experimentation. Only now... Well, it's simply a disaster."*  Heating the Convector  He will then explain his complex research: *"Without boring you with the, ahh, details, I am attempting to re-create the circumstances of the event. The dwarves were very clever, tapping into and drawing power from the [Heart of Lorkhan](/wiki/Lore:Heart_of_Lorkhan "Lore:Heart of Lorkhan") itself. Lacking the heart of a dead god myself, I was attempting to substitute a rather specific soul gem. The ahh, the one you helped me acquire."* He will then answer your question on why the soul gem won't work: *"Well, yes. I mean, no. That is, it might, but I'm not completely sure. I'm no tonal architect, I've only read their writings. Scraps, really. The soul gem by itself isn't enough, you see. It needs to be altered, purified. The dwarves had machines for this sort of thing. I attempted to build my own, based on designs and using parts you helped to provide. My very own Dwarven Convector. It worked, but not fully. And the uhh... The device was destroyed in the process."* If you suggest he should build a new Convector he will be annoyed: *"Hmm? No, no. No! I'm too close now. Can't take the time. Though... Perhaps there's another option. I, umm, I may require further assistance from you."* Two options are available, one of them the greedy route, asking him what you will get out of helping him: *"Well, I... Don't you see? Unlocking this mystery... The story alone is worth more riches than you can even imagine. And perhaps... well, I don't wish to speculate, but... What if we could contact the dwarves? What if they're still out there? Imagine!"* He will then tell you what needs to be done: *"Well, yes. The designs for my Convector were based on real dwarven machines, so there may still be some in existence. I'd go looking myself, but uhh... Yes, there are calculations to double- and triple-check. Many calculations. Perhaps you could seek out these Convectors in Skyrim ruins? I can even teach you the spell to heat them. It's very particular, and very important."* When you accept to learn the spell [Arniel's Convection](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Convection "Skyrim:Arniel's Convection") he will happily say: *"Wonderful, just wonderful! I knew I could count on you! Now this spell is not for defending yourself, but it's just right for heating the Convector. At least three seconds' burn is necessary. Just place the soul gem inside, and heat the Convector. At least three seconds. You'll almost certainly need to find multiple Convectors. I suspect it may be due to the nature of the soul gem versus the crystals this was intended for. Destroys the equipment in the process. But, ahh... It's effective. Three times, and the crystal should be ready for the next step. Isn't this exciting?"* He will then exit conversation and the quest will start.  When you return with the altered soul gem, Arniel will have a new, and very grateful, greeting, ready for you: *"Divines bless you. May the ground you walk quake as you pass."* When you tell him you have his gem, he will be surprised: *"It worked, then? Let me see! Goodness, that's it, isn't it?! Yes! It's not perfect, but it's a close enough approximation that it should certianly*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *suffice for initial tests! You've done excellent work here. Truly excellent. There's only one thing missing now, and that should be arriving shortly. I'll begin preparations. Thank you again so much for this."* This concludes Part 3 of Arniel's Endeavor. |

Another set of unused dialogue (see [bugs](#Bugs)) shows Arniel attempt to make contact with [Brelyna Maryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna_Maryon "Skyrim:Brelyna Maryon") and, once again, [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"):

**Arniel**: *"Do you think you might, err, have a moment to look at something for me?"*
**Brelyna**: *"If this is another dwarven trinket, I keep telling you I'm not familiar with them."*
**Arniel**: *"Yes, I just thought perhaps you'd have, err, come across something like this before."*
**Brelyna**: *"Why, because I'm a Dunmer? We didn't all grow up in dwarven ruins, you know."*
**Arniel**: *"Well, err, yes. Sorry to have troubled you."*

**Enthir**: *"So, Arniel. How's that little project of yours coming along? Any progress worth mentioning?"*
**Arniel**: *"Oh, that. Err, yes. It's... It's quite promising, I believe. Definitely on the right track. Results, err, results should be soon."*
**Enthir**: *"Right. And what did you say the point of this little venture was?"*
**Arniel**: *"Oh, no. Err, wouldn't do to say at all. Not, err, not now. Not at all. I have far too many things to do still."*
**Enthir**: *"If you say so."*

|  |
| --- |
| [MW-item-Dwemer Parchment 02.png](/wiki/File:MW-item-Dwemer_Parchment_02.png) Arniel's Endeavor Part 4 After a few days time, Arniel will have relocated to the storage room on the second floor of the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance") and will be ready with his last task, [Part 4](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor#Part_4 "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor") of [Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor"). When confronted with the question of if he has unraveled the mystery yet, he turns out to be very angry: *"No, and at this rate, I never shall! Enthir is once again holding out on me. He refuses to deliver yet another item absolutely essential to my work! I am close, so close! You must force him to see reason!"* He will, however, have no clue how to persuade Enthir: *"I don't know, I don't know! I've already agreed to pay him quite handsomely for the... well, the item in question. Just... Do whatever it takes to get him to stop lording this over me."*  When you confront Enthir he will once again reveal that Arniel told you the wrong story: *"Oh, by the Divines, you too? I've already told him. I don't have it!"* Enthir proceeds to explain that Arniel's 'thing' was supposed to be delivered by courier, but never showed up from [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") and that there is little he can do about it. When asked about what the 'thing' is, Enthir will reveal that he never got an explanation either: *"I don't know. He never told me. He made most of the arrangements himself, he just needed it transported from Morrowind. That's what I agreed to help with. If I'd known it was so important to him, I'd have charged him more."* Enthir only knows that the courier was on his way through [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") when he disappeared. While optional, it is possible to return to Arniel and tell him the news: *"What? I... I don't understand. Where is it?"* Two options are available. Tell him that it disappeared after leaving Morrowind and he will get scared: *"No, no no no. This can't be happening."* Tell him that the courier never arrived and he will say: *"He has some simple-minded courier delivering it?"* Both choices will lead to him saying: *"It can't be lost. It just can't! It's irreplaceable, do you understand? Without it, I cannot finish my work. All these years, so much time, so much energy... You must find it! It cannot end this way! Not after I've worked so hard!"* You can try and squeeze more information out of him but he will not reveal what you are looking for: *"It... It's very valuable. Critical to my work, and one-of-a-kind. That's all I care to say for now."* You can also try and ask him if he made it clear to Enthir how valuable the item was: *"Have you lost your mind? Think, please, just for a moment, about what he would do if he knew its true value. Do you really believe he would honor our agreement, or go running off to the highest bidder? Please, you must set this right. I'm begging you."*  After locating the [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") and claiming the unique dagger [Keening](/wiki/Skyrim:Keening "Skyrim:Keening") from the body, return to Arniel Gane. He will now have set up the [Warped Soul Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Warped_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Warped Soul Gem") in the storage room. He will be quite surprised when you hand him Keening: *"The dagger...? By Akatosh, they didn't even wrap it correctly? You didn't touch it did you? Well no, of course you must have! Did you attempt to wield it? And you're not dead? Gods, it's a wonder it's in one piece!"* At this final stage, three questions are available:  *"Work, damn you!"*  Arniel replicates the ancient [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer")'s disappearance  **So you have everything you need now?**  *"I do... I do indeed. Keening, one of the great tools of Kagrenac himself, is finally in my possession. I don't think I really believed this day would come."*  **What's the big deal about this dagger?**  *"This is not just a dagger! This is a dwarven artifact beyond nearly all value. A singular instrument of immense power, a tool of impossible import. Keening, and its counterpart, [Sunder](/wiki/Lore:Sunder "Lore:Sunder"). Used by the tonal architects of the Dwemer to tap into the Heart of Lorkhan."*  **So what's next?**  *"Now we see whether my theories are correct. I apologize if I have not been clear about my work. I didn't want to discuss it for fear this moment might never come. Everyone knows the dwarves disappeared. No one knows why. This little experiment is a first step in recreating the events of their disappearance in an effort to unravel that mystery. Lacking the heart of a dead god, I am substituting the crystal you helped craft in its place. I also lack Sunder, the counterpart to the dagger Keening. I am reasonably, confident, however, that this will still work. I certainly don't expect it to have quite the same results. I'm no tonal architect, of course! Well, I suppose it's time, isn't it? Let's see what happens. You, uhh... You may want to stand back a step or two. But please, don't leave. You've been instrumental in this process. I'd like you to see the results first-hand. Right, then..."*  He will then draw the dagger and take a stab at the warped soul gem, with no result: *"Hmm. That... That didn't really do anything, did it? Perhaps a little harder?"* Two more stabs will still yield no effect: *"I don't understand. This should produce some notable effect."* He will then get upset and start shouting at the soul gem: *"Work, damn you!"* He will then run amok and stab the gem several times, until a flash of light appears and everything goes quiet. Arniel is nowhere to be seen and Keening lies on the floor. The quest will end and the unique spell [Summon Arniel's Shade](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Arniel%27s_Shade "Skyrim:Summon Arniel's Shade") will be added to your magical skills. Apparently, Arniel solved the great mystery of the disappearance of the ancient [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer"), but suffered the same fate, taking the mystery and its solution with him. This great discovery will go completely unnoticed at the College – because nobody will even notice that Arniel is gone. |

## Notes

Some additional lines were written and recorded for the [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") quest, although they can never be heard in-game:

- *"You found what? Hmm. Well now. Yes, this might actually be something interesting. You'd better show that to Tolfdir right away."*
- *"You found what? Hmm. Well now. This is all very fascinating, but I don't recall asking to you to touch anything in here. I suppose you'd better show that to Tolfdir nonetheless. And please, ask before tampering with anything else."*
- You do not need to give Arniel the 3 [enchanted rings](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanted_Ring "Skyrim:Enchanted Ring") in Saarthal to finish Under Saarthal.
- With version 1.2.4 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), the ghostly version of Arniel Gane via Arniel's Shade now actually looks like him.

## Bugs

- Arniel will never initiate dialogue with his fellow College members, as all the scenes were set to take place in the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance") where none of them will ever meet.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- Despite being a conjurer, when he is forced to fight, he tends to use his fists only, although he will reanimate weak corpses if they are available. Should he find a weapon to pick up, he will keep it equipped for the rest of the game.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.

## Quick Walkthrough

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Part 1   1. Talk to [Arniel Gane](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel_Gane "Skyrim:Arniel Gane"). 2. Obtain ten [Dwemer cogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cog "Skyrim:Dwemer Cog"). 3. Return to Arniel. | Part 3   1. Speak to Arniel. 2. Place the [warped soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Warped_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Warped Soul Gem") inside a Dwemer convector 1–3 times. 3. Use [Arniel's Convection](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Convection "Skyrim:Arniel's Convection") spell to heat the Dwemer convector 1–3 times. 4. Return to Arniel. |
| Part 2   1. Speak with Arniel once again. 2. Acquire the staff that [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir") sold. 3. Return to Arniel. | Part 4   1. Talk to Arniel in the Hall of Countenance. 2. Talk to Enthir. 3. Retrieve item. 4. Watch Arniel's experiment. |

### Part 1

Talk to Arniel Gane and ask if there is any College business you can assist him with. He'll state that it's nothing official, but he is working on a "project". He refuses to say anything about it, but he asks you to bring him ten [Dwemer cogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cog "Skyrim:Dwemer Cog"). They can be found randomly throughout any and all Dwarven ruins. If you have not already found a Dwarven ruin, [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand") is near the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), and the ruin under [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") is easy to find and lower-level friendly.

There are plenty of Dwemer cogs inside [Dwemer Museum](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum") in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"), specifically in the closest right corner from the entrance; with [stealthy](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") movement, all cogs can be obtained without any repercussions, making this the easiest and quickest method. The main College quest line will take you to [Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft"), which also has more than ten Dwemer cogs. Depending on the ruins and your carry capacity (cogs weigh 10 each) you may end up needing two or three trips to get all the cogs.

Once you have obtained the ten Dwemer cogs, return to Arniel and he will reward you with a [small amount of gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

### Part 2

Arniel needs a very specific item for his project and is having trouble getting Enthir to give it to him. He'd like you to speak to Enthir and return to him with the item. Speaking to Enthir reveals that the item Arniel wants never belonged to him and is Enthir's property. He agrees to relinquish it, though—if you'll retrieve the [Staff of Tandil](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Tandil "Skyrim:Staff of Tandil") he sold to an unscrupulous character.

The character is a boss level caster in a radiantly assigned dungeon. Depending on which one you get the quest may be increasingly more or less difficult. Some of the dungeons, such as [Boulderfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Boulderfall_Cave "Skyrim:Boulderfall Cave") and [Cragwallow Slope](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragwallow_Slope "Skyrim:Cragwallow Slope"), are extremely small while others might be rather involved or of a difficult nature. The staff should be either on the boss level caster, somewhere nearby, or in the boss level chest.

Once you have the staff, return to Enthir. He'll give you the [warped soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Warped_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Warped Soul Gem"), which can then be returned to Arniel to proceed with the quest.

#### Radiant Options

Possible values of `<Dungeon>` are:

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund") [Cragwallow Slope](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragwallow_Slope "Skyrim:Cragwallow Slope") [Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar") | [Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass") [Falkreath Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Watchtower "Skyrim:Falkreath Watchtower") [Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep") [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum") [Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge") | [Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep") [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave") | [Harmugstahl](/wiki/Skyrim:Harmugstahl "Skyrim:Harmugstahl") | [Boulderfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Boulderfall_Cave "Skyrim:Boulderfall Cave") [Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower") | [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast") | [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave") [Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild") |

### Part 3

.jpg)

A Dwemer Convector heated by Arniel's spell

Begin this quest by asking [Arniel](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel_Gane "Skyrim:Arniel Gane") about the progress of his project. He will say that it is going terribly. He reveals that he is trying to simulate the disappearance of the [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") but the warped soul gem that you acquired for him needs to be charged. Unfortunately, the apparatus he was using to charge it was destroyed in the process and he has no time to build another. Thus, he is only too happy to accept your generous offer to charge it for him.

Arniel tells you that the Dwemer used to use convectors to charge their soul gems and that some of these devices probably still exist among Dwarven ruins. He needs two more charges after his own initial charge to power the gem. Due to the nature of the warped soul gem, it will destroy the convector it is charged in. What you need to do is find a few Dwemer convectors and place the warped soul gem inside. He will teach you a spell called [Arniel's Convection](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Convection "Skyrim:Arniel's Convection") that must be channeled onto the Dwemer convector until the stone is charged. Keep channeling the convector until the quest updates. You will then have to find a new convector and repeat this process up to two times. There seems to be some variance on whether it takes one to three times to fully charge the stone and use of dual casting can complicate the matter.

There are six Dwemer convectors in all of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"):

- [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt"): Across the river from it in an unmarked ruin, east-northeast of the map marker.
- [Deep Folk Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Deep_Folk_Crossing "Skyrim:Deep Folk Crossing"): Across the bridge from it at an unmarked ruin, just north of the map marker.
- [Dwarven Storeroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Storeroom "Skyrim:Dwarven Storeroom"): Simple freestanding Dwarven structure near Mzulft. No enemies.
- [Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft"): Near the entrance in the first rooms after the hall, just before the second incline. Must have started [Revealing the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Revealing_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Revealing the Unseen").
- [Ruins of Bthalft](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Bthalft "Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft"): Exterior only ruins, [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") here.
- [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"): Southwest of the village at an unmarked ruin with a single [warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock").

Two are northward of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"), one south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), one southwest of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"), and two among the ruins of Mzulft. The two northwest of Karthwasten are probably the easiest to use since no enemies spawn at their locations (wild animals may be a nuisance however) and they are relatively close together. One is directly north of Karthwasten, northeast and across the river from Druadach Redoubt. It is at the base of the unmarked Dwemer pillar. If you cross the river and follow it upstream you will come to Deep Folk Crossing. Cross the bridge and the second Dwemer convector will be in front of you. The one south of Ivarstead is at the Ruins of Bthalft and has bandits. The one southwest of Shor's Stone is between there and [Autumnshade Clearing](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnshade_Clearing "Skyrim:Autumnshade Clearing") and has a rogue mage. At Mzulft, one is inside the storeroom (a separate building to the right of the ruin entrance when you arrive) and the other is within the ruins proper.

### Part 4

The dead courier

Arniel disappearing in a flash of light

Unlike previous parts of the quest, about two or three days must pass before continuing. Thereafter, talk to Arniel again. He is often to be found on the upper floor of the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"), but may also be in the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance"). Once more, he's used Enthir's services, and once more, you have to pick up the pieces.

Talk to Enthir, who is almost always in his room in the Hall of Attainment. He's quite annoyed since he has no idea where the item is—or even what it is, for that matter. He was only tasked with providing transport for it from [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") and it simply hasn't arrived. Enthir tells you to go look for the [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") somewhere in the east, and marks a location on your map.

The precise location of the courier varies. When you finally do locate him, it's immediately apparent why he didn't complete the delivery. Retrieve the blade "[Keening](/wiki/Skyrim:Keening "Skyrim:Keening")" from his body and return it to Arniel. He is outraged that it wasn't wrapped properly and amazed that you didn't die when you touched it. By way of explanation, he relates something of the background of [Keening](/wiki/Lore:Keening "Lore:Keening") and [Sunder](/wiki/Lore:Sunder "Lore:Sunder"), the [legendary tools](/wiki/Lore:Kagrenac%27s_Tools "Lore:Kagrenac's Tools") of the Dwemer Tonal Architect [Lord Kagrenac](/wiki/Lore:Kagrenac "Lore:Kagrenac").

Arniel now conducts his experiment in an attempt to figure out how and why the Dwemer disappeared. Striking the warped soul gem with Keening, he finds that it does nothing. He strikes again, gaining no apparent result once more. Having lost his temper, he curses, lashes out a third time... and disappears in a flash of light, never to be seen again.

The quest is then unceremoniously updated as complete. Pick up Keening from the floor if you wish (although it seems to have come down in the world somewhat since the Third Era). [Summon Arniel's Shade](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Arniel%27s_Shade "Skyrim:Summon Arniel's Shade") will be added to your spell list automatically.

#### Radiant Options

Possible values of `<Dungeon>` are:

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") |
| --- | --- |
| [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") [Cragwallow Slope](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragwallow_Slope "Skyrim:Cragwallow Slope") [Cronvangr Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Hall "Skyrim:Cronvangr Hall") [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout") [Mara's Eye Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Pond "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Pond") [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch") [Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar") [Uttering Hills Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Camp "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Camp") | [Autumnshade Clearing](/wiki/Skyrim:Autumnshade_Clearing "Skyrim:Autumnshade Clearing") [Broken Helm Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Helm_Hollow "Skyrim:Broken Helm Hollow") [Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower") [Darkwater Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pass "Skyrim:Darkwater Pass") [Faldar's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldar%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Faldar's Tooth") [Pinepeak Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinepeak_Cavern "Skyrim:Pinepeak Cavern") [Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") [Tolvald's Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolvald%27s_Cave "Skyrim:Tolvald's Cave") [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch") |

## Notes

- Part three is not available until you complete the quest [The Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus").
  - It's thus irrelevant that one cannot enter Mzulft until having started [Revealing the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Revealing_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Revealing the Unseen") to find the convector, since this quest has already been completed long before The Eye of Magnus.
- The quest tracker will not track Dwemer cogs you pick up, but they still count for the quest, so you must keep count of them yourself.
- It is not necessary to carry around all ten cogs at the same time; utilize storage at the College to avoid carrying around the heavy cogs.
- Part two is almost identical in nature to [Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request"), but the radiant dungeon assignment might differ. It is possible to be sent to the same location in both quests.
- No matter how many times you use Keening to strike the warped soul gem, you will not disappear in a blinding flash.
- Enthir will have slightly different dialogue during this quest if you are the arch-mage or completed [Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers").
- After providing Keening to Arniel, he will comment on the absence of Sunder. Even with the [Sunder & Wraithguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed and [Sunder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder "Skyrim:Sunder") in your inventory, it will not impact the quest, and Arniel will still mention that he lacks the latter. This is due to the fact that Sunder is added via the Creation Club long after the game was released, so there were no lines recorded for him regarding it.
- Despite displaying the "Take Warped Soul Gem" command when highlighted, the soul gem cannot be removed after the experiment has ended (nor during the experiment).

## Bugs

- In some cases the warped soul gem will get duplicated after heating it. This prevents further dialogue with Arniel, thus making it impossible to complete the quest.
  - You may be able to fix this by leaving one of the duplicates of the gem in the Dwarven convector. This should allow you to be able to finish the dialogue with Arniel.
  -  You can remove extra warped gems through the console with the command `player.removeitem 6a10a 1` (that's for the final version only, the others have different form IDs) for each extra warped gem in your inventory.
  - Assuming this does not occur on the third and final convector heating, this can be fixed by putting both soul gems in the next convector box and then heating it with the spell, this will result in one of the soul gems disappearing, thus leaving only one to collect and allowing the completion dialogue with Arniel.
  - This can be caused by adding the Destruction: Augmented Flames perk or Dual Wielding.
- The quest can fail to update, getting stuck on "Place the warped soul gem into a final Convector". Dual/single casting, alternate convectors does not remedy.

  **Mod Notes**: The objective displayed jumps ahead of the item you possess, causing the script conditions to fail.

  - This can be caused by adding the Destruction: Augmented Flames perk or Dual Wielding.
  - Load a save from before the first convector was used, and heat each convector by casting with a single hand only in short pulses, stopping immediately when each quest stage is reached.
  -  Another option is to place the warped soul gem into a convector, type `setstage MGRArniel03 20` in the console, then heat the convector and the quest updates. If it doesn't update, make sure a warped soul gem is in the convector and type `setstage MGRArniel03 30`.
  - Make sure that you did not leave any item in any convector, they must all be empty.
- After returning the gem the quest will be completed but if you look at it under completed quests the bullet marker for the last stage is hollow (as if the stage was not completed). This does not seem to affect gameplay.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- It is possible to get Keening from the courier before talking to Enthir about the mysterious item Arniel wanted delivered from Morrowind. When this happens, you can find the courier, but you can't advance the quest because you can't get Keening from him again.
  -  Type `setstage MGRArniel04 30` in the console. (Note that you don't actually have to go to the courier again to do this.)
  -  Go to the location of the courier and type `player.dropitem 0006a13c 1` in the console (assuming you have only one Keening in your inventory), then pick up the dropped Keening on the ground in front of the courier. The objective <Find the courier> will complete and the incomplete objective <Deliver the package to Arniel> will appear in your journal.
  - You can wield Keening in front of Arniel and talk to him. This could trigger the following stage.
  - You can also wield Keening and use a weapon plaque, then remove it from the plaque.
  - You can also wield Keening and use a weapon rack, have your follower pick it up, go to the location of the courier's body, then finally take Keening from your follower. This will register as completed task of finding the courier.
  - Sometimes this doesn't work and instead the weapon is placed on the ground. Just get a follower to pick it up. When you take it from them, the quest will update and work properly from there.
- A quest journal would trigger multiple times.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- Keening may disappear with Arniel instead of falling to the floor as it should.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
  - Keening may be forced through the floor and land in the room below the storage area where Arniel's experiment is held. If it goes missing, try looking for it on the first floor of the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance") where [Phinis Gestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Phinis_Gestor "Skyrim:Phinis Gestor") normally sleeps (the first room to the left if you're facing the stairs).
- If Arniel happens to have another weapon equipped before you give him Keening (he has a tendency to pick up stray weapons on occasion), he will attack the warped soul gem with that weapon instead of Keening. The quest will still proceed as normal however, and Keening will still drop when Arniel disappears.
- If you previously killed the boss of the radiant dungeon that contains the Staff of Tandil, the quest marker may direct you to the empty space where the boss's body lay.
  - May happen if dungeon has non-respawning boss, e.g., [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund")
  - Type `setstage MGRArniel02 30` and `player.additem 0006a093 1` in the console to acquire the staff and continue the quest.
- Enthir might not actually take the Staff of Tandil when you bring it to him, but it is not marked as a quest item after showing it to Enthir, so you can drop or sell it as you want.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- If the boss holding the Staff of Tandil has another staff with a calm spell, it may also be marked as a quest item and then will not lose quest item status when the Staff of Tandil does. **?**
- It is possible to turn in the ten cogs to Arniel before he has given you the quest due to a missing condition on the dialogue.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- The Staff of Tandil isn't marked as a quest item before showing it to Enthir.
- Enthir may sell the Staff of Tandil after you retrieve it for him in part 2.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.8, fixes this bug.
-  In the German version of the game, you are asked to collect "Fässer", which translates as barrels, rather than "Zahnräder" (cogs).

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest quest`.

Arniel's Shade

**Arniel's Shade**, a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [sorcerer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatSorcerer "Skyrim:CombatSorcerer"), is the [ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost") of [Arniel Gane](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel_Gane "Skyrim:Arniel Gane") created when you use the spell [Summon Arniel's Shade](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Arniel%27s_Shade "Skyrim:Summon Arniel's Shade"). He has the same dialogue as reanimated [zombies](/wiki/Skyrim:Zombie "Skyrim:Zombie"). Arniel favors [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic, and may cast the following spells in combat: [Sparks](/wiki/Skyrim:Sparks "Skyrim:Sparks"), [Lightning Bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt"), [Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Chain Lightning"), [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball"), [Banish Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Banish_Daedra "Skyrim:Banish Daedra"), and [Heal Other](/wiki/Skyrim:Heal_Other "Skyrim:Heal Other").

He wears [adept robes of Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Adept_Robes_of_Alteration "Skyrim:Adept Robes of Alteration") along with an [adept hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Adept_Hood "Skyrim:Adept Hood") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006b46c "Skyrim:Clothing").

Arniel's Shade has some high-level fixed skill levels. He has 100 in Destruction and [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion"), 97 in [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") and [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"), and 66 in [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"). His skill in One-handed and Heavy Armor are pointless, as he never equips a weapon or any armor. His magical skills differ significantly from when he was alive. Notably, his skill in [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") has fallen from 84 to 25, and his Restoration has fallen from 84 to 66. He has positively gained in Destruction and Illusion (going from 15 and 20 respectively, to 100).

He has the exact same schedule as his living counterpart (sleep from 4am to noon, visit [Phinis Gestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Phinis_Gestor "Skyrim:Phinis Gestor") for three hours from 8pm, and idle in his room), which he may follow if you summon him within the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") grounds, but will be ignored outside the college.

## Related Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

# Skyrim:Arnleif and Sons Trading Company

## Overview

An exterior view of the store.

**Arnleif and Sons Trading Company** is a general goods store located by the market stalls next to the entrance, on the north side of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

The store is managed by [Lisbet](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet "Skyrim:Lisbet"), who inherited it from her husband Gunnar, son of Arnleif.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Imedhnain](/wiki/Skyrim:Imedhnain "Skyrim:Imedhnain") (Employee)  [Lisbet](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet "Skyrim:Lisbet") (Owner) [General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "General Goods") |

## Related Quests

- **[Lisbet's Missing Shipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Missing_Shipment "Skyrim:Lisbet's Missing Shipment")**: Retrieve a missing Dibella Statue for a struggling store. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Arnleif and Sons Trading Company

The store consists of three rooms: a large main area where the store is located and two smaller rooms with two doors on the north wall. The store has fallen on hard times due to the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") constantly capturing shipments of goods. The store does not display any of its merchandise. Upon entering there is a short corridor into the main room, with a raised section around the walls of the room and two pillars that support the ceiling, with a counter between them with wings from the pillars towards the back of the store forming a square U-shape. [Lisbet](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet "Skyrim:Lisbet") will spend most of the day stood behind the counter while [Imedhnain](/wiki/Skyrim:Imedhnain "Skyrim:Imedhnain") wanders the store and sweeps up.

There is little to nothing of interest on the raised section even with a large number of shelving units. There is a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") on a shelf against the west wall and an archery target in the northwestern corner. There is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel, an expert-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") containing random items, and a [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") on a stone ledge all between the two doors at the rear of the store, against the north wall. There are [a piece of sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese") and two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on two different shelves against the east wall. Everything else on the raised section is clutter. There are stairs down to a sunken middle of the room halfway along each of the walls. Descending to the sunken area there are even more shelves against the raised section around the room, with a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") in a wooden bowl on a dresser to the west, a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Dance in Fire, v7](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v7 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v7")* on a crate to the north, a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") to the east, and a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") on a shelf to the south. To the west of the counter is a rack hanging from the ceiling holding a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). On the west side of the counter is a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") with a garlic braid hanging above, while on the east side of the counter is a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") with a bunch of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") hanging above. Under the counter is a copy of *[The Code of Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Code_of_Malacath "Skyrim:The Code of Malacath")*.

The bedroom to the northwest consists of two owned single beds; one to the east and one to the west both having stone ledges as part of the walls. The ledge to the east has an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") on top, while the other ledge has a loaf of bread and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"). There is also a dresser against the north wall. The room to the northeast consists of a single owned bed against the east wall and a huge fireplace to the north with a cast iron pot on the floor beside it holding a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") and a potato. Against the west wall is a long wooden table with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a portion of grilled leeks, a potato, a loaf of bread and a cabbage in a cast iron pot. To the right of the table is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") on a stone ledge with a copy of *[Dwarves, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarves,_v3 "Skyrim:Dwarves, v3")* leaning against it. The chest contains leveled items. To the left of the table is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand. There are also a few food sacks throughout the building.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the store's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ~1 | Leveled Jewelry (unenchanted) or [Amulet of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Amulets_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") | Max 2 (2@25%) |
| ~4 | Leveled Robes (enchanted) | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| ~4 | Leveled [Animal Parts](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Parts "Skyrim:Animal Parts") | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| ~1 | Leveled [Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems") | Max 2 (2@25%) |
| ~3 | Leveled [Enchanted Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel") | Max 4 (4@75%) |
| ~1 | Leveled [Ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingots "Skyrim:Ingots") | Best-quality; Max 5 (5@25%) |
| ~3 | Leveled [Ores](/wiki/Skyrim:Ore "Skyrim:Ore")/[Charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal") | Max 5 (5@50%) |
| ~8 | Leveled [Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") | Max 15 (15@50%) |
| ~11 | Leveled [Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") (empty and full) | Max 15 (15@75%) |
| ~6 | [Lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") | Max 8 (7@75% + 1@100%) |

| 1 | [Potion of Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease") |  |
| ~3 | Random Novice [Spell Tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes") | Max 5 (5@50%) |
| ~5 | [Torches](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch") | Best-quality; Max 10 (10@50%) |
| ~4 | [Miscellaneous Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items") (clutter) | Max 5 (5@75%) |

## Notes

- Once Lisbet has been befriended by completing [Lisbet's Missing Shipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Missing_Shipment "Skyrim:Lisbet's Missing Shipment"), the shop can be freely looted, right down to openly picking the Strongbox towards the back and taking any gold within.
- The store will stay open for business until you enter for the first time, after which it will keep normal hours.
- The [key to the store](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Arnleif_and_Sons_Trading_Company "Skyrim:Key to Arnleif and Sons Trading Company") is carried by both Lisbet and Imedhnain. If you choose to save Brother Verulus in [The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death"), the key can be looted off of Lisbet's body without consequence.
- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the top left of the entrance door.
- If anything happens to Lisbet, her assistant, Imedhnain, will take over running the store.
- All containers in the area, with the exception of some barrels and sacks, are non-respawning.

## Bugs

- The front door of this store may be locked at all hours of the day.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.8, fixes this bug.
  - Picking the lock and entering the shop will resolve this, and the shop will lock/unlock at the normal times thereafter.

Arnskar Ember-Master

**Arnskar Ember-Master** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith") in the [Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). He moves into the area after you complete three special high-profile jobs for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory"). Despite his connection with the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), he is not a fence. He sells weapons and armor as well as the materials to make them. He focuses mostly on melee weapons over bows or armor and carries 1000 gold which is replenished daily.

There is a usable [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") and [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), as well as a counter with a few stealable weapons inside his shop.

Arnskar spends all his time serving his store he has set up in the Ragged Flagon. He will spend much of his time working at the various facilities inside his shop. However, he will occasionally take a break and just stand around or will sit down and dip his feet in the water to cool off. The only time he will not offer you his services is when you have offended the Thieves Guild by breaking one of their rules. He will not offer you his services until you have completed the [Reparations](/wiki/Skyrim:Reparations "Skyrim:Reparations") quest to get back on good terms with the Guild.

Arnskar wears a [blacksmith's apron](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006ff37 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0005b69e "Skyrim:Clothing"). He carries around a leveled [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), which can be up to [Elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality, and a small amount of gold.

## Dialogue

His normal greetings:

:   *"They don't call me the Ember-Master for nothing. What do you need?"*
:   *"Looking for the best smith in Skyrim? You found it*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*."*
:   *"Need your weapon repaired? Or could I interest you in a new one?"*

When you have offended the guild, he will not want your business and will only remark:

:   *"You're in it deep... better start shoveling your way out."*

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Arnskar's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

# Skyrim:Arob

## Overview

| Arob (RefID: 0001992A) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Stronghold | [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal") | | |
| Race | [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 6 | Class | [Orc Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Warrior "Skyrim:Orc Warrior") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001992A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00013B7B |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 108 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 67 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 100 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor")**, **[One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed")** | | |
| Class Details | [GuardOrc1H](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardOrc1H "Skyrim:GuardOrc1H") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Aggressive |
| Voice Type | [FemaleOrc](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleOrc "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleOrc") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [Blood-Kin of the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin_of_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Blood-Kin of the Orcs"); [GuardFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardFaction_(makes_an_actor_a_guard) "Skyrim:GuardFaction (makes an actor a guard)"); [OrcGuardFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:OrcGuardFaction "Skyrim:OrcGuardFaction"); [TownDushnikhYalFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownDushnikhYalFaction "Skyrim:TownDushnikhYalFaction"); [Tribal Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribal_Orcs "Skyrim:Tribal Orcs") | | |

Arob guarding the wall

**Arob** is an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardOrc1H "Skyrim:GuardOrc1H") and the hunts-wife of [Chief Burguk](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Burguk "Skyrim:Chief Burguk") in [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal"), the Orc stronghold southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

While Burguk's favored wife [Shel](/wiki/Skyrim:Shel "Skyrim:Shel") gets to be near the chief around the clock, Arob and forge-wife [Gharol](/wiki/Skyrim:Gharol "Skyrim:Gharol") practically never see their husband and spend all their time doing their duties in the hold. Arob and her son [Nagrub](/wiki/Skyrim:Nagrub "Skyrim:Nagrub") share the same responsibilities, patrolling the stronghold day and night, without ever eating or sleeping, at times scouting the surrounding wilderness for prey.

She wears a set of leveled armor, excluding the helmet; at level 1 she wears [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), at level 6 she wears [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor"), at level 18 she wears [steel plate armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Plate Armor") and at level 25 she wears [orcish armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Armor "Skyrim:Orcish Armor"). She never sleeps but carries a spare set of [ragged trousers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Trousers "Skyrim:Ragged Trousers") along with the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Burguk%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Key to Burguk's Longhouse") to [Burguk's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Burguk%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Burguk's Longhouse"). She wields leveled weapons as well; at level 1 she uses a [steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Steel War Axe") and a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"); at level 6 she uses an [orcish war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_War_Axe "Skyrim:Orcish War Axe") and an [orcish bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Bow "Skyrim:Orcish Bow"). She carries at least twenty leveled arrows and a selection of [middle-class food and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

When approached she will briefly introduce herself and her opinion on Chief Burguk:

:   *"I am the hunts-wife of this stronghold."*
:   *"Burguk is a fine chief. He brings strength and wealth to the stronghold."*

She may also recommend a few service providers in the hold:

:   *"[Murbul](/wiki/Skyrim:Murbul "Skyrim:Murbul") knows many poisons and cures if you need them."*
:   *"You should see Gharol if you're looking for a blade or armor."*

## Conversations

During the long days and nights, Arob and Nagrub will occasionally share their happiness:

**Nagrub**: *"Ah, the air is good today. I welcome the smell of blood from all the kills I will make."*
**Arob**: *"Patience, my son. The hunter days*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *not welcome the blood of his prey, he waits for it."*

**Arob**: *"The air has the smell of beasts. The hunt is good today."*
**Nagrub**: *"Yes, mother. I'm eager to prove my skills today."*

## Notes

- Arob is depicted in *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")*, as the card [Dushnikh Yal Archer](/wiki/Legends:Dushnikh Yal Archer).
- Version 1.3.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") changes her 24/7 guard schedule, letting her sleep at night.

# Skyrim:Arondil

## Overview

| Arondil (RefID: 00037D81) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild") | | |

| Voice Type | [MaleElfHaughty](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleElfHaughty "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleElfHaughty") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [dunYngvildFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DunYngvildFaction "Skyrim:DunYngvildFaction") | | |

Arondil sitting at his throne

**Arondil** is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer"), necromancer, and necrophile. He originally lived in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), where he was studying techniques for reanimating the dead, and often spent time imagining secret encounters between himself and some of the local girls. A buyer is [interested](/wiki/Skyrim:Toying_With_The_Dead "Skyrim:Toying With The Dead") in [Arondil's four part journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Arondil's Journal").

However, when the local citizens found out he was performing experiments on the dead, he was exiled from Dawnstar and moved to [Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild"), an ancient Nord burial ground filled entirely with dead female draugr, which he used as subjects for his experiments.

In his time spent alone, his thoughts changed from the women in Dawnstar to his new dead women in Yngvild. He reanimated each subject into a state of total complacency, bending to his every whim. He ordered some to guard the island, while the rest acted as his personal entourage, never leaving his side.

When his guards caught and brought him a young milk maid from Dawnstar during one of his few moments alone with his favorite servant, she accused him of stalking her, although he claims that she was "nowhere near the most noticeable of maidens in town". Arondil, fearful of discovery and more unwanted guests, had her killed and began new experiments on her, excited by the chance to use fresh materials. The experiments were a complete success and she appeared more [phantasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild_Ghost "Skyrim:Yngvild Ghost") than reanimated dead. He ordered his servants to go and find any more subjects that may have become lost while wandering around Yngvild, continually improving and expanding his collection of undead slaves.

## Related Quests

- **[Toying With The Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Toying_With_The_Dead "Skyrim:Toying With The Dead")**: Retrieve a necromancer's journals for an interested buyer.

## Dialogue

When attacking, Arondil can say:

:   *"What? An intruder? Attack, my lovelies!"* (If you are male)
:   *"Ah, another plaything for my collection."* (If you are female)

If he is attacked by the ghosts (see [notes](#Notes)), he says:

:   *"What's happening? No! Leave me alone!"*

## Notes

- Sneaking into the final chamber of Yngvild unnoticed and removing the soul gem from the pedestal next to Arondil causes the ghosts near him to attack and kill him.
- If Arondil is raised with a raise dead spell ([dread zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Dread Zombie"), [dead thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Dead Thrall"), etc.), whenever he enters combat he will use the same line as when his ghosts attack him (see Dialogue, above).
- Arondil appears as a miniature in *[Call to Arms](/wiki/Call_to_Arms:Call_to_Arms "Call to Arms:Call to Arms")* as part of *[The Elder Scrolls: Call to Arms: Ghosts of Yngvild](/w/index.php?title=Call_to_Arms:The_Elder_Scrolls:_Call_to_Arms:_Ghosts_of_Yngvild&action=edit&redlink=1 "Call to Arms:The Elder Scrolls: Call to Arms: Ghosts of Yngvild (page does not exist)")* set.

## Bugs

- His corpse is permanent.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. His corpse will now clean up properly.
