Arrald Frozen-Heart

**Arrald Frozen-Heart** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Soldier_(class) "Skyrim:Soldier (class)") and the commander of the [Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp"). If [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") is taken by the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), he will relocate to the hold capital, [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), where he will spend most of the day in the [Jarl's longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Highmoon_Hall "Skyrim:Highmoon Hall") directing the war effort, and sleep in the [local guardhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Guardhouse "Skyrim:Guardhouse").

He wears a set of [Stormcloak officer armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Officer_Armor "Skyrim:Stormcloak Officer Armor"), [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Officer_Bracers "Skyrim:Stormcloak Officer Bracers"), and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Officer_Boots "Skyrim:Stormcloak Officer Boots"). He is equipped with a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") coupled with twelve [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), and a random iron or steel [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapon "Skyrim:Weapon").

## Dialogue

When you have not joined either the Stormcloaks or the Imperial Legion he can say:

:   **How does one join the Stormcloaks?**
:   *"[Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak")'s not running a social club. You don't join anything. Either you're a true son of Skyrim, or you're not. If you are, then you make your way to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and talk to the man himself. If you're not, well friend, you'd best walk away before this gets ugly."*

:   **How do you feel about this war?**
:   *"Skyrim is the birthplace of humanity. The birthplace of honor. And those snowbacked Imperials renounced both when they laid down before the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor"). Worse still, to pay for the privilege to keep his throne, the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") sells our very gods - [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos"), no less! - to the damn [elves](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf"). And what did [Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg") do? He and the [Jarls](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") who supported him? They took the Emperor's gold. Sold out their people for a slave master's "[peace treaty](/wiki/Lore:White-Gold_Concordat "Lore:White-Gold Concordat")." Ulfric did right killing him. Soon we'll rid Skyrim of elves, their bloody Justiciars, and the Jarls in their pockets. The whole damn lot of them. And we'll cleave through the Legion to get to them."*

:   **Why are you called Stormcloaks?**
:   *"At first they called us that to belittle our cause. But we gladly accept being named for Ulfric Stormcloak, the only true High King of Skyrim. We are the true sons and daughters of Skyrim, and Ulfric... he's the truest of us all. We fight to make our land great once more, to raise up strong, noble [thanes](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane"), and lay low false Jarls and the cowards who hide behind them. The sound of our fury is a storm about to break on the heads of our enemies. Our friendship, a cloak of true brotherhood for all who would wear it."*

## Bugs

- You may come across him standing outside the guardhouse all night long, locked out since he doesn't have a key.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=13063))

# Skyrim:Artifacts

## Overview

An **artifact** is a unique and unusually powerful magical item. Many of these artifacts in Skyrim have appeared in previous Elder Scrolls games, as listed on the [Lore article on artifacts](/wiki/Lore:Artifacts "Lore:Artifacts").

## Artifact Definition

The definition used for artifacts on this article is that the item must meet **all three** of the following requirements:

- Be unique in appearance.
- Only appear once in the game.
- Have a unique and useful enchantment.

None of these artifacts can be disenchanted to learn the enchantment. Some of them may be improved by [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing"). The material and perk relevant to each item is given below. Improving enchanted items requires the [Arcane Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Blacksmith "Skyrim:Arcane Blacksmith") perk. However, many artifacts do not have an applicable perk that allows improvement past *flawless* quality without a Smithing skill of greater than 100.

Many of the artifacts are of [Daedric](/wiki/Lore:Daedra "Lore:Daedra") origin. These items are formed from the essence of a [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes"), providing the items with their power. Nineteen *Daedric Artifacts* are available in the game; most are rewards for the [Daedric Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Quests "Skyrim:Daedric Quests").

In addition to the Daedric artifacts, there are also other unique relics such as the masks worn by the undead [Dragon Priests](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest"). There are nine of these scattered across Skyrim, each with unique powers and enchantments.

Please see the [following page](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Quests#Achievements "Skyrim:Daedric Quests") for information about what items count as Daedric Artifacts for the following achievements/trophies:

-  **Daedric Influence** (10 points/Bronze) — Acquire a Daedric Artifact
-  **Oblivion Walker** (30 points/Silver) — Collect 15 Daedric Artifacts

This article only lists items that fit the definition of an artifact.

- For items that are leveled, see [Leveled Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Items "Skyrim:Leveled Items").
- For items that do not fit all of the requirements of an Artifact and are not leveled, see [Unique Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Unique_Items "Skyrim:Unique Items").
- For unique items that are quest-related, see [Quest Items](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items "Skyrim:Quest Items").

The [Spear of Bitter Mercy](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_of_Bitter_Mercy "Skyrim:Spear of Bitter Mercy")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins") is an [unobtainable](/wiki/Skyrim:Unobtainable_Items "Skyrim:Unobtainable Items") artifact that is used by the [goblin](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblin "Skyrim:Goblin") [Gogh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gogh "Skyrim:Gogh").

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **[Weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapon_Artifacts "Skyrim:Weapon Artifacts")** | **[Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_Artifacts "Skyrim:Armor Artifacts")** | **[Clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing_Artifacts "Skyrim:Clothing Artifacts")** |
| [Daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapon_Artifacts#Daggers "Skyrim:Weapon Artifacts")  [Maces](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapon_Artifacts#Maces "Skyrim:Weapon Artifacts")  [Staves](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapon_Artifacts#Staves "Skyrim:Weapon Artifacts")  [Swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapon_Artifacts#Swords "Skyrim:Weapon Artifacts")  [War Axes](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapon_Artifacts#War_Axes "Skyrim:Weapon Artifacts")  [Battleaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapon_Artifacts#Battleaxes "Skyrim:Weapon Artifacts")  [Bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapon_Artifacts#Bows "Skyrim:Weapon Artifacts")  [Greatswords](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapon_Artifacts#Greatswords "Skyrim:Weapon Artifacts")  [Warhammers](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapon_Artifacts#Warhammers "Skyrim:Weapon Artifacts") | [Armor (Cuirasses)](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_Artifacts#Armor_.28Cuirasses.29 "Skyrim:Armor Artifacts")  [Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_Artifacts#Boots "Skyrim:Armor Artifacts")  [Gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_Artifacts#Gauntlets "Skyrim:Armor Artifacts")  [Helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_Artifacts#Helmets "Skyrim:Armor Artifacts")  [Shields](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_Artifacts#Shields "Skyrim:Armor Artifacts")  [Dragon Priest Masks](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_Artifacts#Dragon_Priest_Masks "Skyrim:Armor Artifacts") | [Amulets](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing_Artifacts#Amulets "Skyrim:Clothing Artifacts")  [Circlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing_Artifacts#Circlets "Skyrim:Clothing Artifacts")  [Rings](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing_Artifacts#Rings "Skyrim:Clothing Artifacts")  [Robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing_Artifacts#Robes "Skyrim:Clothing Artifacts") |

# Skyrim:Arvel the Swift

## Overview

| Arvel the Swift (RefID: 00039655) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)") | | |

Arvel the Swift

Arvel caught in a web

**Arvel the Swift** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(class) "Skyrim:Thief (class)") who stole a unique [golden claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw") from the [Riverwood Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood_Trader "Skyrim:Riverwood Trader") in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), and then retreated to [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)"). You might be [tasked](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Golden_Claw "Skyrim:The Golden Claw") with recovering the golden claw from him by the [owner](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius") of the shop in question, or you might be tasked with finding the owner of the claw, if found by other means.

Arvel wears a set of [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), including matching pairs of [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"), as well as a [hide helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Helmet "Skyrim:Hide Helmet"). He also carries an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") with him, as well as a spare [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"). Upon his death, his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvel%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Arvel's Journal") and the golden claw can also be found on him.

## Related Quests

- **[The Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Golden_Claw "Skyrim:The Golden Claw")**: A [shopkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius") wants you to retrieve his [prized possession](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw") from a bandit.
- **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)")**: Retrieve the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone").

### The Golden Claw

As you near the webbing-filled room, you will start to hear Arvel calling out, initially assuming you're one of his cohorts:

:   *"Is... is someone coming? Is that you Harknir? Bjorn? Soling? I know I ran ahead with the claw, but I need help! You. Over here!"*

He will also continue yelling as you approach further:

:   *"Hey, over here!"*
:   *"Get me out of here!"*
:   *"Don't leave me, for [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay")'s sake!"*
:   *"Help me! Help!"*
:   *"Help me out of here!"*
:   *"Get me down. Get me down!"*

As soon as you enter the room, a giant [wounded frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Wounded_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Wounded Frostbite Spider") descends to the floor. This will make Arvel state:

:   *"No. Not again. Help!"*

Arvel will then start to panic and yell out remarks such as;

:   *"Ah, kill it. Kill it!"*
:   *"Get it away from me. Get it away!"*
:   *"Don't let it get me. Help!"*
:   *"Agh. Agh!"*
:   *"Keep it away from me!"*

He can also be heard yelling:

:   *"Where are you going? Come back!"*
:   *"Wait, come back!"*
:   *"Noooo!"*
:   *"Aaaaagh!"*

Once the spider has been defeated, he will be overjoyed and say one of the following lines:

:   *"Is it over?*"
:   *"Is it dead?"*
:   *"Is it safe now?"*

When you greet him for the first time, his response will depend on whether you have killed the spider or not. If you have not yet killed it, he will say:

:   *"What? Who are you? Oh, never mind. Cut me down before that thing gets us!"*

If you've dispatched it already, he will instead thank you:

:   *"You did it. You killed it. Now cut me down before anything else shows up."*

Either way, you can then follow up by asking him about the claw:

:   **Where's the golden claw?**
:   *"Yes, the claw. I know how it works. The claw, the markings, the door in the Hall of Stories. I know how they all fit together! Help me down, and I'll show you. You won't believe the [power](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") the Nords have hidden there."*

:   :   **Hand over the claw first!**
    :   *"Does it look like I can move? You have to cut me down, first."*

:   :   **Fine. Let me see if I can cut you down.**
    :   *"Sweet breath of Arkay, thank you."*

As you begin to cut him down he will say;

:   *"That's it. Keep hacking at it."*
:   *"Don't stop. Keep cutting."*
:   *"It's coming loose. I can feel it."*

If you start leaving before he's fully freed will have him yelling at you:

:   *"Cut me down, or you'll never get the claw!"*
:   *"Where are you... get me down from this!"*

However, once you free him it becomes clear that he has no intention of giving the claw to you. He will instead run towards the next room and brush you aside with;

:   *"You fool! Why should I share the treasure with anyone?"*
:   *"Sorry, but I have a treasure to get to..."*
:   *"So long "friend." Ha ha ha!"*
:   *"I'm too swift for you!"*

Once he reaches the next room full of [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), he will try to defend himself, but usually dies. If you save him from the undead, he will be killed by the [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") trap or the [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") trap. If you get too close, he will also turn hostile and start fighting you directly. Regardless, it is impossible to keep him alive.

## Notes

- At the entrance to the barrow you may hear two bandits talk about Arvel:
  - **Bandit #1**: *"So we're just supposed to sit here while Arvel runs off with that golden claw?"*
  - **Bandit #2**: *"That dark elf wants to go on ahead, let him. Better than us risking our necks."*
  - **Bandit #1**: *"What if Arvel doesn't come back? I want my share from that claw!"*
  - **Bandit #2**: *"Just shut it and keep an eye out for trouble."*
- Talking to Arvel after freeing him will cause a "This person is busy." message to appear on the top left of the screen.
- Arvel was featured in pre-release videos of the game, such as for E3 and QuakeCon. However, a slightly different version of Arvel was shown in those demo videos which still exists in the files (BaseID `00099991`). The most notable differences include the fact that this version doesn't have a unique face, instead using the default Dark Elf male face, and that both the claw and journal can always be found in his inventory. In the final game, they're added to his inventory via script upon his death.

# Skyrim:Asbjorn Fire-Tamer

## Overview

| Asbjorn Fire-Tamer (RefID: 00019DF3) | | | |

| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 6 | Class | [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith_(class) "Skyrim:Blacksmith (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00019DF3 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00019DF2 |

Asbjorn resting in the blacksmith shop

**Asbjorn Fire-Tamer** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:VendorBlacksmith "Skyrim:VendorBlacksmith") working for [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund"), the owner of [the Scorched Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Scorched_Hammer "Skyrim:The Scorched Hammer") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). In the event of Balimund's demise, Asbjorn will assume the role of blacksmith at the Scorched Hammer. Asbjorn grew up in the [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage") under the 'care' of [Grelod](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind") until Balimund, seeing some spark of talent, took him in and began training him in blacksmithing.

Asbjorn sleeps in the southwestern room of the shop every night between midnight and 6am and always starts the day with a two-hour breakfast with Balimund. His workday starts at 8am and, while Balimund works the forge outside, Asbjorn stays inside where he divides his time between working with the various tools in the basement and relaxing in the upstairs area. When the store closes at 8pm Asbjorn takes a two-hour dinner and then strolls around until his bedtime at midnight. If Balimund dies, Asbjorn will take over the shop and the duties outside at the forge between 8am and 8pm but will otherwise keep his old routine.

Asbjorn wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261bd "Skyrim:Clothing"). He is equipped with a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") which can be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality, and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Scorched_Hammer_Key "Skyrim:The Scorched Hammer Key") to the store, as well as a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Spread the Love](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love")**: Distribute religious [literature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara") to the citizens of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

### Spread the Love

:   **Here, brother. Blessings of Mara upon you.**
:   *"Oh, well thank you. I'll try and read this if I can."*

## Dialogue

His potential greetings are:

:   *"Have you met Balimund? I'm his apprentice. He's teaching me all about being a blacksmith."*
:   *"I used to live at the orphanage here in Riften. Grelod said my ma and da left me there when I was a baby... that they didn't want me."*
:   *"Balimund took me in and has been so kind to me. I don't know why, but he thinks I can be a great blacksmith like him."*
:   *"At first I don't know why he picked me. I never even held a hammer in my life! But the first time I picked it up, it just felt right!"*
:   *"Folks in town say that Balimund is the greatest blacksmith in all of [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel"). I hope I can live up to that some day and make him proud of me."*

Should anything happen to Balimund, Asbjorn will take over the business and use phrases like:

:   *"Here to purchase some armor or a weapon?"*
:   *"How can I help you today?"*

When spoken to directly:

:   **You look young for a blacksmith**
:   *"I was apprenticed to Balimund before he died. He taught me everything I know about forging armor and weapons. Balimund pulled me out of Grelod's orphanage when I was just a child. I don't know what he saw in me, but I was glad to get out of there. I've spent years watching his techniques and learning his tricks. Sadly, I don't think I'll ever be as talented as he was."*

When exiting conversation:

:   *"Thanks for your business."*
:   *"It was nice to meet you."*

Asgeir Snow-Shod

**Asgeir Snow-Shod** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") living in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). He works at the [Black-Briar Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery") as [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar")'s investor and partner. His parents are [Nura](/wiki/Skyrim:Nura_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Nura Snow-Shod") and [Vulwulf Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vulwulf_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Vulwulf Snow-Shod"), and his brother is [Unmid](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmid_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Unmid Snow-Shod"). He also had a sister, Lilija, who was killed while serving as Battle Maiden for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").

His family has connections to the Stormcloaks and his [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") to someone with [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") connections is seen as a step towards reconciliation. He is marked essential until he becomes the new husband of [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") in the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest.

Asgeir wears a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes#00086991 "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots#00086993 "Skyrim:Fine Boots"). He is equipped with a leveled [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") which can be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality. He carries two leveled [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems"), a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_House_Key "Skyrim:Snow-Shod House Key") to [his manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow-Shod_Manor "Skyrim:Snow-Shod Manor"), and a selection of [upper-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

He will drop [his wedding band](/wiki/Skyrim:Asgeir%27s_Wedding_Band "Skyrim:Asgeir's Wedding Band") if killed. If he is not killed during the related quest, the band will remain in his inventory unequipped and can be pickpocketed from him afterwards.

## Related Quests

- **[Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death")**: Assassinate [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") at her own wedding.
- **[Spread the Love](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love")**: Distribute religious [literature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara") to the citizens of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

### Bound Until Death

Asgeir and Vittoria at their wedding

During this quest, Asgeir will be found in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") as the proud groom to Vittoria Vici. When you approach him, he will greet you with:

:   *"Make sure to get yourself something to drink."*
:   *"You hungry? There's plenty of food. Eat up, now."*

He may also jokingly say either:

:   *"Now now, fella. Let's not get too close to my new bride, eh?"* (If you are male)
:   *"Well aren't you a pretty thing? Should my new bride by*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *worried? He he he he."* (If you are female)

You can congratulate him and mention how it's quite a day, which he will agree:

:   **Congratulations. Quite the day, hmm?**
:   *"The best. Vittoria's a good woman. Any man should be so lucky. I know my father's not happy about me marrying an Imperial, but that's his problem."*

As Vittoria Vici lies dead, the now-widowed Asgeir can be found screaming:

:   *"My wife is dead! Dead!"*

Should he survive the wedding, he will now detest you for murdering Vittoria.

### Spread the Love

If you [give](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love") him a [religious missive](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara"):

:   **Here, brother. Blessings of Mara upon you.**
:   *"Not really my usual read, but I'll give it a try."*

## Dialogue

He shows that he is charitable, as he gives a coin to Riften's beggars, saying:

:   *"Of course, here. Be well."* to [Edda](/wiki/Skyrim:Edda "Skyrim:Edda") and *"Absolutely. Here you are. Be well."* to [Snilf](/wiki/Skyrim:Snilf "Skyrim:Snilf").

Asgeir will greet you with:

:   *"Sorry, I'm afraid I can't help you much right now... I'm currently in mourning."*
:   *"You've caught me at a bad time. I've lost someone dear to me."*
:   *"Yes? What is it?"*

Ending conversation with him will have him say:

:   *"It's been good talking to you."*

When spoken to directly you can ask questions:

:   **May I ask why you're in mourning?**
:   *"It was my sister, Lilija. She served as a Battle Maiden with the Stormcloaks. We recently heard she'd been killed... I... I find it difficult to talk about. Perhaps you'd be better off speaking to my parents about it. Anyway, I'm glad my work at the Black-Briar Meadery keeps me busy. Helps me keep my mind off of things."*

:   **You're involved with the meadery?**
:   *"Yes, actually. I'm partnered with Maven Black-Briar. I put up a chunk of the gold she needed to get the place off the ground. We've been staggeringly successful so far. In fact, I'm almost surprised how quickly she's generated business for us. My name may not be on the label, but some of my blood, sweat and tears are in every drop. Uh, figuratively of course."*

:   **Tell me about your parents.**
:   *"My father was a Stormcloak soldier in his younger days. Now he just walks the streets spewing his hatred and propaganda. My mother is the Priestess of [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos"). She tends to the shrine and teaches his ways. I'm just not so sure she's delivering the right message."*
:   **Are you at odds with them?**
:   *"Don't mistake my political beliefs as a substitute for my family values. They're still my parents, and I love them dearly.
    I just think they've let my sister's death skew their outlook on [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") and what he really brings to the table with [this war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). I'm not so certain that Ulfric's intentions are as noble as they think. I think Ulfric cares about Ulfric and the rest is a smokescreen.
    I'd... appreciate if you kept my opinion between us. The last thing I want to do is have my parents 'lose' another child."*

## Conversations

At [the Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb"), Asgeir and his father can be heard conversing:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Asgeir**: | *"I'm sorry you disapprove, father. But I've made up my mind. I'm not a warrior, I'm a businessman."* |
| **Vulwulf**: | *"The only reason you have the gold for your 'business' is because I gave it to you."* |
| **Asgeir**: | *"I'll pay you back, if it means that much."* |
| **Vulwulf**: | *"It's not about the coin, it's about honoring your legacy by picking up arms and keeping this land free. The sooner you remember that, the better."* |
|  |
| **Vulwulf**: | *"Drink up, my boy! Drink to those who have fallen! May their souls find their way to [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)")!"* |
| **Asgeir**: | *"Take it easy, father. You're making a scene."* |
| **Vulwulf**: | *"I'll rest easy when we've driven every last Imperial pig back across the [Jerall Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Jerall_Mountains "Skyrim:Jerall Mountains")! Now, do me the honor I deserve as your father and drink up!"* |
| **Asgeir**: | *"Yes... father."* |

At their house, the family may discuss about Asgeir's profession:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Nura**: | *"How are things at the [Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery"), my dear?"* |
| **Vulwulf**: | *"Not this again..."* |
| **Nura**: | *"Hush, Vulwulf... let the boy speak."* |
| **Asgeir**: | *"It's going very well, actually. The war hasn't even slowed down our production or shipping at all."* |
| **Vulwulf**: | *"Of course it is. That's what happens when you're partners with a corrupt [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") whore like Maven."* |
| **Nura**: | *"Vulwulf! The Empire may be our enemy, but Asgeir is still our son and we're a long way from [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil")."* |
| **Asgeir**: | *"Father, I promise you, this has nothing to do with Empires or politics. It's just business."* |
| **Vulwulf**: | *"It has everything to do with politics. Asgeir my son, you have so much to learn."* |

Ash Zombie

**Ash Zombies** are [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") victims who have been transformed into disfigured [ash creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Creatures "Skyrim:Ash Creatures") by [Erden Relvel](/wiki/Skyrim:Erden_Relvel "Skyrim:Erden Relvel") using the power of the [Mask of Dagoth Ur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Dagoth_Ur "Skyrim:Mask of Dagoth Ur"). As part of this transformation, Erden removes the soft tissue of the upper face down to the bone, as Dagoth Ur did. However, Erden goes a step further and the zombies' lips are ritualistically stitched closed. The zombies have no dialogue as a result.

Ash Zombies are relatively weak enemies, as they only attack with their fists. They can be encountered attacking [Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear") and guarding Erden Relvel at the [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)") graveyard, and a group of them can also attack you randomly as a [world interaction](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions").

## Related Quests

- **[Ashen Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Heart "Skyrim:Ashen Heart")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Find out [who](/wiki/Skyrim:Erden_Relvel "Skyrim:Erden Relvel") attacked the temple and retrieve their [unique mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Dagoth_Ur "Skyrim:Mask of Dagoth Ur").

## Bugs

- Ash Zombies may spawn in your house and become hostile if they find you there.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.342, fixes this bug.

Ashen Heart

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the Matriarch's note
2. Read [Priest Arthamis' Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest_Arthamis%27_Note "Skyrim:Priest Arthamis' Note")
3. Use the mannequins to solve the armory room puzzle. The solution (left to right) is: Mask of Sotha Sil, Mask of Almalexia, Mask of Vivec.
4. Kill [Erden Relvel](/wiki/Skyrim:Erden_Relvel "Skyrim:Erden Relvel") and retrieve [Mask of Dagoth Ur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Dagoth_Ur "Skyrim:Mask of Dagoth Ur").

## Detailed Walkthrough

After dealing with the ash zombie attack, speak to the Matriarch:

:   **Is there anything I can do to stop these attacks?**
:   *"Of course. It's all in this note."*

She will then hand you a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Matriarch_Drevlan%27s_Note "Skyrim:Matriarch Drevlan's Note"). After reading it you will have to head to the armory and pick up and read [Priest Arthamis' Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest_Arthamis%27_Note "Skyrim:Priest Arthamis' Note").

### Armory Puzzle

Correct order

The solution for the armory puzzle can be deduced from the banner above the locked gate. The solution (left to right) is: Mask of Sotha Sil, Mask of Almalexia, Mask of Vivec. The other mannequins are irrelevant.

Open the chest to find [Hopesfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hopesfire "Skyrim:Hopesfire") and [Erden Relvel's note](/wiki/Skyrim:Erden_Relvel%27s_Note "Skyrim:Erden Relvel's Note"), read the note and you will have to then travel to the graveyard of [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn").

You will have to kill the ash zombies and Erden Relvel, you can then loot his body for the [Mask of Dagoth Ur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Dagoth_Ur "Skyrim:Mask of Dagoth Ur"), the [Robe of the Lich](/wiki/Skyrim:Robe_of_the_Lich "Skyrim:Robe of the Lich") and a [Fahlbtharz Forge Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz_Forge_Gem "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz Forge Gem").

## Bugs

- Just adding the masks to the mannequins may not result in the door opening. In this case, removing the other armor from one or more of the mannequins may trigger the door to open.

- The mannequin might spawn with 2 set of identical armor where one is invisible this can cause the corresponding mask and armor to be marked as Quest item (if removed) and unable to re-equip on the mannequin ( You can drop the item but you can't equip it and it somehow prevent the right mask to be equipped on the mannequin , On "MAKE A QUICK SAVE BEFORE INTERACTING WITH ANY MANNEQUIN " and open console and select the mannequin and perform a "resetinventory" then equip the mask on the mannequin you shouldn't need to do this for the one in the middle just equip the mask on the display case on it but do the same if it's doesn't work.

## Quest Stages

| Ashen Heart (ccASVSSE001\_QuestD) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | The temple was attacked by Ash Zombies, and the Matriarch has handed me a note that may provide more clues on who is responsible for the attack. *Objective 5:* Read the Matriarch's note |
| 10 |  | I should investigate the temple armory and look for clues as well as pick up any valuable weapons or armor that may suit my needs. *Objective 10:* Look for clues in the armory |
| 15 |  | Inside the temple armory, I found a note that implies something important is hidden in the chest on the rear wall. The note implies that to open it, I need to place masks on the appropriate mannequins. *Objective 15:* Use the mannequins to solve the armory room puzzle |
| 20 |  | After solving the armory puzzle, I now have access to the treasure behind the portcullis. I should open it and see what I can learn. *Objective 20:* Examine the chest |
| 30 |  | After solving the armory puzzle, I now have access to the treasure behind the portcullis. Inside I found a note whose contents may provide further information. *Objective 30:* Read Erden Relvel's Note |
| 40 |  | After solving the armory puzzle, I now have access to the treasure behind the portcullis. Inside I found a note from a priest of Dagoth Ur. *Objective 40:* Kill the Priest of Dagoth Ur |
| 90 |  | After solving the armory puzzle, I now have access to the treasure behind the portcullis. Inside I found a note from a renegade priest. I located and defeated the priest and can now take the Mask of Dagoth Ur from his corpse. *Objective 50:* Retrieve the Mask of Dagoth Ur |
| 100 | ☑ | After solving the armory puzzle, I now have access to the treasure behind the portcullis. Inside I found a note from a renegade priest. I located and defeated the priest and took the Mask of Dagoth Ur off his corpse. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 50, 60, 70, 80.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccASVSSE001_QuestD stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccASVSSE001_QuestD`.

Ashfall's Tear

**Ashfall's Tear** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") containing a hidden [Tribunal Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple") shrine to the goddess [Almalexia](/wiki/Lore:Almalexia "Lore:Almalexia"). It contains only one zone, *[Ashfall's Tear](#Ashfall.27s_Tear)*.

The cultists within are outcasts from [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") society, persecuted by the [New Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple "Skyrim:Temple") for their heretical beliefs. They will be hostile towards you, although it is possible to infiltrate and later join the cult during the quest [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |

## Related Quests

- **[Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Decide the fate of a [heretical cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple").
- **[Trueflame](/wiki/Skyrim:Trueflame_(quest) "Skyrim:Trueflame (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Restore power to the Dwarven Forge in [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz") to restore a [powerful artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Trueflame "Skyrim:Trueflame").
- **[Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Ambush a meeting to retrieve the [Mask of Vivec](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Vivec "Skyrim:Mask of Vivec").
- **[Careless Curation](/wiki/Skyrim:Careless_Curation "Skyrim:Careless Curation")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Find the missing Curate to retrieve the [Mask of Sotha Sil](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Sotha_Sil "Skyrim:Mask of Sotha Sil").
- **[Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Spread the word of the Goddess [Almalexia](/wiki/Lore:Almalexia "Lore:Almalexia").
- **[Ashen Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Heart "Skyrim:Ashen Heart")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Find out [who](/wiki/Skyrim:Erden_Relvel "Skyrim:Erden Relvel") attacked the temple and retrieve their [unique mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Dagoth_Ur "Skyrim:Mask of Dagoth Ur").

### Exterior

The cave can be reached by following the slope east of [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine"), then turning left until you reach the mountainside. An [emerald geode](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald_Geode "Skyrim:Emerald Geode") can be found north of the cave.

### Ashfall's Tear

Walk along the corridor, there's a door and a pull chain, you need rotate 3 pillars to the correct position and pull the chain to open the door, the opened door can be closed again after respawned. After the door is a long winding downslope to the door of the heretic temple, the door is guarded by two [Ordinators](/wiki/Skyrim:Ordinator "Skyrim:Ordinator"). There's a Shrine of Almalexia(+10 Heavy Armor, +10% One-handed weapon damage) in front of the temple door. The area behind the door can be seen as a chamber, there are some plants, ebony ore and heartstone ore in it. Walk along the chamber corridor, you will come into a large hall, within it are [Temple Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_Priest "Skyrim:Temple Priest"), [Matriarch Drevlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Matriarch_Drevlan "Skyrim:Matriarch Drevlan") and 4 potential followers [Hand Ethra Mavandas](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Ethra_Mavandas "Skyrim:Hand Ethra Mavandas") a one-handed warrior, [Hand Kydren Indobar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kydren_Indobar "Skyrim:Hand Kydren Indobar") a one-handed warrior with [Hand Indobar's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Indobar%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Hand Indobar's Journal"), [Vesparth the Toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Vesparth_the_Toe "Skyrim:Vesparth the Toe") a double dual warrior with [Cleaver of St. Felms](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleaver_of_St._Felms "Skyrim:Cleaver of St. Felms") and [Vesparth's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Vesparth%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Vesparth's Journal"), [Watchman Sindras](/wiki/Skyrim:Watchman_Sindras "Skyrim:Watchman Sindras") an electric mage.

There's are 7 rooms in total including the large hall, the exit where you come is to the west.

- To the north is a garden, a [Caretaker Ineril](/wiki/Skyrim:Caretaker_Ineril "Skyrim:Caretaker Ineril") may be within if you have delived the translated propaganda letter to [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") during [Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs").
- To the east are 4 rooms.
  - East-north is a sculpture room, within are Shrine of Sotha Sil(+10 Magicka, +5% Magicka Regeneration) and Shrine of Vivec(5% better price, 5% harder to detect), [Sculptor Visthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sculptor_Visthar "Skyrim:Sculptor Visthar") is always sculpting in it, [Sculptor Visthar's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Sculptor_Visthar%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Sculptor Visthar's Journal") is on the rack.
  - East-east is a upslope circling road to a higher room, it's where Matriarch Drevlan stays during night, there's [Matriarch Drevlan's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Matriarch_Drevlan%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Matriarch Drevlan's Journal") on the desk, west of the small room is a high platform, it looks like a speech podium, from which you can overlook the large hall.
  - East-south is a smithing and resting room with 4 beds.
  - East of smithing room is the armory room, which can only be accessed after completing all three concurrent tasks during [Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)"), inside the armory room are 6 display cases and 7 mannequins, [Fahlbtharz Forge Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_Items#Fahlbtharz_Forge_Gem "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal Items"), unique mask [Mask of Almalexia](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Almalexia "Skyrim:Mask of Almalexia"), unique weapons [Light of Day](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_of_Day "Skyrim:Light of Day"), [Magebane](/wiki/Skyrim:Magebane "Skyrim:Magebane") and [Skull Crusher](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull_Crusher "Skyrim:Skull Crusher") are in the display cases. There's a portcullis at the east of the armory room which need be opened by a mask riddle during [Ashen Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Heart "Skyrim:Ashen Heart"), behind the portcullis is a chest, the unique weapon [Hopesfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hopesfire "Skyrim:Hopesfire") and [Erden Relvel's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Erden_Relvel%27s_Note "Skyrim:Erden Relvel's Note") are in the chest.
- To the south is a alchemy and enchanting room with an Alchemy Lab and an Arcane Enchanter, there're also a lot of potions on 5 racks, [Priest Drureth](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest_Drureth "Skyrim:Priest Drureth") lives in it, [Priest Drureth's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest_Drureth%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Priest Drureth's Journal") is on the desk, [Curate Melita](/wiki/Skyrim:Curate_Melita "Skyrim:Curate Melita") also lives in it should she survives in [Careless Curation](/wiki/Skyrim:Careless_Curation "Skyrim:Careless Curation").

## Notes

- This cell exists even without Ghosts of the Tribunal installed as `ccPlaceholder16Interior01` "Creation Club Cell".

## Bugs

- Even after you have befriended the Temple, the pillar door may close and the first interior door may lock again, with no in-game option but to pick the lock.
- Summoning [Hilda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilda "Skyrim:Hilda") or any of the pets added by the [Pets of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") within Ashfall's Tear will cause the cultists to become hostile and attempt to attack the creatures (but not you) relentlessly. This can cause congestion in the narrow passages, making it difficult to exit the temple.

Ashfallow Citadel

**Ashfallow Citadel** is a small Imperial [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Highpoint Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Highpoint_Tower "Skyrim:Highpoint Tower") and northwest of the [Sun Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Stone "Skyrim:Sun Stone") being used as a base of operations by the [Morag Tong](/wiki/Skyrim:Morag_Tong "Skyrim:Morag Tong").

## Related Quests

- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").
- **[Served Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Served_Cold "Skyrim:Served Cold")**: Save [Councilor Morvayn](/wiki/Skyrim:Lleril_Morvayn "Skyrim:Lleril Morvayn") from an assassination plot.

### Exterior

The easiest approach to the fort is from the south. If you are coming here on the quest [Served Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Served_Cold "Skyrim:Served Cold"), as you climb two flights of partly buried stairs, you will find both [Redoran Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard_(dead) "Skyrim:Redoran Guard (dead)") dead on the stairs and will be attacked by two [Morag Tong assassins](/wiki/Skyrim:Morag_Tong_Assassin "Skyrim:Morag Tong Assassin"). A third flight of stairs ascends to the outer wall of the fort, with an archway in the wall to the north. The wall is in very poor condition, with large parts of it collapsed and partly buried in ash. On the west side of the fort are two [heart stone deposits](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone_Deposit "Skyrim:Heart Stone Deposit"). The entrance door is in the small central tower. It is possible to reach the roof of the tower by using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") and clever jumping; however, there is nothing up there of interest.

### Ashfallow Citadel

The entrance leads into a circular room partly filled with ash, debris, and unlootable [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). To the west is a set of shelves holding an [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox"). Beyond the broken section of wall to the right of the shelves is a small room containing a lootable skeleton and a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"). To the east the path continues down a wide flight of curved stairs typical of Imperial forts.

At the bottom of the stairs is a room guarded by a Morag Tong assassin, with a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") by the east wall. To the southeast, a natural tunnel descends to the south to a north-south corridor lit by two chandeliers and patrolled by a Morag Tong assassin. A wall of bars blocks further progress a short distance ahead. Before the bars, an open door is on the right, and a doorway is on the left. Any fighting with the first Morag Tong assassin will alert a second in the room beyond this doorway, as well as three more assassins behind the bars blocking the corridor. Note that Morag Tong assassins use [invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_(spell) "Skyrim:Invisibility (spell)") to mask themselves; [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") or the [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") shout are very helpful in these instances. At least one of the assassins behind the bars will be an archer. You can use the open door on the right to shield yourself while killing all three assassins with a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), but ranged area magic will be blocked by the bars.

Beyond the door on the right is a barracks containing six unowned beds and three sets of shelves. The shelves hold ten random books, an [elven dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), two pairs of [chitin heavy boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Chitin_Heavy_Boots "Skyrim:Chitin Heavy Boots"), two pairs of [Morag Tong boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Morag_Tong_Boots "Skyrim:Morag Tong Boots"), a [Morag Tong hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Morag_Tong_Hood "Skyrim:Morag Tong Hood"), two [chitin heavy helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Chitin_Heavy_Helmet "Skyrim:Chitin Heavy Helmet"), a pair of [Morag Tong bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Morag_Tong_Bracers "Skyrim:Morag Tong Bracers"), three [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a [chitin heavy armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Chitin_Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Chitin Heavy Armor") cuirass, a [Morag Tong armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Morag_Tong_Armor "Skyrim:Morag Tong Armor") cuirass, a random enchanted [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), and an adept-locked [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Safe "Skyrim:Safe"). Returning to the corridor, on the right along the west wall just past the barracks door is another set of shelves holding nine more random books.

Beyond the doorway on the left is a room containing a table along the east wall set with an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") and an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"). A random filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and a random empty soul gem are behind the arcane enchanter, and an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") and two random potions of [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), or [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") are between the arcane enchanter and the alchemy lab. Along the north wall is a sideboard holding a random potion of healing, magicka, or stamina, a filled [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), an empty petty soul gem, an empty random soul gem, and a random book. Along the south wall is a cupboard holding six random books, an empty petty soul gem, and a filled petty soul gem, with three ingredient barrels to the right of the cupboard. Between the barrels and the doorway is a pull chain that lowers the bars and allows you to continue along the corridor.

Just past the bars the corridor briefly rises, with a wall of crossed bars blocking further progress a short distance ahead. A Morag Tong assassin stands guard to the right. At the top of the rise, a door is on the right. Beyond the door is a short dead-end passage containing five [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") and a pull chain that operates the vertical bars blocking the corridor. On the right along the west wall just past the door is a cupboard holding seven random books and an elven dagger, with an ingredient barrel to the left of the cupboard. Opposite the cupboard, a door on the left leads to a training room, where three more Morag Tong assassins and [Mirri Severin](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirri_Severin "Skyrim:Mirri Severin") (see [notes](#Notes)) are working out. Four chairs, one of which has a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") on top, are set around a raised central platform with three sparring dummies. Along the east wall at the back of the room is a row of six weapon racks holding a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe") and an enchanted [elven mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Mace "Skyrim:Elven Mace"). Returning to the corridor, on the left on the east wall just past the training room door is another pull chain that operates the horizontal bars blocking the corridor, with an ingredient barrel to the right of the pull chain.

Past the second set of bars is a sideboard on the right holding an elven dagger and four random books. Past the sideboard, a total of eight [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") littering the floor activate a series of three [spike walls](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") and several sets of [spear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") coming out from the walls. The corridor ahead is again blocked, this time by a wall of bars and a wooden gate. The two pull chains to operate the bars and gate are on the back of the two pillars in the small alcove on the right.

This opens the way to the final room. On the right on the east wall just before the doorway where the gate had been is a pull chain that operates the bars behind you. Through the doorway is a large circular room, with wooden planking on the floor covering deep water except for an open area in the center where stairs descend into the water. Two Morag Tong assassins, [Vendil Severin](/wiki/Skyrim:Vendil_Severin "Skyrim:Vendil Severin"), and his wife [Tilisu Severin](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilisu_Severin "Skyrim:Tilisu Severin") (see [notes](#Notes)) occupy the room. Along the south wall at the back of the room is a boss-level chest. Three lootable skeletons float in the water. Two unlootable skeletons are also shackled to the wall in the water; however, even opening the shackles does not release them.

You must exit the fort the way you came in, as there is no shortcut exit.

## Notes

- The tunnel entrance will be blocked by a wall if you haven't started the quest Served Cold.
- Mirri and Tilisu Severin will not appear at the fort if they are already dead.
- An East Empire Company strongbox can be found west of the fort at a small [reaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") camp across a stream.
- Another East Empire Company strongbox can be found north of the fort behind a barred wooden gate at the source of the stream.

# Skyrim:Aslfur

## Overview

| Aslfur (RefID: 0001AA68) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") | | |
| Location | [Highmoon Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Highmoon_Hall "Skyrim:Highmoon Hall") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 6 | Class | [Ranger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranger_(class) "Skyrim:Ranger (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001AA68 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000135E7 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 100 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 75 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor")**, [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery"), [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed"), [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionHjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionHjaalmarch "Skyrim:CrimeFactionHjaalmarch"); [Imperial Government](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Government "Skyrim:Imperial Government"); [Morthal Longhouse Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal_Longhouse_Faction_(Both_Sides) "Skyrim:Morthal Longhouse Faction (Both Sides)"); [Ruling Government](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruling_Government "Skyrim:Ruling Government"); [TownMorthalFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownMorthalFaction "Skyrim:TownMorthalFaction") | | |

Aslfur in Highmoon Hall

**Aslfur** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [ranger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranger_(class) "Skyrim:Ranger (class)") who serves as [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward") to [Idgrod Ravencrone](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"). He is also her husband, and the father of [Idgrod the Younger](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_the_Younger "Skyrim:Idgrod the Younger") and [Joric](/wiki/Skyrim:Joric "Skyrim:Joric").

His normal schedule consists of him waking up at 7am, and wandering around Highmoon Hall for most of the day, often warming up by the fire. Then at 7pm, he'll head to [Moorside Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Moorside_Inn "Skyrim:Moorside Inn") and stay there for four hours. After that, he'll head home and finally go to sleep at midnight. However, if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") take Hjaalmarch, he'll be permanently relocated to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") where he'll stay in the basement twenty-four hours a day.

He wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006c1da "Skyrim:Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots"). He is equipped with an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

He seems to be protective of his wife, with his greetings being:

:   *"If you've business with the Jarl, I'd ask that you speak to me first."*
:   *"I do what I can to see that Idgrod's time isn't wasted, and that she only has to deal with important matters."*
:   *"Too many bother my wife with their petty problems, and then don't even understand the advice she gives them."*
:   *"The only thing that matters to me is keeping my wife safe. I won't let anyone harm her."*

When spoken to directly:

:   **What was that argument outside the Hall?**
:   *"Ah, you saw that, did you? Life in Morthal has been troubled lately. The people are uncertain, restless. They merely look to the Jarl for leadership."*

:   **What's going wrong in Morthal?**
:   *"There's news of rebellion against the Empire. Strange noises have been heard in the marshes at night. And then, the tragedy with [Hroggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroggar "Skyrim:Hroggar")'s home. The men simply seek wisdom. Everything will be fine."*

:   **Morthal seems like a quiet little town.**
:   *"That's what many here wanted. A quiet life in a quiet place, without the noise or the trouble of a city. Now some worry this wizard, [Falion](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion"), will foul it all up."*

If he gets exiled to the Blue Palace when the Stormcloaks take Hjaalmarch, he'll be disheartened, worriedly saying:

:   *"We're safe here now. But what of Morthal?"*
:   *"The Empire brought stability, assurance to the people of Morthal, even if they didn't appreciate it. Now what do they have?"*
:   *"I fear for what this change will do to my family."*

## Conversations

Morthal's citizens arguing with Aslfur

He can initially be found outside [Highmoon Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Highmoon_Hall "Skyrim:Highmoon Hall") having the following argument:

:   **Jorgen**: *"What's the Jarl going to do about it?"*
:   **Thonnir**: *"How are we supposed to feel safe in our own homes?"*
:   **Aslfur**: *"Please, enough already! I have told Igrod of your concerns. She'll look after you. Please, go back to your business."*
:   **Jorgen**: *"We've no need for wizards in our midst!"*
:   **Thonnir**: *"Morthal has enough problems as it is!"*
:   **Jorgen**: *"Bah, it's no use. Let's get back to it then."*

Inside the Hall, he can often be found talking to his wife:

:   **Idgrod**: *"The people still doubt me, don't they."*
:   **Aslfur**: *"No, not at all. It's just..."*
:   **Idgrod**: *"It does not surprise me. They do not share in what I see, and I cannot explain it to them."*
:   **Aslfur**: *"Just guide them well, and all will work out."*
:   **Idgrod**: *"I have never doubted that, husband."*

:   **Aslfur**: *"Have you made a decision about Falion?"*
:   **Idgrod**: *"What decision is there to be made? I allowed him to live here. I stand by that."*
:   **Aslfur**: *"Yes, but there are concerns. Rumors that he's up to something."*
:   **Idgrod**: *"We are all up to something, my dear. All is as it should be."*

:   **Idgrod**: *"What troubles you, husband?"*
:   **Aslfur**: *"What? Oh, nothing. All is well."*

This last conversation will play out differently when Idgrod and Aslfur are outside of the Hall, as they are when in exile, for example:

:   **Idgrod**: *"What troubles you, husband?"*
:   **Aslfur**: *"It's Joric. I fear his condition is worse. He calls out in his sleep sometimes. I've heard Falion's name. What does it mean?"*
:   **Idgrod**: *"Joric will be what Joric will be. Give it time."*
:   **Aslfur**: *"Still, I fear there is some connection."*

When he winds down in the evening, he can also be found talking to the local innkeeper, [Jonna](/wiki/Skyrim:Jonna "Skyrim:Jonna"):

:   **Aslfur**: *"How's business?"*
:   **Jonna**: *"Very funny."*
:   **Aslfur**: *"No, I... I was just asking."*
:   **Jonna**: *"It's as bad as ever."*

:   **Jonna**: *"When are you gonna do somethin' to help Falion? Stop people sayin' things about him?"*
:   **Aslfur**: *"You have to understand, his presence here has caused... Well, it's difficult for the people to get used to."*
:   **Jonna**: *"They got used to Idgrod just fine, didn't they? So what's the difference?"*
:   **Aslfur**: *"Yes, well. Perhaps you're right."*

## Notes

- In the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*, the summary for him reads:

:   *"Aslfur met Idgrod during the time she spent wandering Tamriel. A young warrior then, Aslfur protected Idgrod during her pilgrimage, and the two were married before returning to her home in Morthal. Over the years, Aslfur has served as Idgrod's advisor, and now, in her old age (and some say her insanity), he is more protective than ever."*

# Skyrim:Aspiring Mage

## Overview

| Aspiring Mage | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000753CB |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| Class Details | [CombatWarrior1H](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleCommonerAccented](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCommonerAccented "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCommonerAccented") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [WIGenericCrimeFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:WIGenericCrimeFaction "Skyrim:WIGenericCrimeFaction") | | |

The Aspiring Mage

The **Aspiring Mage** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") who is [randomly encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#College_Application_Denied "Skyrim:World Interactions") in the wilderness. He can be seen attempting to [reanimate the corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate_Corpse "Skyrim:Reanimate Corpse") of a woodland creature. He had wanted to follow in his grandfather's footsteps and become a mage, but his application to join the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") was denied. It turns out he is only able to cast magic because of his grandfather's [leveled staff of reanimation](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves#Reanimate "Skyrim:Staves"). You may persuade him to give you the staff, intimidate him, or just pay for it.

The Aspiring Mage wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006c1d9 "Skyrim:Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots"). Apart from his staff, he also carries a leveled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems").

## Dialogue

As he tries to reanimate the creature, he will intone:

:   *"Rise up and live again!"*
:   *"I grant you a new life!"*
:   *"Come on, get up!"*
:   *"This should work. I've done it before."*
:   *"Gah! This staff is useless... I'm useless. The whole world is useless!"*

You can approach him to ask what the problem is:

:   **What's the problem?**
:   *"Oh... hello there. Didn't notice you come up. I was focusing my magicka. Or at least, I thought I was. I don't really know what I'm doing."*

You can reply in two ways:

:   **Yes. It's painfully obvious you don't know what you're doing.**

    :   *"You don't have to tell me that."*

:   **That's quite a staff you have there.**

    :   *"I used to think so, too."*

Either way, he will continue by explaining:

:   *"See, my grandfather was a wizard. My father wouldn't talk about him much. But I found some of his things in the attic. Including this staff. After that I thought I was turning into a wizard too, because dead things near me would come to life again for while. I even went to the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). But they just laughed at me. The magic is in the staff, not in me they said."*

At this point, you can try to acquire the staff from him.

| Player Choice | Response |
| --- | --- |
| **Give the staff to me before someone gets hurt.**  *(Persuade)* | **Passed:** *"Okay, okay. You've talked me into it."* **Failed:** *"Nah. I don't think so."* |
| **Hand over the staff, or else.**  *(Intimidate)* | **Passed:** *"No need to get rough!"* **Failed:** *"I don't have to take that from you!"* |
| **Seems like coin would be worth more to you.**   *(<BribeCost> gold)* | **Passed:** *"Gold solves most problems, doesn't it?"* |

A successful attempt will have him say:

:   *"In fact. Keep it. I must have used up the magic in the staff or something. It's just a dumb stick of wood now."*

## Bugs

- He never unloads properly from the game, because the associated world encounter does not complete as it should.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- He may not have his staff equipped and may not actually be wielding it when encountered in the wilderness.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.

## Related Quests

- **[In the Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:In_the_Shadows "Skyrim:In the Shadows")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_of_Shadows "Skyrim:Bow of Shadows"): Save the Jarl of Whiterun from an assassination plot.

## Quest-Related Events

The assassin will not appear if the Jarl is occupied, and will not appear if you haven't started the quest [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)"). The Jarl is considered occupied when the following quest stages are active:

- [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)") - Stage 10: When Jarl Balgruuf is showing you to [Farengar](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire").
- [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") - Stages 10, 12, 13, 15, 20, 110, 120, 130, 150: During the scenes inside Dragonsreach at the beginning of the quest and after the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") summon you to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar").
- [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen") - Stages 25, 27 - When persuading the Jarl about to trap [Odahviing](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing") in Dragonsreach.
- At any point during [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun"), [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude"), or [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm").

# Skyrim:Assassin

## Overview

This article is about the randomly encountered assassin. For the corpse in Hag's End, see [Dark Brotherhood Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Assassin").

A female Khajiit Assassin

**Assassins** of the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") are occasionally sent to track and subsequently make an attempt on your life throughout the game. The assassin's race and gender will vary between an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") female, a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") male, or a [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") female.

The assassins appear as [random encounters](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin_Sent_to_Kill_the_Player "Skyrim:World Interactions") starting at level 5. Unlike [hired thugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Hired_Thug "Skyrim:Hired Thug"), the assassins appear for no reason and there is no way to avoid encountering them. A [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin%27s_Note "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Assassin's Note") detailing their mission can always be found on their bodies, though it is never revealed who performed the [Black Sacrament](/wiki/Lore:Black_Sacrament "Lore:Black Sacrament") to order the assassination.

After completing either the [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") or the [Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!") quest, you are no longer in danger of being attacked by these assassins.

## Notes

- [Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Shrouded Armor") cannot be collected from slain assassins.
